mahāmbhodhimahāśailamekhalaiva mahāmahī ।। merukailāsakūṭebhyaḥ spṛhayanti na nāgarāḥ ।। yatra saṃnipatanto api na bādhante parasparam ।। mahākālaprabhṛtayas tyaktvā śivapuraṃ gaṇāḥ ।।
yasya devīsahasrāṇi ṣoḍaśa śrīpater iva ।। gopālaḥ pālakaś ceti sutau jātau guṇāmbudhī ।। rohantakaḥ surohaś ca tasyāstāṃ tatsamau sutau ।। prayogeṣu ca daṣāṇāṃ yānti sma divasāḥ sukham ।।
pālako api yavīyastvād yauvarājyam apālayat ।। navamantrikṛtārakṣā jāyate sma punar vā ।। adhiṣṭhāya jagatsāraṃ nirjagāma bahiḥ puraḥ ।। bibhyad vyāḍād gajāt tasmād itaś cetaś ca vidrutam ।।
prāṃśuprākārataḥ prāṃśor agamyāṃ parikhām agāt ।। taṭasthā hastipṛṣṭhasthaṃ sābhāṣata ruṣā nṛpam ।। adhītavedaṃ yo hanti brāhmaṇaṃ tasya ke mṛgāḥ ।। cinteṣu bhinnahṛdayaḥ praviveśa niveśanam ।।
janavādopalambhāya pradoṣe niryayau gṛhāt ।। samantrāgadasaṃnāhaḥ saṃcacāra śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।। abhisārikayā sārdhaṃ bhāṣamāṇasya kāminaḥ ।। mayā yena tvayā sārdhaṃ baddhā prītir abuddhinā ।।
mayā tvaṃ tu gṛhād eva na niryāsi pativratā ।। khalīkṛtaiḥ kim asmābhir vṛtheva kulaputrakaiḥ ।। vihasya viṭam āha sma tvādṛśā hi hatatrapāḥ ।। na hi bhartṝn aviśvāsya ramante kulaṭā viṭaiḥ ।।
jahi ghātaya bālaṃ me patiṃ nityapramādinam ।। nanu durvārarāgāndhaḥ sutāṃ yāti prajāpatiḥ ।। yena rājyasukhāndhena prajāpālaḥ pitā hataḥ ।। gacchann anyatra śuśrāva dhvaniṃ viprasya jalpataḥ ।।
tvaritaṃ yājate dehi stanyaṃ kaṇṭho asya mā śuṣat ।। pitṛghātin mriyasveti nirdayaṃ nirabhartsayat ।। bālo ayam uktety enaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ kupito abravīt ।। śrutismṛtivid ity etad uvāca brāhmaṇī patim ।।
anayat kṣaṇadāśeṣam asaṃmīlitalocanaḥ ।। apṛcchat ko ayam asmāsu pravādaḥ kathyatām iti ।। kaulīnahetuśrutaye cittaṃ devāvadhīyatām ।। āsann avyabhicārīṇy ariṣṭāny aṣṭau mumūrṣataḥ ।।
uddhartāraṃ mahīpālaḥ kartayām āsa nāpitam ।। kulakramāgato vṛddhaḥ sūpakāraḥ pramāpitaḥ ।। prabho vidher vidheyatvād brāhmaṇān apy abādhata ।। adṛṣṭabhartṛvyasanaḥ pūrvam evāgamad divam ।।
guruśokasahāyena sahasaivābhyabhūyata ।। prajāsu ca viraktāsu jātau svaḥ kiṃkriyākulau ।। kaulīnam idam āvābhyāṃ saparyanteṣv avantiṣu ।। bandhayām āsa rājānaṃ rājaputraḥ priyaprajaḥ ।।
sukhasya mahato dadhyau sa rājendro gajendravat ।। sa kṣapāḥ kṣapayan kṣīṇaḥ saṃvatsaraśatāyatāḥ ।। na mukta eva muktaś ca yāvat prāṇaiḥ priyair iti ।। itarad vādhunā devaḥ prabhur ity atha bhūpatiḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā ca sāsram ākāśam anātha idam abravīt ।। anapāyam upāyaṃ kaḥ prayuñjītaitam īdṛśam ।। dṛṣṭādṛṣṭabhayagrastacetasāṃ na tu mādṛśām ।। idaṃ tv alīkakaulīnam aśakto aham upekṣitum ।।
kūjan prakāśayām āsa kṣīṇāṃ tāmraśikhaḥ kṣapām ।। yaśodhavalitānantadigantodbudhyatām iti ।। pidhāya pārthivaḥ karṇāv uttamāṅgam akampayat ।। kṣate kṣārāvadekena kiṃ phalaṃ bhavatām iti ।।
nanu praśasyam ātmānaṃ nāham arhāmi ninditum ।। rājaputreṇa laḍitaḥ kenānyena yathā mayā ।। varṇāśramāḥ svadharmebhyaḥ kiṃ vā vicalitā mayā ।। putraḥ punnarakāt trātā kasyānyasya yathā mama ।।
naravāhanadevena jāmātrā cakravartinā ।। prasādān mantrivṛṣayor yat tapovanasevanam ।। sasiṃhāsanam āsthānaṃ maṇḍape dīyatām iti ।। kamaṇḍalusanāthaś ca bhūpālo niryayau gṛhāt ।।
dṛśyamāno avarodhena viveśāsthānamaṇḍapam ।। pālakenābravīt taṃ ca sthita eva sthitaṃ sthitam ।। buddheḥ svasyāś ca śuddhāyāḥ kiṃ nāma na parīkṣitam ।। yena loke tae ucyante viyātāḥ pitṛśikṣakāḥ ।।
varṇāśramaparitrārtham idam adhyāsyatām iti ।। mādṛśāṃ hi na vākyāni vimṛśanti bhavādṛśāḥ ।। uttaraṃ cintayām āsa nāsāgrāhitalocanaḥ ।। bhoḥ siṃhāsanam āroha kiṃ tavottaracintayā ।।
vegaḥ prāvṛṣi śoṇasya caraṇeneva durdharaḥ ।। viṣādagadgadagiraḥ pramṛjyāśru babhāṣire ।। tvanniyogān niyoktāraḥ kasmād vayam udāsmahe ।। mṛgendrāsanam ārohan khaṭvārūḍho bhaven nanu ।।
parivettāram ātmānam ayaṃ manyeta ninditam ।। śokajāny aśruvārīṇi bhavantv ānandajāni naḥ ।। alaṃ vaḥ pīḍayitvā māṃ vacobhir iti pārthivaḥ ।। khaṭvārūḍho na bhavitā ninditaḥ śabdavedibhiḥ ।।
parivettāpi naivāyaṃ bhaviṣyati narādhipaḥ ।। prajābhis tac ca na mṛṣā mayā hi nihataḥ pitā ।। prāyaścittaṃ vrajan kartuṃ na nivāryo asmi kenacit ।। tasya pratyupakārāya pālakaḥ pālyatām ayam ।।
avantivardhanaṃ putraṃ matprītyā pālayer iti ।। avantivardhano rājā rājan kasmān na jāyatām ।। nikṣiptavantaḥ śrūyante putreṣv eva guruṃ dhuram ।। tvaṃ ca vṛddhas tadā yuktaṃ svayam eva kariṣyasi ।।
sarvatīrthāmbukalaśair abhyaṣiñcat sa pālakam ।। nirjagāma purāt svasmād ekarātroṣito yathā ।। atha rājani kānanāvṛte puram āspanditalokalocanām । nibhṛtaśvasitāmayadhvaniṃ mṛtakalpāṃ praviveśa pālakaḥ ।।
utsṛṣṭapṛthivīcintaḥ pālakaḥ kālam akṣipat ।। utsīdantīḥ prajā rājan nārhasi tvam upekṣitum ।। kiṃ śocasi na śoko ayam upāyaḥ kṣitirakṣaṇe ।। nikṣiptakṣitirakṣas tu sarvam eva na muñcati ।।
rājan dhanyāḥ prajāḥ kāryāḥ sukhaṃ cānububhūṣatā ।। dhruvaṃ drakṣyasi saṃkrāntādeśān rājanvataḥ prajāḥ ।। balād agnigṛhān nītaḥ puroḍāśaḥ śunā kila ।। baṭutvāt kṣiptacittasya hṛtaḥ kākena modakaḥ ।।
mṛgendrāsanam adhyāste sumeruṃ maghavān iva ।। udayācalakūṭasthe nalinya iva bhāskare ।। dharmam ācakṣatāṃ pūjyāḥ śuddham ity atha te abruvan ।। ācāro ayam iti vyaktam anuyuktās tvayā vayam ।।
sāṃkhyādīnām akāryatvād vedasyaiva pramāṇatā ।। śrutvedaṃ nṛpatir yajñair īje niḥsaṃkhyadakṣiṇaiḥ ।। mantrinau jātasaṃtrāsau taṃ kadācid avocatām ।। uddhāryaḥ sāṃprataṃ kena dīkṣāpaṅkād duruttarāt ।।
durlabho hi vinā tābhyāṃ dharmaḥ suddho nṛpair iti ।। devatāyācanavyagrastrīkam antaḥpuraṃ yayau ।। antaḥpuracarīḥ praiśyāś cacāra paritoṣitāḥ ।। vāsukinyā mahādevyā nināya saha yāminīm ।।
upāsiṣṭa puraḥsaṃdhyām ādivākaradarśanāt ।। stūyamāno jayāśīrbhir āsthānasthānam āgataḥ ।। mānayitvā yathāyogyaṃ sopacāraṃ vyasarjayat ।। āpānabhūmir udyāne ramaṇīyā prakalpyatām ।।
viṣayān na niṣeveta dṛṣṭādṛṣṭāvirodhinaḥ ।। ātmānaṃ ca bhavannāthaṃ yojayāmi sukhair iti ।। pānopakaraṇaṃ sarvaṃ sajjam evety avocatām ।। vastrābharaṇamālyānnadānaiḥ prītām akārayat ।।
kṛtajotkāram anyo anyaṃ pīyate sma tato madhu ।। gīyate sma manohāri naṭādyair nṛtyate sma ca ।। visṛjya prakṛtī rājā viveśāntaḥpuraṃ tataḥ ।। pāyitāśeṣabhāryaś ca paścān nidrām asevata ।।
vivṛddhasukharāgasya bahavas tasya vāsarāḥ ।। svapno mayādya yo dṛṣṭaḥ praśasyaiḥ śrūyatām asau ।। mattaṃ mahāntam āyāntaṃ mātaṅgaṃ vanacāriṇam ।। krodhād unmūlitālāno yātaḥ prati vanadvipam ।।
āhūtavān iva yuddhaṃ sagarvaiḥ kaṇṭhagarjitaiḥ ।। saṃnipāto mahān datto dantayor vanadantinaḥ ।। dūram utkṣipya nikṣiptas tato yātaḥ parāṅmukhaḥ ।। nivarttayitukāmo aham āsannān idam uktavān ।।
śikṣito vatsarājena hastiśikṣām ahaṃ nanu ।। pratibuddhaḥ sasaṃtrāsaḥ kim etad iti cintayan ।। phalam iṣṭam aniṣṭaṃ vā pūjyair atrocyatām iti ।। rājopacāracaturāḥ sthāpayām āsur anyathā ।।
yaś cābhiṣekahastī taṃ rājyavighnaṃ śarīriṇam ।। tvam apy unmūlitānarthaś ciraṃ pāhi mahīm iti ।। sukhaṃ nālabhatāthainam abrūtāṃ mantriṇāv idam ।। āvābhyāṃ śrutam etac ca gṛhe kathayataḥ pituḥ ।।
yathāpradhānamilitāḥ pṛṣṭāḥ svapnaṃ dvijātayaḥ ।। vicitraiḥ saptabhiḥ pakṣaiḥ ko asau vyākriyatām iti ।। sakampavacano avocan nīcaiś cañcalabhīrukaḥ ।। trasyadbhiḥ paruṣād vāpi mādṛk kasmān na yujyatām ।।
duṣkarapratikāre tu yuktam ittham udāsitum ।। śāṇḍilyam idam aprākṣīd vivakṣuṃ sphuritādharam ।। yasmāt vyāhartum ārabdhaḥ pratiṣiddho na kenacit ।। ahitādi hitāntaṃ ca śrūyatāṃ deva mā kupaḥ ।।
sapta pakṣās tu ye tasya sapta pakṣān nibodha tān ।। kaścid āropyatām etad yasya necchasi jīvitam ।। atīteṣv aśanir hanti patitvā mūrdhani dhruvam ।। akṣiṇī mukharasyāsya khanyetām ity acodayat ।।
mantrī sākṣinikocena grāhyavākyān asūcayat ।। deva nonmattavākyāni gṛhyante paṭubuddhibhiḥ ।। tenāpi nayanoddhāraṃ naiva nigraham arhati ।। pakṣāḥ sapta gatā yāvat tataḥ prāpsyati nigraham ।।
lagne asminn eva sauvarṇaḥ parīkṣārthaṃ dvijanmanaḥ ।। viparyaye khalīkāraṃ manvādiparibhāṣitam ।। kurvadbhiḥ śāntikarmāṇi mahākālaṃ niṣevatām ।। bandhayitvā ca śāṇḍilyaṃ mahākālaṃ yayau nṛpaḥ ।।
madhyaṃdine payodālīm unnamantīṃ raviṃ prati ।। nīlakaṇṭhagalacchāyā pravṛṣṭā vṛṣṭim aśmanām ।। rājapratikṛtiṃ piṣṭvā tatraivāntardadhe tataḥ ।। kṣamayitvā ca vipulaiḥ saṃpradānair atoṣayat ।।
so ayaṃ mukharaśāṇḍilyaḥ siddhādeśo anuyujyatām ।। śṛṇu rājan na kopaṃ ca pitṛvat kartum arhasi ।। bhavadīyo bhavān eva sarvathā śrūyatām idam ।। svataḥ pracyāvitas tasmād yuktam āsthīyatām iti ।।
śanair mukharaśāṇḍilyapramukhā niryayur dvijāḥ ।। kaḥ syād rājeti cintāvān niṣasāda nṛpāsane ।। viṣādād dīnayā vācā mahīpālam abhāṣata ।। vañcaya tvam api kṣipram atyāsannaphalo hy asau ।।
devo api divasān kāṃcid vanavāsī bhavatv iti ।। gopālatanayas tatra viveśāvantivardhanaḥ ।। nipatyotpatya ca punaḥ siṃhāsanatalaṃ gataḥ ।। siṃhāsanatalād eva kandukaḥ kṛṣyatām iti ।।
kiṃ cāhaṃ bhavataḥ praiṣyā yenādiśasi mām iti ।। avantivardhano anyatra sthāpayām āsa nirvyathaḥ ।। siṃhāsanād avaplutya pariṣvaktas trapānataḥ ।। uvāca rājaputro ayam adya rajye abhiṣicyatām ।।
avantivardhanaṃ putraṃ matprītyā pālayer iti ।। pitryam āsanam adhyāstāṃ nyāsaṃ pratyarpitaṃ mayā ।। sabhāyām ānatāṅgāyāṃ na kaścid kiṃcid uktavān ।। putram āropayām āsa siṃhāsanam avantiyam ।।
adhyāsita munivaraiḥ saha kāśyapena mandaspṛho asitagiriṃ tapase jagāma ।। janyate sma na saṃtāpaḥ pārthive avantivardhane ।। kadācid vāhayitvāśvān nivṛtto dṛṣṭavān kvacit ।। kālindīhradasaṃkrāntāṃ lolām indukalām iva ।।
nirmucyamānanirmokaṃ bhogaṃ bhogavadhūm iva ।। āvṛto hayaśālābhiḥ svaṃ viveśa niveśanam ।। dolāyamānahṛdayo dolām eva vyacintayat ।। mandadharmārthacintasya divasāḥ katicid gatāḥ ।।
kṣubhitānām ivāśrauṣīt sa nirghoṣam udanvatām ।। prāsādatalam arohad antaḥpuracarāvṛtaḥ ।। saṃpramardantam adrākṣīn mātaṅgaṃ saṃghamardanam ।। bhṛṅgamālāparīvāraḥ sa yayau prati pakṣaṇam ।।
mātaṅgarājam adrākṣīn mātaṅgagrāmaṇīs tataḥ ।। hastikīṭo ayam uddāmo durdānto damyatām iti ।। ārāt siṣeca kariṇaṃ kare kuñcitapuṣkare ।। vavande caraṇau tasyāḥ saṃspṛśya śirasā mahīm ।।
citrīyamāṇahṛdayaś cintayām āsa cetasā ।। vaśīkṛtaḥ śarīriṇyā vaśīkaraṇavidyayā ।। vaśīkuryād viśantī ca calayed acalān api ।। baddhāṃ dolām adhiṣṭhāya nāgaṃ yāhīty acodayat ।।
abhistambham agād vītabhayapaurajanāvṛtaḥ ।। aśokapallavaiś chāyām atha tasyāś cakāra saḥ ।। vanditvā ca mahīpālaṃ mātaṅgī pakṣaṇaṃ yayau ।। keyaṃ kasya kuto veti pṛcchati sma surohakam ।।
sahasaivedam āyātaṃ parun mātaṅgapakṣaṇam ।। grāmaṇīs tasya kanyeyaṃ sutā surasamañjarī ।। svadehaṃ yāpayām āsa pittajvaracikitsitaiḥ ।। ākhyad aṅgāravatyai sa tannaptur vṛttam īdṛśam ।।
smitāpagamitatrāsaṃ surohakam abhāṣata ।। tatheyam api kenāpi nimittenāgatā mahīm ।। vyāpāro ayam adivyasya prekṣitaḥ kena kasyacit ।। kanyāṃ varayituṃ yāmi nātmatulyāsti dūtikā ।।
gatvā pakkaṇamadhyasthaṃ dadarśotpalahastakam ।। saha mātaṅgasaṃghena vavande dūram utsṛtaḥ ।। ahaṃ tvāṃ draṣṭum āyātā tvam apy eṣa palāyase ।। dūrotsaraṇam utsṛjya tena ḍhaukasva mām iti ।।
mannaptre dīyatāṃ rājñe rājñī surasamañjarī ।। na ca grāmeyakālāpais tvaṃ māṃ bādhitum arhasi ।। mamāpi bhadra dauhitraś cakravartī bhavādṛśām ।। anuktottara evāsyai tatheti pratipannavān ।।
mṛtasaṃjīvinī naptūr asāv oṣadhim ānayat ।। sa buddhyāpi na yāti sma pratyakṣam api tāṃ smaran ।। gandharvanagarākāraṃ sa saṃsāram amanyata ।। sa prāsādagato apaśyat pakṣaṇaṃ nirjanaṃgamam ।।
krandantī parimṛjyāśrum anuyukteti bhūbhṛtā ।। utānyad asti duḥkhasya kāraṇaṃ kathyatām iti ।। kiṃ tu kāraṇam asty anyad bhīṣaṇaṃ tan niśāmyatām ।। saptavarṇapure pūrvaṃ vāyumukte pure avasat ।।
ipphako nāma tasyaiva pitrāhaṃ ca pratiśrutā ।। rajaḥpiśaṅgabhṛṅgālīm aharat kusumasrajam ।। sthāṇusthiraṃ bhujaṃgīva vilolā paryaveṣṭayat ।। nāradaś caṇḍakopatvād uccair idam abhāṣata ।।
kṣiptā mayi manuṣyeṣu caṇḍālaḥ sa bhavatv iti ।। tīvrasya brahmaśāpasya pratīkāro bhavatv iti ।। nāradāgnir uvācedaṃ mlānam utpalahastakam ।। utsṛṣṭaḥ kṛtapuṅkhena dhānuṣkeṇeva sāyakaḥ ।।
svalpenāpi hi vañcyante tena tvam api vañcaya ।। tadā tvaṃ dāruṇād asmād asmacchāpād vimokṣyase ।। uṣitā varjitā duḥkair ahorātrasamāṃ samām ।। tenāpi śāntaśāpena svargād asmān nirākṛtā ।।
matkṛte tvām api krūra ipphakaḥ pīḍayed iti ।। caṇḍālabhayaśaṅkinyā ruditaṃ niḥsahāyayā ।। mahārājasya sādhyatvāt pratikūlo hi pārthivaḥ ।। tato vijñāpayiṣyāmi kartavye tu bhavān prabhuḥ ।।
muktvānyastrīkathāṃ bhīru sarvaṃ saṃpādayāmi te ।। atiprasāda ity uktvā abravīt surasamañjarī ।। hiṃsitavyaḥ sadoṣo api na antaḥpuragato nṛpaḥ ।। anugrahe api yācñeti yad idaṃ tad idaṃ nanu ।।
amāvāsyāṃ śaśīvāsīj janadurlabhadarśanaḥ ।। śrutvā harmyāvalīśeṣāṃ rājāpy āsīt samutsukaḥ ।। tadālpadarśī samayaṃ visasmāra sa taṃ tataḥ ।। taṭaṃ śivataḍāgasya citravṛttāntam ānayat ।।
plavena vyacarat sārdhaṃ bhāryayā vītanidrayā ।। so apaśyad dayitāṃ bhītāṃ mā bhaiṣīr iti cābravīt ।। tasyaivorasi tiṣṭhantī bibhemīti na yujyate ।। ihāsitam ahaṃ manye tasmād āvartyatām iti ।।
sabhāryaṃ baddham ātmānam aikṣatāvantivardhanaḥ ।। ipphakaḥ sphuritakrodhaḥ samutkṣipya jahāra tam ।। hlādayām āsatur vākyaiḥ sacivau sajalānilaiḥ ।। pālakaḥ śrāvyatāṃ sūnor vṛttāntam iti tau gatau ।।
vanditāyācacakṣāte pālakāya hṛtaṃ sutam ।। svantaḥ khalv eṣa vṛttānta iti vākyāmṛtena tam ।। āyāntīm eva jānīhi putravārttāṃ śivām iti ।। cakāsadasicarmāṇaṃ divi divyaṃ tapasvinaḥ ।।
saha cāvantināthena kāśyapādīn avandata ।। vidyādharaḥ kathitavān vṛttāntaṃ munisaṃnidhau ।। māṃ divākaradevākhyaṃ jānīta paricārakam ।। upariṣṭād avantīnāṃ caṇḍālaṃ dṛṣṭavān imam ।।
ipphakaṃ nāma mātaṅgaṃ vidyādharakulādhamam ।। tadā yuddhena nirjitya prāptitaś cakravartinam ।। kim ity avocad etena yan me dārā hṛtā iti ।। sabhāsadbhiḥ sabhāṃ sadbhiḥ kāśyapādyair adhiṣṭhitām ।।
vardhamānakamālāṃ vā nirjito ayaṃ sarāsabhām ।। āgantā svaḥ pratijñātaṃ teṣām āgamanaṃ mayā ।। āliṅgya ca sasauhārdaṃ mayā saha visṛṣṭavān ।। cakravartī ca vo draṣṭum āgantā sāvarodhanaḥ ।।
harṣāśrusiktatanavaḥ kṛcchrād akṣapayan kṣapām ।। ākarṇya munayo apṛcchan kim etad iti khecaram ।। vimānagarbhavartitvāt śrūyate garjitākṛtiḥ ।। garjaddundubhijīmūto nabhasā dṛśyatām iti ।।
ambhodānām iva vyāptasakalāśānabhastalam ।। ārād āyādvimānānāṃ divo vṛndam adṛśyata ।। sthitam anyāni śailasya kandarāsānumūrdhasu ।। padmarāgapalāśānāṃ ṣaḍviṃśatyā pariṣkṛtam ।।
sthitās tasya palāśeṣu bhāryāś citravibhūṣaṇāḥ ।। sabhāṃ kamalinīm āgāt phullānanasaroruhām ।। harṣātiśayaniśceṣṭaṃ vavande mātulaṃ munim ।। devībhir vanditās tasya śvaśuras tadanantaram ।।
prasṛṣṭānandanetrāmbur abravīd gadgadākṣaram ।। āyuṣmatā tu tat prāptam āśiṣāṃ yad agocaram ।। ācāram anugacchadbhir asmābhir idam ucyate ।। mahākalpāvasāne api kūṭasthaṃ tiṣṭhatām iti ।।
gomukhaḥ kathayām āsa preritaś cakravartinā ।। abravīd ipphakaḥ pūjyāmātaṅga anuyujyatām ।। sārdhaṃ surasamañjaryā rājānaṃ hṛtavān iti ।। dattvā duhitaraṃ paścād etasmai dattavān iti ।।
dattvā na dattavān yo asmai nanv asau pṛcchyatām iti ।। yathāhāyaṃ tathaivedaṃ viśeṣaṃ tu nibodhata ।। pratyakṣam eva pūjyānāṃ divyalocanacakṣuṣām ।। sutā dattā mayā tubhyam upayacchasva tām iti ।।
kanyakām upayaccheta śāpadagdhāt kulād iti ।। avantipataye dattā tadā surasamañjarī ।। pṛcchyantām iti pṛṣṭaiś ca tat tatheti niveditam ।। caṇḍasiṃhādibhir yasmāt pramāṇaiḥ pratipāditaḥ ।।
vārāṇasyāṃ mṛtāṅgāni gaṅgāmbhasi nimajjaya ।। bhaikṣāśanaś ca varṣānte muktaśāpo bhaviṣyasi ।। didṛkṣubhir vatsanarendranandanaṃ tapovanaṃ sapramadais tadāvṛtam ।। ṛṣimātulamitrāṇāṃ pṛṣṭo bhāryāgaṇasya ca ।।
tvatkathāśravaṇotkaṇṭhaniṣkampamanasaḥ sthitāḥ ।। svīkṛtāś ca yathā vadhvas tathā naḥ kathyatām iti ।। trāsāt pṛthutarākṣasya jātam acchāyam ānanam ।। atyāsanno aticapalaḥ ko na dahyeta vahninā ।।
idaṃ sacetanaḥ ko nu kathayed gurusaṃnidhau ।। iti śūrakathāṃ śūraḥ kuryāt kaḥ śūrasaṃnidhau ।। sulabhānto varaṃ śāpo dustaraṃ na tu pātakam ।। smarer iti na ca nyāyyaṃ tām api smartum īdṛśi ।।
abhāṣata mahāgaurī prabhopahatabhāskarā ।। śrotuṃ yad ucitaṃ yasya sa tac chroṣyati netaraḥ ।। caritaṃ kathayām āsa sā citraṃ cakravartinaḥ ।। ākhyāyamānaṃ caritaṃ śṛṇvantv acalacetasaḥ ।।
saṃniviṣṭānukālindi tasyām udayano nṛpaḥ ।। kathayeyaṃ yadi guṇān na kathā kathitā bhavet ।। ratnāni gaṇayen meroḥ kadā draṣṭā sa medinīm ।। kathyamānāṃ kathām eva śṛṇuta prakṛtāṃ mayā ।।
tasya vāsavadattāyāṃ padmāvatyāṃ ca bhūpateḥ ।। sakāyā iva copāyāś catvāro mitramantriṇaḥ ।। vasantakaś ceti sa taiḥ saha kālam ayāpayat ।। jānuspṛṣṭamahī pṛṣṭau saṃvijñāpayatām idam ।।
saha tena sa potena nāgalokaṃ praveśitaḥ ।। gatas tatraiva ca gataḥ so api tātagatāṃ gatim ।। sthitā na mṛgyamāṇāpi bahukṛtvaḥ prayacchati ।। bhrātṛjāyā tataḥ sā nau vyutthitā dāpyatām iti ।।
duṣkaraṃ kulanārībhīrājāsthānapraveśanam ।। sā yadāha sabhāyās tat samakṣaṃ kathyatām iti ।। vijñāpayati sā yat tad ākarṇayitum arhatha ।। svāgtaṃ rājajihvāyāity avocat kṛtasmitā ।।
sā mām āhāgame kāryam āryayā jñāpyatām iti ।। ārye sarvam idaṃ satyaṃ devarau me yad āhatuḥ ।। vahanasya punaḥ svāmī vipanna iti na śrutam ।। avipannā gṛhān eva śrūyante punar āgatāḥ ।।
vimuktaḥ punar āyāyān mamāvaidhavyalakṣaṇaiḥ ।। vartate bhrātṛputro api kadācid anayor bhavet ।। tataḥ svīkṛtasarvasvau devarau me kva yāsyataḥ ।। na nikṣiptavatī śeṣam āryayā jñāpyatām iti ।।
kuṭumbācāracaturā yuktam āha kuṭumbinī ।। ubhayor nobhayorvāpi yuktaṃ bhokṣyāmahe tadā ।। tūryagarjitasaṃbhinnas tāraḥ kalakalo abhavat ।। vaṇiggaṇikayā rājā vyajñāpyata viyātayā ।।
vaṇijo bhrātṛjāyāyājātaḥ putro anayor iti ।। aho putrasya māhātmyaṃ pratyakṣam anubhūyate ।। harṣavibhrāntacittānāṃ vaṇijāṃ paśya ḍambaram ।। samaṃ harṣaviṣādābhyāṃ mitrāmitrasamā gatāḥ ।।
avasāne vinā putrāt pālakaḥ ko bhaviṣyati ।। dīrghaśvāsasahāyasya divasāḥ katicid yayuḥ ।। yātrā mṛgājinodyāne tvaddṛṣṭyā maṇḍatām iti ।। viśālāś citraśālāḥ sa citranyastanarādhipāḥ ।।
ye caitān anutiṣṭhanti te ke ke puruṣā iti ।। ṣaṣtyā putrasahasrāṇāṃ śūrāṇāṃ parivāritaḥ ।। ayaṃ pāṇḍur amī cāsya tanayāḥ pañca pāṇḍavāḥ ।। vicintaś cintayām āsa citrāṃ yātrām acintayan ।।
mandapuṇyena yātavyaṃ manye puṃnarakaṃ mayā ।। nivṛtyāpaśyad āvantyāṃ mandirodyānasevinīm ।। tāmrāśokalatāprāntam avalambya vyavasthitām ।। udvegam iva śaṃsantīṃ mlānānanasaroruhām ।।
vandyeta labdhavijayo rakto bālo niṣevyate ।। mahārāja kutaḥ śoko nāmāpi tava gṛhyatām ।। āvapantīṃ svaśāvānām īkṣe putravatīm iti ।। anantayā saṃtatayā tatheyam api khidyate ।।
adṛṣṭvā tatra tāṃ tasyāḥ pṛṣṭavān paricārikām ।। mādhavyā sahakārasya vivāham anutiṣṭhati ।। bhāryāṇāṃ divasā yānti saha putramanorathaiḥ ।। phalakeṣu kṛtākrandair avakāśo na labhyate ।।
na labhyate sutaḥ paśya vaiparītyaṃ vidher iti ।। anāgatāgatasuhṛtparivāra upāviśat ।। mūlaṃ kulataroḥ kasya kiyantaḥ putrakā iti ।। vasantakaḥ parihasan praṇayitvād abhāsata ।।
yāvantaḥ svāminaḥ putrās tāvanto asmākam apy ataḥ ।। aprastāve api bhavato mukham etad anāvṛtam ।। nanv anekaguṇāṃ bhartur utpādayasi vedanām ।। svāmicittānukulaiva vṛttir āsthīyatām iti ।।
tataḥ piṅgalikaiveyaṃ devam ārādhayed iti ।। yāsau piṅgalikā sā naḥ putriṇī kathyatām iti ।। putravān bhava deveti brāhmaṇī tam avardhayat ।। āgamyate kutaḥ ke vā tavāmī bālakā iti ।।
bālakāś ca sutā ete mameti kathitaṃ tayā ।। na hi bhartrā na ca sutair bhavitavyaṃ tavedṛśaiḥ ।। ciraproṣitakāntāyāgṛhabhittir iva striyaḥ ।। tasmād idaṃ mahac citraṃ sphuṭaṃ naḥ kathyatām iti ।।
mahatī tu kathā śrotum icchā cec chrūyatām iyam ।। agnikuṇḍacitasīmā sphītagodhūmagokulaḥ ।। yasyāntevāsibhir vyāptā vasudhā vedavedibhiḥ ।। vasiṣṭhapatnīm api yā sādhuvṛttām alajjayat ।।
utpannolkeva saṃdhyāyāṃ sutā locanadurbhagā ।। patiputradhanair hīnām ādideśa bhaviṣyatīm ।। dhūmaketuśikhevoccaiḥ paruṣā sā vyavardhata ।। aprakṣālitahastaiva tatsamakṣam abhakṣayat ।।
na kaścid varayām āsa varaḥ prāptavarām api ।। mā sma yujyata duḥkhena prāpyaināṃ ninditām iti ।। sarvaṃkaṣaprabhāvena prabalenāṅgajanmanā ।। mastakastho bhayakaraḥ somadattam abhāṣata ।।
iṣṭakāloṣṭakair hanti tenāsau vāryatām iti ।। ulke piśācike gaccha śīghraṃ mama gṛhad iti ।। smarapīḍāsahatvāc ca maraṇāya mano dadhe ।। adrākṣit kvacid uddeśe prāsādaṃ daityaghātinaḥ ।।
guñjanmadhukaraśreṇīm anumātavyarodhasam ।। upāyeṣu tu saṃdehas tatropāyo ayam uttamaḥ ।। paṅkajāvayavāhārāt kṣīṇā tyakṣyāmi jīvitam ।। narakaṃ tu na yāsyāmi strīmṛtyumṛtasaṃkulam ।।
rātrau ca baddhaparyaṅkā devaṃ mādhavam asmarat ।। varaṃ varaya putrīti bhāṣamāṇaṃ mudāyutam ।। maraṇaṃ me jagannātha prasādaḥ kriyatām iti ।। prāṇihatyāvipāko ayam ātmahatyā ca ninditā ।।
yena hīnāsi vairāgyān niryātā svagṛhād iti ।। ahaṃ tv ācaritāpuṇyā duḥkhair eva vibhāvitā ।। mṛtyunā śāntim icchāmi sā me saṃpādyatām iti ।। yavāḍhakaḥ pitur gṛhe brāhmaṇāyopapāditaḥ ।।
surūpaḥ sādhuvṛttaś ca sa te bhartā bhaviṣyati ।। krīto yavāḍhakena tvam iti yāvan na vakṣyasi ।। aṣṭau nipatitā vahnāv añjaler viralāṅguleḥ ।। maraṇād dāruṇāt tena cittam āvartyatām iti ।।
saśiṣyavargaṃ pitaraṃ tadgaveṣiṇam āgatam ।। śrāmyantīm anayad gehaṃ viśrāmyantīṃ tarau tarau ।। varaṃ labdhavatī tasmāt tāṃ mām eva nibodha tām ।। gṛham asmākam āyātaḥ kṛtātithyo dadarśa mām ।।
kāntininditacandrābhā yuktaṃ cet kathyatām iti ।। pitrā dattaṃ ca vidhivan muditaḥ pariṇītavān ।। na kāṃcin na karoti sma mamājñāṃ ninditām api ।। labdhā mayā sutā ye asya prasādāl lokadhāriṇaḥ ।।
pṛṣṭhaṃ duḥkhāyamānaṃ me caṇḍi saṃvāhyatām iti ।। kim ahaṃ bhavatā krītā pṛṣṭhasaṃvāhiketi tam ।। ahaṃ vā kiṃ tvayā krīto yena preṣyatvam āgataḥ ।। krīto yavāḍhakenāsi mayety apriyam abruvam ।।
saṃnikarṣād apakramya saṃbhrānta idam abravīt ।। kaccit piṅgalikā nāsi kaś ca nāma yavāḍhakaḥ ।। so api saṃjātanirvedo na jāte kva palāyitaḥ ।। pitṛbhartṛvihīnāham enaṃ deśam upāgatā ।।
saputrānugṛhītā asmi bhaktāc chādanarakṣaṇaiḥ ।। evam ete mayā labdhās tuṣṭān nārāyaṇād iti ।। sacivaiḥ sahitaś cakāra rājā sutasaṃprāptiphalaṃ kriyāvicāram ।। yad bravīmi nibodhantu bhavantas tat sacetasaḥ ।।
brahmacaryeṣṭisaṃtānair ṛṣidevasvadhābhujām ।। aputratvāt tu pitṛbhir gṛhītaḥ piṇḍabhojibhiḥ ।। sukhibhiḥ sa hi nirdiṣṭaś candanād api śītalaḥ ।। dṛṣṭādṛṣṭasukhaprāpteḥ putrād anyan na kāraṇam ।।
ārabhadhvaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ devatārādhanaṃ tataḥ ।। siddhakalpātmasaṃkalpāḥ pratyūcur darśitasmitāḥ ।। piṅgalīdarśanaṃ ceti prayogo ayam anuṣṭhitaḥ ।। kṛtaḥ kāle prayogo hi nāphalo jātu jāyate ।।
sacivair abhyanujñātas tatheti pratipannavān ।। yayau nāgavanodyānaṃ sadāraḥ saha mantribhiḥ ।। alam āli tavānena khedeneti nivāritā ।। anubhūtasukhā cāsi bhrātur bhartuś ca veśmani ।।
anubhūtāni tenāhaṃ śaktā duḥkham upāsitum ।। kṛttikāgarbhasaṃbhūto bhavānyā iva ṣaṇmukhaḥ ।। tapobhir acirād rājā rājarājam atoṣayat ।। hā devi hāryaputreti vyāharantau parasparam ।।
puraḥ purohitādīnām ācakhyau svapnam ādṛtaḥ ।। prabhāmbhaḥsaṃtativyastanabhomaṇḍalanīlatām ।। tvām āhvayati vitteśas tadāśāṃ gamyatām ataḥ ।। āropya prasthitā vyomni diśaṃ vitteśapālitām ।।
ityādīn darśayantī nau pradeśaṃ pārvatīpituḥ ।। candrapāṣāṇanirmāṇaprākārām alakāpurīm ।। yasyā bāhyam adṛṣṭāntaṃ kalpapādapakānanam ।। śubhrayaty eva harmyāṇi yasyāṃ rudrenducandrikā ।।
vadati kṣaṇam atraiva sthīyatām iti devatā ।। anujñātapraveśo asi devenāgamyatām iti ।। kakṣāntare prakṛṣṭarddhau paśyāmi draviṇeśvaram ।। sakhi nūnam asāv eṣa yasyāsau bhavitā sutaḥ ।।
bharatānām ayaṃ vaṃśe viśuddhe jāyatām iti ।। so api sādhūpamānasya putraḥ pātraṃ bhaviṣyati ।। asāv api śacīśakracaritau pitarāv api ।। sakiṃkaragaṇaṃ prahvaḥ praṇamāmi dhanādhipam ।।
udyamyāha manuṣyendra svāgataṃ sthīyatām iti ।। vyavadhāya tu mām āste devī nīcaistarāsanā ।। anekākārakaraṇaḥ śrūyate puṣkaradhvaniḥ ।। gāyantyaḥ kuṭṭitatalānartayante tilottamām ।।
rājarājasutaḥ krīḍann āyātaḥ saha bālakaiḥ ।। krīḍāśakaṭikāṃ karṣann itaś cetaś ca gacchati ।। utplutya patitaṃ ratnaṃ vaiḍūryakṣodakuṭṭime ।। mahyam etad dadasveti tad ratnam udayācata ।।
ratnaṃ paṅkajagarbhasthabandhūkam iva rājate ।। ṣaḍviṃśatyā padmarāgam aṣṭāśri bahalaprabham ।। stanayor antare nyastam anayāpi sphuranmudā ।। vidārya dakṣiṇaṃ kukṣim etasyāḥ praviśaty asau ।।
pratibuddha iti svapnam ācaṣṭe sma narādhipaḥ ।। ādityaśarmā svapnasya dvijaḥ phalam avarṇayat ।। samādhineva balinā rāgādīnāṃ balīyasām ।। vidyādharasamūhendraḥ putras tava bhaviṣyati ।।
mahākulā bhaviṣyanti bhāryās tava sutasya tāḥ ।। vidyās tā viddhi putrasya bhaviṣyantī bhaviṣyataḥ ।। svasvapnaḥ kathitas tatra devyā vāsavadattayā ।। kukṣau vidāryamāṇe ca hāryaputreti bhāṣitam ।।
bhaviṣyadviṣaye jñāne dṛḍhatāṃ niścayo gataḥ ।। dṛṣṭaḥ svapno mayā yaḥ sa śravaṇenānugṛhyatām ।। devasyāpatyalābhāya sarve saniyamāḥ sthitāḥ ।। mārgitaś ca mayā dehi svāmine naḥ prajā iti ।।
tavāpi pūrayāmīti mahyaṃ bāṇaṃ vitīrṇavān ।। akālakaumudīṃ cemāṃ paśyāmi pratibodhitaḥ ।। yādṛśo asya suto bhavī tādṛśaḥ śrūyatām iti ।। putraḥ ṣāḍguṇyatattvajño yuktaś cāyaṃ guṇair guṇaiḥ ।।
tena rājasutapraiṣyaḥ khecaraś ca bhaviṣyati ।। mamādyaikonapañcāśan maruto darśanaṃ gatāḥ ।। svaṃ vimucya mudā mahyaṃ saṃnāhaṃ dattavān iti ।। bhavato bhavitety evaṃ svapnam āsthāpayad dvijaḥ ।।
bravīti tatra mām ekā praviśemāṃ guhām iti ।। catasraś ca mahāvidyāvinyastāś citrakarmaṇi ।। bodhito jṛmbhaṇair mandrair bherīṇāṃ garjitair iti ।। aśeṣacitravinyastakalākuśaladhīr iti ।।
dattavān pāvako mahyaṃ kuṇḍalaṃ rucirojjvalam ।। ।। bhinnaṃ bhābhis tamo jātaṃ cakoranayanāruṇam ।। resur vivādarasitāḥ sarasīṣu śakuntayaḥ ।।
devatāgārabherīṇām uccair dhvanir ajṛmbhata ।। pūritārthisamūhāśa tavāśā pūryatām iti ।। ityādibhir dvijāś cainaṃ mantravādyair avardhayan ।। ādityaśarmaṇo jātam aṅgaṃ romāñcakarkaśam ।।
vasantake dhvanattāle nanarta gaṇikāgaṇaḥ ।। vadhūvṛndaparīvārāḥ pranṛttāḥ śvaśurā api ।। tāḍayanti sma gandharvāḥ svarāvismṛtasāraṇāḥ ।। kṛtābhiṣekādividhiḥ suraviprān apūjayat ।।
pauram antaḥpuraṃ caiva dānādibhir amānayat ।। devyāṃ sattvasamāveśavārttāṃ prāvartayat kṣitau ।। giriṣṭhaḥ pañjarastho vā mugdhas tatraiva tatra saḥ ।। garbhakarmavidaś cānye nityaṃ tāṃ paryacārayan ।।
śvaśrūs tasyā mukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā bubudhe dohadavyathām ।। anākhyāte hi garbhasya vaiphalyam api dṛśyate ।। tadā svavṛttaṃ sā vadhvai vyāhartum upacakrame ।। bādhate dohado yas tvāṃ sa kṣipraṃ kathyatām iti ।।
sakhīmukhena kathitaṃ bahukṛtvo anuyuktayā ।। sā ca saṃpāditāmātyaiḥ śatānīkasya śāsanāt ।। vyacaranta purīṃ raktām ambarābharaṇasrajaḥ ।। raktāśokavanākāraparivārakadambakāḥ ।।
digdāhād iva raktānām apaśyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ diśām ।। jyeṣṭhaputra ivāgacchad garuḍasya vihaṃgamaḥ ।। agamad gaganaṃ vegāc chatānīkasya paśyataḥ ।। bhakṣayiṣyan niṣiddhaś ca kenāpy ākāśam āśrayat ।।
prabhāmaṇḍalasaṃsargapiṅgalāṅgau jvalajjaṭau ।। vasiṣṭhasyāśritaḥ puṇyām udayādrer upatyakām ।। paśyāmi sma jagajjyeṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhatāpasaveṣṭitam ।। putri putraṃ vijāyasva yaśaḥpātram ajarjaram ।।
ādityavaṃśajānāṃ hi saṃniveśaḥ parāyaṇaḥ ।। āvāsaḥ kriyatāṃ vadhvā iti śiṣyān samādiśat ।। khātaśālaparikṣiptaṃ vasiṣṭhāya nyavedayan ।। ṛṣibhiḥ kriyamāṇeṣu garbhasaṃskārakarmasu ।।
anukūlasavitṛādigrahasūcitasaṃpadam ।। divase dvādaśe nāma putrasya kṛtavān mama ।। tasmād udayano nāma prasiddhim upayātv iti ।। sāstreṣu cāstraśastreṣu buddhir asya vinīyata ।।
mā kadācid bhavān asmād dūraṃ gā āśramād iti ।। niryāya mṛgayām eṣa samakrīḍata kānane ।। abhivāditavān bhīto vasiṣṭhaṃ darśitasmitam ।। nalinyāṃ prastutakrīḍābhavatā bhoginām iti ।।
ācakṣva vistareṇeti vasiṣṭhas tam abhāṣata ।। na gantavyaṃ tvayā dūram etasmād āśramād iti ।। māṃ nivārayatīty āsam ahaṃ kautūhalākulaḥ ।। dūram adyāśramād asmād gacchāmi diśam uttarām ।।
vanavāraṇasaṃkṣobhasaṃghaṭṭitanadāmbhasam ।। unmajjanto nimajjantas tarantaś cāruṇekṣaṇāḥ ।। dīrghadīrghabhujākṣepair agādhaṃ jalam āśritāḥ ।। nanv ahaṃ bhavato draṣṭum āśramād ṛṣir āgataḥ ।।
kiṃ te asmābhir mahāsattva bhāṣitair gamyatām iti ।। tena mā bhaiṣṭa ḍhaukadhvam iti tān aham uktavān ।। āgaccha prārthito mitra gṛhaṃ no gamyatām iti ।। mām ādāya nimagnās te tasyaiva saraso ambhasi ।।
candrasūryamaṇidyotapradhvastadhvāntasaṃcayam ।। ramyaharmyāvalīgarbhajṛmbhitātodyanisvanam ।। praveśito asmi muditair adhiṣṭhānaṃ kumārakaiḥ ।। purī bhogavatī nāma vasatiḥ kalpajīvinām ।।
anye ca sūnavo anyeṣāṃ nāgasenābhṛtām iti ।। grāhitārghādisatkāraḥ kārito veṣam īdṛśam ।। anujānīta mām adya suhṛdo mā sma kupyata ।। bhītaś ca kupitāt tasmāt tasmān nayata mām iti ।।
punar āgacchatā kāryam anutkaṇṭhabhujaṃgamam ।। suhṛdo api yadīcchā syād gacchet tāṃ nalinīm iti ।। uttīrṇam aham ātmānaṃ paśyāmi sarasas tataḥ ।। mamāsminn aparādhe ca pramāṇaṃ bhagavān iti ।।
yena nāgakumārās te dṛṣṭigocaratāṃ gatāḥ ।। gāndharvaṃ hastividyā ca śikṣitavyāḥ savistarāḥ ।। sanāgamūrchanā grāhyā vīṇā ghoṣavatī tvayā ।। madhuraṃ nisvaneyus tāṃ vidyāṃ ghoṣavatīm iti ।।
gate bahutithe kāle vīṇāpāṇir upāgataḥ ।। tadviyogāgnitaptāṅgīm ambām aṅgair aśītayat ।। tāta ghoṣavatīghoṣasaṃgītaṃ śrāvyatām iti ।। jagatpracalanācāryo nabhasvān api nācalat ।।
raktāṃ ghoṣavatīṃ muktvā tuṣṇīm āsīt patis tava ।। vādanīyā punar vīṇā geyaṃ vā śanakair api ।। samādheḥ kiṃ punar yena sākṣiṇo api vimohitāḥ ।। dūre tapovanād asmād vīṇeyaṃ vādyatām iti ।।
nāgān udayano agṛhṇād ramyair ghoṣavatīrutaiḥ ।। kvaṇadghoṣavatīpāṇir āyāti sma tapovanam ।। dārakas taruṇo jātaḥ kauśāmbīṃ gamyatām iti ।। guruṇā tīrthasalilair abhiṣiktaḥ suto mama ।।
ākāśena nayanti sma kṣaṇena nagarīm imām ।। muhūrtaṃ preritavatī gaganāgamanaśramam ।। padmabhañjikayā krīḍan dṛṣṭa udyānapālakaiḥ ।। adhunaivāgataḥ svargād gāhate nalinīm iti ।।
deva evāyam ity uktvā praṇāmaṃ kartum udyataḥ ।। rājann udayanaputraṃ na namaskartum arhasi ।। premasaṃbhramasaṃtrāsalajjābhiḥ kheditām iti ।। muhūrtaṃ cintayitvā tu vihasan prasthito gṛhān ।।
na gantavyaṃ na gantavyaṃ naiṣa svapno nivartyatām ।। durlabhenāpi hi svapne vallabhena samāgamaḥ ।। tato yasyāsi sāpatyām ādāya dayitām iti ।। ācakṣate sma vṛttāntam āśramānayanād iti ।।
nipatan dharaṇīpṛṣṭe putreṇa lambhitaḥ kṣaṇam ।। niśvāsair akṣipad dīrghair netrāmbukaṇikāgaṇam ।। avatāreṇa gurubhiḥ prasādaḥ kriyatām iti ।। gacchāmo nāvatīryaiva svasti tubhyaṃ bhavatv iti ।।
asmatpāvanam ujjhitvā yatheṣṭaṃ gamyatām iti ।। tatraivāntardadhuś caṇḍamarudvyastā ivāmbudāḥ ।। pūjayitvā tad udyānaṃ namnāvocan mṛgājinam ।। pravartitā nṛpatinā prasiddhim agamad bhuvi ।।
praviṣṭo hṛṣṭahṛdayaḥ prahṛṣṭāṃ nagarīm iti ।। tavāpi dohado yaḥ sa putri saṃpādyatām iti ।। māgadhīm uktavān pṛccha dohadaṃ bhaginīm iti ।। duḥsaṃpādā kila śraddhā mamety āha śanair iyam ।।
mugdhe kiṃ nāma duḥsādhyam upāyacaturair nṛbhiḥ ।। ugraseno mahāsenaḥ śatrusenāmbudānilaḥ ।। āsīn manoramācārā yā nāmnāpi manoramā ।। rasanmayūrasāraṅgameghamaṇḍūkamaṇḍale ।।
kadambānilam āghrātum udbhūtaprathamārtavā ।। udyānaśobhayākṛṣṭadṛṣṭis tāṃ tatra dṛṣṭavān ।। samagacchata sadyaś ca sasattvā samapadyata ।। viṣṇoḥ śoṇitamāṃsāntrair gamayāmi tṛṣām iti ।।
sṛṣṭaḥ piṣṭamayo viṣṇur meṣāmiṣabhṛtodaraḥ ।। nyastaḥ piṣṭamayo viṣṇuḥ kṣapāyāṃ kṣapitas tayā ।। vadhyaṃ yādavasiṃhasya kaṃsaṃ sutam asuta sā ।। tasmāt tavāpi yā śraddhā sāpi saṃpādyatām iti ।।
ambarasthavimānasthā kṛtsnāṃ draṣṭuṃ mahīm iti ।। devasya dāsabhāryāṇām ayam eva manorathaḥ ।। dolām āruhya nabhasā muhur āyāta yāta ca ।। tenākāśagatiśraddhā tathā ca pūryatām iti ।।
nivartyatāṃ parīhāsaḥ prastutaṃ vartyatām iti ।। asādhāraṇa evāyaṃ viṣayaḥ śilpinām iti ।। yantram ākāśasaṃcāri tvaritaiḥ kriyatām iti ।। rumaṇvantam abhāṣanta saṃtrāsapraskhaladgiraḥ ।।
jalāśmapāṃśuyantrāṇi kāṇḍarāśikṛtāni ca ।। asmākaṃ tu na yātāni gocaraṃ cakṣuṣām iti ।। bhoḥ sabhe śrūyatāṃ tāvad yan mayākhyānakaṃ śrutam ।। skandhāvāreṇa sārdhaṃ sa surāṣṭraviṣayaṃ gataḥ ।।
viśvilo nāma yaḥ śilpī sadṛśo viśvakarmaṇā ।। tava putrāya duhitā dattā ratnāvalī mayā ।। kularūpābhijātyādiguṇaratnāvalī hi sā ।। tasmāt saṃvardhasiddhyarthaṃ putraṃ prasthāpayer iti ।।
jāmātrāgamanākāṅkṣī mahāntaṃ kālam akṣipat ।। bhaṇati sma na taṃ kaścit snāhi bhuṅkṣveti cākulaḥ ।। āgantukena kenāpi sarvam ākulitaṃ gṛham ।। mandako aham amībhir me maṇḍaḥ saṃpādyatām iti ।।
tenāyam ākulo lokas tat kim etad bhaved iti ।। gṛhasthe vardhase diṣṭyā prāptas te duhitur varaḥ ।। śiraḥ prāvṛtya bhāryāsmai karmaśālām adarśayat ।। abhivāditavān prahvaḥ prasāritabhujaṃ gurum ।।
nirantaraṃ pariṣvaktaś cirādṛṣṭaḥ suhṛd yathā ।। kiṃmayās taṇḍulās tāta kathyatām iti so abravīt ।। ghaṭitā ghaṭikāmātrāt karaghāṭataror iti ।। tavāpi śilpisiṃhasya tṛtīyasya na vidyate ।।
gṛhyatām iti tenokte viśvilenoktam om iti ।। saṃmīyate sma nāṅgeṣu daridra iva kāmukaḥ ।। mahān kālo atiyāti sma nimeṣojjhitacakṣuṣoḥ ।। kim etad iti saṃdihya kim etad iti pṛṣṭavān ।।
bhartṛdāraka yady asti śrotum icchā tataḥ śṛṇu ।। adhunā saha jāmātrā puṣṇīmo bhaginīm iti ।। yantrāṇi ghaṭayām āsa yāvanāny atha viśvilaḥ ।। āyurārogyakārīṇi pākopakaraṇāni ca ।।
śvaśurāya dadāti sma sa ca prītas tad ādade ।। viśvilādīn samāhūya saviṣādam abhāṣata ।। kāśideśapatis tena praṇayād aham arthitaḥ ।। dharmādhikārakārāya sa me prasthāpyatām iti ।।
vārāṇasyām avighnena bhavān āvartatām iti ।। martavyaṃ cāsya caṇḍasya rājño vākyam akurvatā ।। tasmāt pukvasakaḥ sarvaiḥ sudṛṣṭaḥ kriyatām iti ।। bhṛtyaṃ vārāṇasīṃ yāntam anujānīta mām iti ।।
dūtaiḥ sa pratidūtaiś ca saha vārāṇasīṃ gataḥ ।। saṃtatāśrujalāsāradhautaṃ mlānakapolakam ।। dantāvaraṇasaṃskāraśūnyam agalitālakam ।। na dadhāti sma śokāndhā bāhū ca skhaladaṅgadau ।।
gṛhiṇīṃ cakitaḥ paśya niścintāṃ tanayām iti ।। na darśayāmi nanv evaṃ straiṇaṃ kim api cāpalam ।। vṛtā na labhate śāntim apaśyantī tam utsukā ।। seyam evam aśoketi mandabhāgyā bhaṇāmi kim ।।
dinastokeṣu yāteṣu garbhaṃ ratnāvalī dadhau ।। bho paśya dayitāpatye duhituḥ prakriyām iti ।। jātena ca nṛpāc caṇḍāt prākampata bhayena sā ।। sutādoṣavipākaṃ ca paśyan rājakulaṃ gataḥ ।।
jāmātraivāhito garbhas tac cedam avadhīyatām ।। nivṛttamatrais tair eva mahyam āveditaṃ yathā ।। yantrakukkuṭam āsthāya pradeśe kvāpi yātavān ।। avijñātaḥ kilāsmābhir adhyaśeta svasaṃstare ।।
pādeṣu patitas teṣām ayācata viṣaṇṇakaḥ ।। ākāśayantravijñānaṃ survijñānam ayāvanaiḥ ।। lokena paribhūyeta kṣaṇarāgā hi mānuṣāḥ ।। dṛṣṭa eva mahān doṣo jīvanasyāpahāraṇam ।।
kurvan narapater ājñāṃ neṣyāmi divasān iti ।। draṣṭum icchā samutpannā yena duścakṣuṣām api ।। na gṛhṇāti sma vakti sma gurur me labhatām iti ।। sarvasvaharaṇāt trastaṃ toṣayām āsa pukvasam ।।
ākāśayantram āsthāya praviṣṭaś ca gṛhān niśi ।। adya mām āha nṛpatiḥ śanair utsārya sasmitam ।। yan mahyam api tat sarvam arthine kathyatām iti ।। tasmai tu kathitaṃ prītaiḥ śilpibhir yāvanair iti ।।
śilpinaḥ saha śāṭhyena jāyanta iti ghuṣyate ।। anyathā jīvaloko ayaṃ sudṛṣṭaḥ kriyatām iti ।। rājñe tad yantravijñānam arthine kathyatām iti ।। rātrau ratnāvalīṃ suptāṃ pratibodhyedam abravīt ।।
upāyais tava pitrāham asmāt sthānād vivāsitaḥ ।। pracchādyaṃ ca tad asmābhir nidhānaṃ kṛpaṇair iva ।। vijñānasyāsya rakṣāyai tyajeyaṃ bhavatīṃ api ।। kiṃ cāhaṃ durbhagā yena bhaktāṃ tyajasi mām iti ।।
rātrāv ākāśam utpatya svasthānaṃ viśvilo yayau ।। te śilpaṃ darśayantīti kasyeyam asatī matiḥ ।। asādhyāḥ sāmadānābhyāṃ nīcā hi vadhasādhanāḥ ।। atāḍayad avocac ca yantram āyojyatām iti ।।
ahaṃ karomi vo yantraṃ mā sma tāḍyanta śilpinaḥ ।। tac ca saṃpāditaṃ sarvam acireṇa rumaṇvatā ।। ārohakaparīmāṇaṃ senānīr anuyujyatām ।। vipannayantraiḥ śrūyante mathitāḥ kupitair iti ।।
kiṃ vā vacobhir bahubhiḥ kṣaṇam āsthīyatām iti ।। vimānam ambaropetaṃ mandārakusumārcitam ।। ākramya garuḍaṃ krāma krāntapūrvāṃ mahīm imām ।। vimānam idam āruhya yatheṣṭaṃ gamyatām iti ।।
nodyānam api gacchāmi kuto anālambanāṃ divam ।। nanu voḍhum idaṃ śaktaṃ sakalāṃ nagarīm iti ।। sapauraśreṇivargaś ca yānam adhyāsta bhūpatiḥ ।। puṇyam ākāśam āviśya prāk prācīm agamad diśam ।।
devo vidyādharo vāpi bhoḥ ko ayam iti cābravīt ।। anujñātaś ca saṃyāto nṛpaḥ pavanavartmanā ।। avantinagarīṃ prāyāt pravṛttodakadānakām ।। stambhayām āsa tad yantram athātuṣyan narādhipaḥ ।।
kim etad iti saṃdehadolādolam abhūn manaḥ ।। iṣṭasaṃprāptilambhaś ced nāsmābhiḥ śrutam īdṛśam ।। pātayām āsa vatseśaḥ śanakair lekhitākṣaram ।। rājann udayanaś cauraḥ sadāras tvāṃ namasyati ।।
caurāya dattam abhayaṃ tasmād avataratv iti ।। draṣṭavyeṣu tanūbhūtam udbhūteṣu kutūhalam ।। lokālokitayānaś ca kauśāmbyām avarūḍhavān ।। ājñāpitaṃ nṛpatinā śilpī saṃmānyatām iti ।।
tiṣṭhantīm ambare apaśyad devatām avanīśvaraḥ ।। pūjitaiva tvayā yat tvāṃ pūjyaṃ pūjitavaty aham ।। guhyakādhipater āptā bhadreti paricārikā ।। kandarāyāṃ nagendrasya mahendrasya nabhaḥprabham ।।
vījyamānaṃ sarasijaiḥ kāntārakariyūthapam ।। kartāro hastiśikṣāyāṃ satyam āhur idaṃ yathā ।। kanyāḥ sujātā diṅnāgair nānāsattvās tato gatāḥ ।। madāmodavibhinnāmbhas tad evāvataraṃ saraḥ ।।
prītena yūthapatinā ciram ākrīḍitaṃ mayā ।। sa gajaḥ kṣālitakaṭaḥ kaṭakaṃ prāviśad gireḥ ।। sadyaḥ kṛtanijākārā rājarājasabhām agām ।। smarantī tāḍayāmi sma cāmareṇa dhanādhipam ।।
trāsotkampitadikcakraḥ kṛtavāñ chāpabhājanam ।। tvam avantipates tasmād abhavye hastinī bhava ।। prabhunā devadevena muktaḥ śāpo mahān iti ।। śaptayā pīḍitas tasmād bhava hastī mahān iti ।।
karaṇotkhātakopasya navanītanibhaṃ manaḥ ।। śāpād asmād vimokṣyethe vibhītaṃ mā sma putrakau ।। pūrṇabhadro api tasyaiva nāgo vyālo nalāgiriḥ ।। āvayoś caritaṃ yat tat sarvaṃ pratyakṣam eva te ।।
aham aprapya kauśāmbīṃ vipannā gahane vane ।। yathā mayi vipannāyāṃ priyadāraḥ striyām iva ।। tvām eva śocitavatī seva śaptaṃ śatakratum ।। kaṃ nāma ca kariṣye aham upakāraṃ manāg iti ।।
bhrāmitaś ca vimānena sugarbhasthasuto mahīm ।। vidyādharendram uddhartā sukham āstāṃ bhavān iti ।। yat tad bhadravatīdvāraṃ kauśāmbyāṃ prathitaṃ bhuvi ।। siddhādeśavacaḥ satyaṃ kṛtaṃ vyomacarair iti ।।
śuddhānte ca śukādipañjaravayaḥkolāhale api śrute rājā dārakajanmasaṃpadaghanaprahlādam utpraikṣata ।। divākare mṛdukare devī putraṃ vyajāyata ।। śaṅkājanma ca śatrūṇāṃ samaṃ samabhavat trayam ।। cakravartipitā lokāv ubhau vijayatām iti ।।
alpakālāntare jātāḥ kanīyāṃso nṛpātmajāt ।। āgataṃ cedivatsānām iti nāsīd viniścayaḥ ।। anvarthanāmnas tanayān akurvan rājamantriṇaḥ ।। naravāhanadatto astu dattas tena yatas tataḥ ।।
bhūmihemagajāśvādidānaprītadvijanmanā ।। tasmai vitīrṇavān svapne devadevaḥ śaraṃ hariḥ ।। saṃnāhachadmanā tasmai yatas taṃ maruto daduḥ ।। svayaṃ gobhiḥ prasannābhiś citraṃ tasmai pradarśitam ।।
yasmāt taṃ tapanas tasmai kuṇḍalachadmanā dadau ।। aham eva sa te caite sarve hariśikhādayaḥ ।। avardhāmahi laghv eva sanāthāḥ pādapā iva ।। sabrahmacaryakaiś chāttrair dhātrībhiś cāśrayāmahi ।।
savratais tu catasro api vidyāḥ sarvaṃ ca vāṅmayam ।। bālabhāvād anadhyāye krīḍati sma sakandukaḥ ।। ahaṃ javena mahatā prayātaḥ pitur antikam ।। baddhamuṣṭikaraḥ krodhād āgato marubhūtikaḥ ।।
kanduko me hṛto anena tam ayaṃ dāpyatām iti ।। tarjanītarjitaḥ pitrā kumāravaṭakāṃ gataḥ ।। mā sma tāta punar bhrātṝn kopayeḥ kopanān iti ।। yathainān kopayāmi sma tathaite mām akopayan ।।
icchati sma ca visraṣṭuṃ mayā ca calitaṃ dhanuḥ ।। mālatīmukulaṃ lakṣaṃ tan mātreṇaiva nāspṛśat ।। āsthānasthamahīpālasamīpam agamat tataḥ ।। kupito bhartsayitvedam abhāṣata mahīpatim ।।
rājaputro mahārāja yauvarājye abhiṣicyatām ।। tāvat tāvad bhavanty eṣāṃ kuṇṭhāḥ kāryeṣu buddhayaḥ ।। vijānanto api śāstrāṇi sutarām andhabuddhayaḥ ।। prabhum eva jighāṃsanti mṛgendraṃ markaṭā iva ।।
vijñāpanā madīyeyaṃ saphalīkriyatām iti ।। bhoḥ sādhu sādhunarakuñjarasādhumantrin ity ujjhitāsanam abhāṣata nirvyavastham ।। yathāpradhānam ābhāṣya vinītavad abhāṣata ।। apṛṣṭā eva bhāṣadhve prītinirvāsitatrapāḥ ।।
tatrāyaṃ svasutaḥ prītyā bālaḥ saṃskriyatām iti ।। kaliṅgasenayā rājā dūrād eva namaskṛtaḥ ।। upagamyopaparyaṅkam adhyāstādiṣṭam āsanam ।। saradvimalahaṃseva cakāśat kāśacāmarā ।।
paścimācalakūṭasthatimirā dyaur ivoṣasi ।। calaccaṭulatākārā bhṛtāpi nibhṛtākṛtiḥ ।। mitavāg api vācālāvyākhyātavyā hi tanmatiḥ ।। tayā me dṛṣṭir ākṛṣṭā guṇair naur iva mantharā ।।
nilīnakokilakulā tanvī cūtalateva sā ।। cakṣuṣā vīkṣyamāṇā māṃ sahasrākṣam ivākarot ।। drāḍimīmukulākāravibhaktadaśanacchadā ।। raktendīvaramāleva mṛṇāladalabandhanā ।।
latāyāḥ sahakārasya phalāni mukulair iva ।। duhitṛtvam anuprāptā nāmāsyāḥ kathyatām iti ।। yām eva pṛcchati svāmī bhṛtyāṃ madanamañjukām ।। ūrūm āropayad bālāṃ sā cemāṃ vāmalocanām ।।
aho citram iti smeram abhūc ca nṛpater mukham ।। dhvanināpi na taccakṣur ākṣiptaṃ nihitaṃ mayi ।। sāmbāyai dāpayitvāsyai tadāsthānaṃ vyasarjayat ।। dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca viśvasya bālā svaṃ bhavanaṃ yayau ।।
svayaṃ bhadrāsanasthaṃ māṃ yauvarājye abhiṣiktavān ।। yatra prasthāpyate bhartā gantavyaṃ tava nirvyatham ।। ity ājñāpitavān rājā prahvaṃ hariśikhaṃ tataḥ ।। ity ājñayā pramuditaṃ kṛtavān marubhūtikam ।।
ramaṇīyaiḥ kriyālāpair apavādojjhitair iti ।। na tyājyo bhavatā svāmī kadācid iti pārthivaḥ ।। maṅgalālaṃkṛtāṅgaś ca suraviprān avandiṣi ।। ambādvayapradhānaṃ ca sphītaṃ rājāvarodhanam ।।
puṣpapallavalājādyām ākrāmaṃ paritaḥ purīm ।। svādhikāraparaiḥ krīḍan saṃvatsaram ayāpayam ।। āvṛttyā sarvavidyānāṃ sthiratām udapādayam ।। prātar bhojanavelāyāṃ na paśyāmi sma gomukham ।।
tenānena vināsmabhir abhuktair gamitaṃ dinam ।। unmattakaḥ sa saṃvṛtta ity avocad gatāgataḥ ।। gatvā tapantakas tasya vikārān prekṣatām iti ।। āryaputra na tan mithyā yad āha marubhūtikaḥ ।।
kampayitvā śiraḥ krodhān nirdārayati locane ।। saṃcārayati karṇāntaṃ kadācin nāsikāntaram ।। vivṛtya dūram adharau dantāntenāpi niśyati ।। tenāryaputra tvaritaṃ kriyāsya kriyatām iti ।।
prāgalbhyān mṛduvailakṣyo mām avandata gomukhaḥ ।। kim arthaṃ cāham svastho na hy ahaṃ marubhūtikaḥ ।। unmattakaṃ sa unmattaḥ prakṛtibhraṣṭamānasaḥ ।। ahaṃ śikṣitum ārabdhaḥ sa cāpi vyāpṛtaḥ sadā ।।
tena māṃ mā pratīkṣadhvaṃ bhojanāyodyatā iti ।। kadācid divase anyasmin dvayos triṣu gateṣu ca ।। aho śobhantae ity uccaiḥ prāśaṃsat khaṇḍamodakān ।। balād ākṛṣya gatavān svayam ucchiṣṭamodakān ।।
acikitsyaś ca saṃvṛtta ity avocat tapantakaḥ ।। labdhalabdhaṃ gacchati sma gṛhītvā kvāpi gomukhaḥ ।। niveditābhyāgamano rumaṇvān mām avandata ।। tena coddhatahastena tāta mā meti vāritaḥ ।।
vandyas tvam adhunā prāpto loke asmiṃl lokapālatām ।। yat tvām āha mahārājaḥ sabhṛtyaṃ tan nibodhyatām ।। yā nāgavanayātreti na kvacin na vikathyate ।। mā bhūd vidyāvighāto vas tadvyākṣiptadhiyām iti ।।
cittavidyā ca vidyeta durghaṭas trikasaṃgamaḥ ।। granthabhīroś ca sidhyanti na śāstrāṇi tapāṃsi ca ।। bhavanto niḥsukhāḥ santaḥ saṃtapantīva me manaḥ ।। tato yāta nirāśaṅkānāsti ced āsyatām iti ।।
tad vo vijñāpayiṣyāmi tāvat pṛcchāmi tān iti ।। haihayānāṃ kulaṃ tuṅgaṃ ciraṃ vijayatāṃ jagat ।। yan naḥ saṃbhāvitāḥ putrāḥ praśnaprativacaḥkṣamāḥ ।। yasya yad vaḥ sthitaṃ buddhau tena tat kathyatām iti ।।
yataḥ śūnyāni durgāṇi gṛhyante anantarair nṛpaiḥ ।। vijñāya nagarīṃ śūnyāṃ yat tad āruṇinā kṛtam ।। khyāpitaṃ dhīracittatvam ātmanaś ca bhaved iti ।। yuktaṃ hariśikhenoktam ity etac ca tapantakaḥ ।।
kim atra bhaṇyate ko anyo mantrī hariśikhād varaḥ ।। rakṣataś cāniyuktasya doṣam andha na paśyasi ।। bhavadādisahāyaś ca kathaṃ yāyād acittatām ।। tadāśayaparīkṣārtham api cet tan na duṣyati ।।
praśnānugraham arhanti nedṛśakūṭamantriṇaḥ ।। cetasyaiḥ saha saṃparkaḥ prayogakuśalair mama ।। yac coktaṃ dharmaśāstreṇa tat tāvad avadhīyatām ।। veṣavāgbuddhisārūpyam ācaran vicared iha ।।
krīḍiṣyāmaś ca kāntāsu sthalīṣu mṛgayām iti ।। yuktasac cānukūlaṃ ca vacaḥ kasmai na rocate ।। prāsādatalam āruhya samṛddhir dṛśyatām iti ।। prāsādam āroham udāraśobhaṃ śaśīva pūrvācalarājakūṭam ।।
citrālaṃkārasaṃskārāṃ vācaṃ kavimukhād iva ।। kuṭumbiparivāro api yatrāgacchad amaṇḍanaḥ ।। niṣkrāmantaṃ rumaṇvantam āryaveṣasahāyakam ।। kañcukyādiparīvāram antaḥpuram ataḥ param ।।
gaṇikāgaṇam ākṛṣṭapramattajanamānasam ।। ayaṃ vaḥ samayo gantum ity athāham avātaram ।। nadannandimṛdaṅgāditūryaḥ pracalam adhvagam ।। śikhaṇḍighanasaṃghātanirghoṣae iva jṛmbhitam ।।
rājamārgam atikramya rājadvāram ayāsiṣam ।। gaccha gaccheti bhūpalaḥ kṣiptapāṇir acodayat ।। prātiṣṭhe bandisaṃghātaprayuktajayaghoṣaṇaḥ ।। rājamārgam adhiṣṭhāya mandiraṃ gantum ārabhe ।।
hemabhāṇḍaiḥ pravahaṇaṃ yuktam ukṣakumārakaiḥ ।। gṛhītamandasaṃcāraṃ paśyāmi sma samīpagam ।। apaśyaṃ megharuddhārdham iva prāleyadīpitam ।। nibaddham añjaliṃ cārusarojamukulākṛtim ।।
na jānāmi sma kenāpi taṃ baddhaṃ vandanāñjalim ।। lalāṭam āvṛtaṃ tena tat samādhīyatām iti ।। yāne kanyābhir unmuktas tasmin kalakalaḥ paṭuḥ ।। gomukhena smitaṃ sadya upakṣiptaṃ kathāntaram ।।
samāsīdāma kālindīṃ tarajjananirantarām ।। uttāryamāṇaṃ yamunāṃ sādareṇa rumaṇvatā ।। nāvaḥ saṃcaratā nāvaṃ tenaivottāritā vayam ।। sthitvā krīḍāgṛhe rātrim utthitāḥ prasthitās tataḥ ।।
prāptā nāgavanodyānaṃ śobhāninditanandanam ।। yātrāṃ paśyan prayāmi sma janatāṅgulidarśitaḥ ।। kḹptanānāvidhākrīḍaṃ yātrāgṛham avaśayat ।। kriyāḥ kurvan nayāmi sma netronmeṣasamaṃ divam ।।
śvaḥ saṃpādayitā krīḍā yā vaḥ sā kathyatām iti ।। abhinīya niśāṃ prātaḥ pratiṣṭhāmahe kānanam ।। kareṇukarabhāśvādivāhanāḥ saṃghaśo avrajan ।। pluṣṭasthāṇuvanākārapulindabalam agrataḥ ।।
senāpatiḥ siṃhaśatruḥ senāpatim avandata ।। tau vā śāmbarasāraṅgau putrau kuśalināv iti ।। yad arthaṃ vayam āhūtās tat samājñāpyatām iti ।। nyāsas tena sasainyena prayatnāt pālyatām iti ।।
tailakumbhasahasraṃ ca rumaṇvān siṃhaśatrave ।। nivṛtte gomukhenoktam aho tātena śobhitam ।। kumāravaṭakeveyaṃ bhaved dāruṇayantraṇā ।। nighnanto ghātayantaś ca na tṛptim alabhāmahi ।।
yamāya prahiṇoti sma mahiṣaṃ marubhūtikaḥ ।। carantaḥ saṃcarantaś ca tatra vātamajā mṛgāḥ ।। bhagnotsāhā nyavartanta vīrebhya iva bhīravaḥ ।। mṛgā yadi ca jānāsi tato naḥ kathyatām iti ।।
prastāve kvacid ācaṣṭa yāṃ vārttāṃ kathayāmi tām ।। evaṃrūpajavākārādṛśyante mṛgajātayaḥ ।। samāsādayituṃ śakyāḥ kuta evānyasāyakaiḥ ।। tūṇam āyāti tasyaiva vitta taṃ cakravartinam ।।
te ca māṃ dūram ākṛṣya divaṃ haṃsā ivāsthitāḥ ।। ramaṇīyasarastīratarucchāyām upāśrayam ।। senānubaddhavartmānaḥ prāptā hariśikhādayaḥ ।। kiyanto vātahariṇāyuṣmābhir nihatā iti ।।
pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sa tān eṣa tūṇaṃ mamāgataḥ ।। yaś cakravarticihnānāṃ sphuṭānām agraṇīr iti ।। siddhasārthavadhajātasaṃmado dattakāṅkṣitavarām ivāmbikām ।। sarojapattraṃ karajaiś chettum ārabdha gomukhaḥ ।।
sajīvam iva saṃpannaṃ calatvāt paṭuraṃhasaḥ ।। pattracchedyam apaśyāmo muktāvayavasaṃkaram ।। gomukho vyākaroti sma pattracchedasya lakṣaṇam ।। tryasraṃ ca caturasraṃ ca dīrghaṃ vṛttaṃ ca bhedataḥ ।।
caturasraiḥ saśālāni purāṇi puruṣādi ca ।। vṛtte bhūṣaṇasaṃyogaśakuntamithunādayaḥ ।। aho nu mahad āścaryam āryaputrety abhāṣata ।। kūpakacchapakalpānām āścaryaṃ sthūlacakṣuṣām ।।
idam āścaryam ity uccaiḥ pulinaṃ no vyadarśayat ।। āścaryaṃ pulinaṃ paśya namas tasmai sacakṣuṣe ।। āścaryaṃ yadi tan mūḍha dveṣaḥ kaḥ salile tava ।। puline yat tad āścaryam atha vā dṛśyatām iti ।।
nety ukte tena dṛṣṭvā tu pulinaṃ gomukho abravīt ।। mayā hi puline dṛṣṭaṃ saṃniviṣṭaṃ padadvayam ।। atyāścaryam idaṃ paśya padakoṭīś caturdaśa ।। idaṃ vicchinnasaṃtānaṃ tenāścaryaṃ padadvayam ।।
bhaveyur iti tenoktaṃ tataḥ syād eva vālukā ।। tayā gatvāvatīrṇaḥ syāt kaścin nāgarako yadi ।। nivarteteti tenokte parṇākīrṇā mahī bhavet ।। divyānāṃ katamasyeti sa vidyādharam ādiśat ।।
dūraṃ padāni majjanti pulineṣu viśeṣataḥ ।। avyaktāṅgulipārṣṇyādinikṣepaṃ jāyate padam ।। avagāḍhaṃ bhavaty agre viparītaṃ tu yoṣitaḥ ।। śilāpādapaśatrūṇāṃ ko asya bhāro bhaved iti ।।
śatrau na śatruṃ puline ramaṇīye avatārayet ।। na vidyāsiddhim āptvāpi jāyante paṅguvṛttayaḥ ।। nimagnaṃ yena tasyedaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ kāminaḥ padam ।। mālatīkusumair vāsam avakīrṇaṃ na paśyasi ।।
tenānyatrāpi dṛśyantāṃ padāni nipuṇair iti ।। strīpuṃsayor adṛśyanta padāni salilāntike ।। tena nāgarakenāpi bhāvyam ity etad uktavān ।। jñeyaṃ kim atra durjñānam atha vā kathayāmi vaḥ ।।
yeyaṃ nāgarakair uktā sā nāgarakatā matā ।। ayaṃ nāgarako yasmād atikramya na gacchati ।। tathā hi caraṇākrāntinatam adyāpi śādvalam ।। saptaparṇam apaśyāma pravṛttabhramarotsavam ।।
svayam ācaritānīva gomukhas tāny avarṇayat ।। ayaṃ sakusumaś cātra kḹptaḥ pallavasaṃstaraḥ ।। āsanaṃ jaghanākrāntijātajarjarapallavam ।। iyaṃ vijṛmbhamāṇāyāmagnāgracaraṇā mahī ।।
niryāntīm anvagacchāma tayoś caraṇapaddhatim ।। mādhavīgahanaṃ veśma kāminām anivāritam ।। puṣpavatyā pariṣvaktaṃ śyāmayā tan nirantaram ।। pracchannaṃ ramaṇīyaṃ ca na hīdaṃ tyāgam arhati ।।
tasmān muhūrtam anyatra kvacid viśramyatām iti ।। chāyayā ca palāśānām atiṣṭhāma tale tataḥ ।। nāsty asāv atra kāmīti saśiraḥkampam uktavān ।। idānīm api nāstīti sarvathonmattako bhavān ।।
śikhaṇḍimithunaṃ kasmān mūkam andha na paśyasi ।। muktārtakekam uḍḍīya vṛkṣadurgaṃ viśed iti ।। calayantaś tu hastāṃs te śūnyam ākhyaṃl latāgṛham ।। prakīrṇapallavanyāsaṃ kiśoraluṭhitair iva ।।
anyatrānyatra ca kṣaumam ambhoruhadalāruṇam ।। varmaratnaṃ sphuradratnaprabhākuñcitalocanam ।। tasmai niryātayiṣyāmi dṛṣṭāyety atha gomukhaḥ ।। tābhyāṃ hi paratantrābhyāṃ bhūṣaṇādīdam ujjhitam ।।
lagnāḥ pādapaśākhāyām adyāpi hi sugandhayaḥ ।। nātidūram atikramya kvacit tuṅgatarau vane ।। vidyādharam apaśyāma lepavidyādharācalam ।। apasṛtya tataś chāyām āśrayāmi sma śākhinaḥ ।।
śakyāḥ kraṣṭum upayena sarvair api surair iti ।। etā oṣadhayaḥ pañca sadāsthāḥ kila varmaṇi ।। vraṇasaṃrohiṇī kācit kācid varṇaprasādanī ।। yadi varmaṇi tāḥ santi tābhiḥ saṃjīvyatām iti ।।
prasādād aryaputrasya jīvitaḥ sa nabhaścaraḥ ।। śalyaprote ca hariṇe prayuktāḥ kramaśas tataḥ ।। akṛtāṅgaḥ kṛtaḥ sadyaḥ samāśvasyeti bhāṣate ।। asmākam aryaputreṇa prakārais caturair iti ।।
āmeti ca mayā prokte tenoktaṃ na sa mānuṣaḥ ।। prasīdantu tam ākhyāta prasādaṃ cakṣuṣām iti ।। jīvayitvābhyanujñeyo mā sma paśyat sa mām iti ।। punaḥsaṃdarśanāyātas tāta prasthīyatām iti ।।
viniśvasya ca tenoktaṃ dainyagadgadayā girā ।। svāminaṃ yan na paśyāmi bhaviṣyacakravartinam ।। evaṃ muñcāmi bhūyas tān na cet paśyatu mām iti ।। gāṃ spṛśañ jānuśirasā sa mām idam abhāṣata ।।
sarvavidyādhareśena praṇaman dṛśyatām iti ।। suhṛddṛṣṭyā ca dṛṣṭaḥ san prahṛṣṭaḥ samupāviśat ।। satyaṃ tat priyasaṃbhāṣo mahānāgarako hy ayam ।। nedaṃ nāgarakatvaṃ me śrūyatāṃ ca kathā yathā ।।
śikhare kauśiko nāma munis tulyāśmakāñcanaḥ ।। ārādhitavatī yatnāt sudīrghaṃ kālam apsarāḥ ।। yadi me bhagavān prītaḥ tato apatyaṃ dadātv iti ।। ahaṃ ca putraḥ putrī ca matsvasā matsanāmikā ।।
dhārayāmi ca tadvidyās tena vidyādharo abhavam ।। mādṛśaṃ putram utpādya kiṃ roditi bhavān iti ।। aṅgād aṅgān madīyāt tu vṛthā jāto bhavān iti ।। tenoktaṃ cakracartī yaḥ sa cāpy anviṣyatām iti ।।
dṛṣṭvā tāni dhiyā mahyam ācaṣṭāṃ bhagavān iti ।। jīvayiṣyati jānīyāt svāminaṃ taṃ bhavān iti ।। saudaryo gamayāmi sma tābhyāṃ kālaṃ sukhaṃ saha ।। kāśyapasthalakaṃ nāma puraṃ mānasalobhanam ।।
dṛṣṭā kanyāparivārā kanyakā kusumālikā ।। praśastir iva vinyastā bhittau vindhyaśilābhṛtaḥ ।। rataye saṃcarāmi sma saridgiritarusthalīḥ ।। rāgād apatrapātrāsaṃ vakragrīvānirīkṣitam ।।
anāmantryaiva māṃ nīco nīcair utthāya yātavān ।। na jānāmi kva yāmīti cakitaḥ saha kāntayā ।। avatīrṇo asmi puline komalāmalavāluke ।। latāgṛham ahaṃ prāptaḥ phullaśyāmālatāvṛtam ।।
tasmād āptopadeśo ayaṃ na nāgarakatā mama ।। mocayen mādṛśaṃ tasmāt tathedam ṛṣibhāṣitam ।। yena tenātmarakṣārthaṃ madvidyā gṛhyatām iti ।। na gṛhītābruvaṃ cainam anugaccha priyām iti ।।
apramatto bhaviṣyāmi bhavato deharakṣaṇe ।। vegenākāśam utpatya prāgād aṅgārakaṃ prati ।। prahlādināmitagateḥ kathitena jātam utkhātasaṃśayakalaṅkatayā viśuddham ।। aśitvodāram āhāraṃ yātrāyai gantum ārabhe ।।
haṃsair iva śaśāṅkābhair vimānaṃ yādasāṃ patiḥ ।। mṛṣṭahāṭakadaṇḍaṃ ca cāmaraṃ marubhūtikaḥ ।। ātatajyadhanuṣpāṇiḥ pārśvaṃ hariśikho abhavat ।। mandam mandaṃ ca naḥ sainyaṃ syandanaṃ parito agamat ।।
dṛṣṭvā hariśikhaṃ vākyam avocan marubhūtikaḥ ।। pradāya prāṇinaḥ prāṇān dharmaḥ prāpto mahān iti ।। śramavyāyāmasāreṇa bhāṣitaṃ yat tvayedṛśam ।। tan mūlatvād itarayos tasmān mitram upārjitam ।।
dharmādīnāṃ pradhānaṃ yat tad ācaṣṭāṃ bhavān iti ।। prādhānyaṃ tena kāmasya kāmaś cecchāsukhātmakaḥ ।। yenedam iha vinyastaṃ taṃ paśyeyaṃ kathaṃ nv iti ।। tan na mitraṃ na dharmārthau kiṃ tu kāmo ayam arjitaḥ ।।
yūyaṃ hi sarvakāmibhyo bāhyā dārumanuṣyakāḥ ।। uttamā madhyamā hīnāś caturthās tu nakecana ।। adhamān kathayiṣyāmi bhavantas tu nakecana ।। aho nāgarakatvaṃ te niṣpannam anujīvinaḥ ।।
ko nāma mānuṣamukhaḥ sann aśuddham udāharet ।। prabhor adhikam ātmānam itthaṃ kaḥ kathayed iti ।। na hi prabhutvamātreṇa bhavaty uttamakāmukaḥ ।। akāmī kāmyate yas tu madhyo asāv aryaputravat ।।
te nakecana bhaṇyante ye na kāmyā na kāminaḥ ।। nakecana bhavantas tu yena nirlakṣaṇā iti ।। apṛcchad garjitamukhaṃ gomukhaṃ marubhūtikaḥ ।। svāmino yauvanamadhu kvāsau kathaya tām iti ।।
na tubhyaṃ sthalamaṇḍūka na hi bhasmani hūyate ।। pṛcchyatāṃ sthiragarvo ayaṃ prasādaḥ kriyatām iti ।। apratyākhyātakathitaṃ kathayety anumoditam ।। saṃkāsya śuddhakaṇṭhaś ca ramyām akathayat kathām ।।
abhivādayituṃ devyau narendrāntaḥpuraṃ gataḥ ।। varṇakramaviśuddhyā yad rājyam asyeva bhūpateḥ ।। paśyasīti tato devi trayam ity aham uktavān ।। ṛddhiṃ vaḥ śilpināṃ śilpaṃ bahuratnāṃ ca gām iti ।।
acetasyo hi puruṣaḥ katham evaṃ vaded iti ।। cetasyaḥ kiṃ nu guṇavān āho svid doṣavān iti ।। mā sma budhyata sā bālam acetasyaṃ ca mām iti ।। saṃcaran mandiraṃ ahaṃ nirgato rājaveśmanaḥ ।।
nirantarakhuranyāsaiḥ pārasīkais turaṃgamaiḥ ।। pratodagarbham ādhāya mūrdhany añjalim abravīt ।। kulakramāgatā bhṛtyārathavāhanajīvinaḥ ।। acirād bhavatā rathyāḥ kriyantāṃ turagā iti ।।
na tu saṃbhāvayāmy etān kuśalair aparīkṣitān ।। padavākyapramāṇārthacatureṇa āgamā iva ।। upacāro bhaved eṣa satyam evety acintayam ।। kāyasthaṃ samaṣīpātraṃ lekhanīkarṇapūrakam ।।
sarvathā dhig imāṃ kṣudrāṃ śvavṛttim anujīvinaḥ ।। acetasyāś ca kartavyaṃ teṣāṃ lekhyaṃ mayā kila ।। acetasyās tu sakalāṃ kṣobhayanti mahīm iti ।। prasāritāṅgulīkena mām uddiśya sakautukam ।।
ājīvārthacikitsākaṃ cikitsakam ivādhanam ।। ya evam anunīto api rathaṃ nāroḍhum icchati ।। cetasyapustakasyādau namaskārād anantaram ।। mā smānyaḥ kaścid ārohad ity āroham ahaṃ rathaṃ ।।
sukhāyamānaṃ madhurair ālāpair parikarmiṇām ।। anyato naya mātaṅgaṃ mā cetasyarathaṃ rudhaḥ ।। vihantum aham etasya necchām icchāmi dantinaḥ ।। icchāyāś cāvighātena tena naḥ kṣamyatām iti ।।
ādhoraṇaḥ pathānyena rathaḥ prasthāpyatām iti ।। cetasyāvāsamadhyena tvāṃ nayāmīti coktavān ।। rundhatā yena me mārgaṃ cetasyā darśitā iti ।। mālyabhūṣaṇadhūpādiprāyapaṇyaṃ vaṇikpatham ।।
saśarīrā iva nyastāvāstuvidyākṛtāṃ dhiyaḥ ।। tādṛśān eva puruṣān sevamānāḥ parāṅmukhān ।। tayā nirbhartsyamānaṃ ca vākyair madhuradāruṇaiḥ ।। bahuballavakacchuptāṃ chupa ballavikām iti ।।
kāṃcit koṇaparāmarśaśiñjānaparivādinīm ।। paṭhantīḥ paṭṭikā vyagrāḥ paśyāmi sma kumārikāḥ ।। dūrāt prahitakarṇena sphuṭam ākarṇitaṃ yathā ।। prāṇāpānau ca yatnena samaṃ saṃdhārayed iti ।।
manye sārathinopāyair ahaṃ veśaṃ praveśitaḥ ।। abhāṣata kṛtārtho ahaṃ nidrāṃ prāpsyāmi saṃprati ।। avandhyaṃ yauvanaṃ kartum eṣa veśaṃ vigāhate ।। adhunā tu rathaḥ kṣipraṃ pratīpaṃ nīyatām iti ।।
na ca darśanamātreṇa kaścid bhavati doṣavān ।। rathaḥ kiṃ pṛṣṭhato yātu kiṃ puraḥ preryatām iti ।। prairayat tatra cāpaśyaṃ mandiraṃ mandaronnatam ।। yoṣidvarṣavaraprāyaṃ vinītajanasaṃkulam ।।
kāntibādhitapadminyaḥ parivārya rathaṃ sthitāḥ ।। bhartṛdāraka vijñāpyam āgacchata kileti mām ।। jagataḥ prabhur apy eṣā yena praiṣyeva bhāṣate ।। yaiḥ kṛtā paratantreyaṃ lakṣmīr yena ca sūcitā ।।
dainyamlānamukhāmbhojās tā niraikṣanta pṛṣṭhataḥ ।। vātāyanaṃ kavāṭasthamaṇijālāṃśubhāsuram ।। vibhrāntagrāhiṇīpāṇikaraprakarapiñjaram ।। sarastaraṃgarandhrastham unnālam iva paṅkajam ।।
sukumāramarutprāptam iva vidrumapallavam ।। bhuvam āgatam ātmānam āśu cetitavān aham ।। karotu saphalaṃ tena bhartṛputra praviśyatām ।। dhuryān viśramayann āse jātatīvraśramān iti ।।
vārīm iva dṛḍhadvārām ādyāṃ kakṣyāṃ praveśitaḥ ।। adhīyamānavinayām apaśyaṃ nāgakanyakām ।। karṇīrathapravahaṇe śibikāṃ ca śivākṛtim ।। nānādeśāṃs tṛtīyāṇāṃ vājinaḥ sādhuvāhinaḥ ।।
sarāvakukkuṭavrātaṃ vayaḥpañjaramaṇḍalam ।। suvarṇatāratāmrāṇi kalpitāni tataḥ param ।। dhūpānulepanamlānavāsanāni tatas tataḥ ।। vāsāṃsi paṭṭakauśeyadūkūlaprabhṛtīni tu ।।
saṃskārān dṛṣṭavān asmi niśānavyadhanādikān ।। svakauśalāni śaṃsanto vighnanti sma gatiṃ mama ।। abruvan kāraṇīmūlyād bhavanto mūḍhabuddhayaḥ ।। durbhagair dhāryate kasmāt svaśilpakathitair iti ।।
prayuktaratnapuṣpārgham avocan mām atha striyaḥ ।। alaṃkṛtaṃ ca guptaṃ ca gamitaṃ ca pavitratām ।। guṇisaṅganimittā hi guṇā guṇavatām iti ।। kanyāyūthaparīvāraḥ prāptaḥ sopānapaddhatim ।।
prasuptae iva saṃsāre citre dṛṣṭiṃ nyaveśayam ।। aprameyaguṇākārāṃ kanyāṃ kanyābhir āvṛtām ।। pratyakṣeṇāpi tadrūpaṃ durnirūpaṃ nirūpakaiḥ ।। pāṣāṇapuruṣākāraḥ pratyakṣeṇa kim īkṣate ।।
na ca kālasvabhāvādyais tādṛśī sukarākṛtiḥ ।। kariṣyatha svayaṃ tasyāguṇarūpavicāraṇām ।। tadrūpaṃ vismitaḥ paśyaṃs tūṣṇīm āsaṃ muhūrtakam ।। ciraṃ gomukha jīveti māṃ pūrvaṃ samabhāṣata ।।
evaṃ nirabhimānā ca yayāhaṃ samayārthitaḥ ।। hastau praśastau tābhyāṃ hi pūrvam eva kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। apramattā hi jīvanti mṛtā eva pramādinaḥ ।। nikharvadantacaraṇaṃ tatra cāham upāviśam ।।
āgacchatīti kathitaṃ mayā rājakulād iti ।। rumaṇvadādayo vāpi mantriṇaḥ saparigrahāḥ ।। tūṣṇīṃbhūtā kṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭiṃ nāsāgre niścalām adhāt ।। mayā kuśalam ity uktaṃ mām apṛcchad asau punaḥ ।।
prakarṣo yasya yasyāṃ vo vidyāṃ kathaya tām iti ।। mānuṣair avigahye ca gāndharvajñānasāgare ।। rathādiyānavidyāsu niṣṭhāyātas tapantakaḥ ।। gṛhītāḥ sarvavidyānām ekadeśā manīṣitāḥ ।।
bhavatām ucitaḥ kālaḥ katamad vā vinodanam ।। maṅgalālaṃkṛtāḥ paścād itihāsam adhīmahe ।। abhyasyāmaḥ sayānāni niyuddhāny āyudhāni ca ।। arthaśāstrāṇi śaṃsanto mahākāvyāni cāsmahe ।।
ramāmahe sukhaṃ kāntair veṇutantrīrutair iti ।। bālikām antikāsīnāṃ dṛṣṭvāpaśyan madantikam ।। mayāsanne niviṣṭā sā manāg api na lakṣitā ।। yadāparā tadāyātā rūpiṇī rūpadevatā ।।
itaś cātithisatkāraḥ kim atra kriyatām iti ।। tasmād gurur guror ājñā saiva saṃpādyatām iti ।। kariṣyati nirutkaṇṭham ivaṃ tvā padmadevikā ।। na yuktam ananujñātaiḥ preṣyair āsannam āsitum ।।
praviśya rathasaṃkṣobhakhedaṃ vinayatām iti ।। śayanaṃ hemaratnāṅgaṃ sāpāśrayam apāśrayam ।। mandapuṇyair asaṃbhāvyāṃ pādasaṃvāhanām iti ।। saṃvāhakaviśeṣeṇa kim atreti mayoditam ।।
nirdoṣe mayi keneyaṃ prayuktā viṣakanyakā ।। viceṣṭāni ca me aṅgāni dhig anāryām imām iti ।। kathaṃ dāsajano vakṣaḥ śrāntaṃ vaḥ sevatām iti ।। spṛṣṭapādatalau hastāv urasy ādhātum icchati ।।
uraḥ spṛśati vaḥ ko vā karābhyāṃ mūḍhadhīr iti ।। paracittajñatā yasmān nāsti rāgavatām iti ।। stanotpīḍitakaṃ nāma saṃvāhanam aninditam ।। tato mām anujānīta bhartṛtantrā hi yoṣitaḥ ।।
anujñāṃ labhate yāvat tāvad āste nirākulā ।। yaḥ saṃvāhanaśāstrajñaḥ sa svatantraḥ pravartatām ।। saṃvāhayitum ārabdhā sakampena savepathu ।। saṃkṣiptavastu ramye arthe na kadācid virajyate ।।
upāgacchaṃ muhūrtāc ca tām evāryasutāgatā ।। ālapan madhurālāpā smitapracchāditāratiḥ ।। dṛśyamāno bhujaṃgo api kālena paricīyate ।। vijñāpyam asti me kiṃcit tac ca nādyety abhāṣata ।।
tam eva ratham āruhya kumārāgāram āgamam ।। upahāsaṃ ca kurvantaṃ taṃ tathā marubhūtikam ।। gatvāryaduhitur mūlam āseve padmadevikām ।। vṛttānto ayam atas teṣāṃ mā gamat karṇagocaram ।।
tad vaḥ kiṃ vismṛtaṃ kāryam iti meti mayoditam ।। dhatte saṃdhriyamāṇaṃ hi rahasyaṃ ramyatām iti ।। śokamūkapravṛddhāsram apaśyam abalājanam ।। mandaśabdaṃ mayā dṛṣṭā krandantī padmadevikā ।।
jaṅgamasya kutaḥ śoko yuvarāje ca rājati ।। tadā kila viṣaṇṇo ahaṃ mumoha ca papāta ca ।। tvannāthāślāghanīyeyam aśocyā padmadevikā ।। yasyāḥ śokopataptāyāyato rakṣas tato bhayam ।।
tvādṛśāṃ suhṛdāṃ yasyāḥ samaduḥkhasajīvanam ।। dṛṣṭā kamalinīkūle tatrāryaduhitā mayā ।। śoṣayantī saniśvāsair muhur viparivartanaiḥ ।। tadaṅkanyastacaraṇā dhyāyantī puruṣottamam ।।
devī duḥkhāṅgadānena saṃbhāvayatu mām iti ।। tathā mamāpratīkārāṃ lajjāśokakarīṃ kathām ।। taran makaragambhīrāṃ viśed vaitaraṇīm iti ।। bhartṛdārikayā kaścit smaryate na vimānitaḥ ।।
tato mām anujānātu dhṛṣṭo hi gaṇikājanaḥ ।। akṛtvā sāhasaṃ kair vā mahāl labdho manorathaḥ ।। bhedasaṃdhānadakṣo hi dūtaḥ kārye niyujyate ।। mahyam ākhyātum ārabdhā kṣaṇam adhīyatāṃ manaḥ ।।
sa samāhṛtavān kāntāḥ kumārīr ā mahodadheḥ ।। sukhāny anubhaviṣyāmi saṃtatānīty acintayat ।। tasyām eva sa saṃtuṣṭaḥ śuddhapuṇyārjitākṛtau ।। manoruhakarākārān aṣṭau prākalpayad gaṇān ।।
anujñātāsanacchatracāmarām akaron nṛpaḥ ।। taṃ mahāgaṇikāśabdam alabhanta narādhipāt ।। yāvad ghaṭakasaṃghaṭṭakaṭhorakaṭayaḥ khalāḥ ।। tataḥ kālāt prabhṛty eva bharatena pravartitaḥ ।।
jātā kaliṅgaseneyaṃ sarasyām iva padminī ।। anayā tanayā labdhā seyaṃ madanamañjukā ।। aham apy āci yāmīti punaḥ punar abhāṣata ।। gṛhītabālābharaṇām anayan nṛpasaṃsadam ।।
savikāsaiḥ satoṣeva kapolanayanādharaiḥ ।। karoti sma sakhīmadhye rājāsthānagatāḥ kathāḥ ।। prātaḥ sādaram ādatta citraṃ maṇḍanam ātmanaḥ ।। tayā pṛṣṭā kva yāsīti yatra tvam iti cābravīt ।।
rājāsthānaṃ tanusnehāḥ paruṣā hi narādhipāḥ ।। dhṛṣṭā hi dveṣyatāṃ yānti praṇayinyo api yoṣitaḥ ।। kaṭukā durghaṭāś ceyaṃ manyamānā nyavartata ।। muktanidrāśanālāpā śayyaikaśaraṇābhavat ।।
svaptum icchāmy ahaṃ sakhyas tāvan nirgamyatām iti ।। etāḥ prasthāpitāḥ sakhyaḥ kim akāraṇam etayā ।। tasyās tā eva nighnanti nidrām iti na badhyate ।। maṇḍanavyāpṛtām etāṃ paśyāmi sma sadarpaṇā ।।
janmāntare api bhūyāsam ahaṃ tasmin vadhūr iti ।। udalambayad ātmānaṃ satvarā nāgadantake ।। kaṇṭhapāśaṃ tam etasyāḥ kālapāśam ivākṣipam ।। balāt pratyānayaṃ saṃjñāṃ pretarājakulād aham ।।
ninīya mayi mattaś ca pratyāhṛtyedam abravīt ।। vyasane praharantyā tu śatrutvaṃ darśitaṃ tvayā ।। tvayā jīvitam ujjhantī vidhṛtā kim akāraṇam ।। vighnantyā mama saṃkalpaṃ darśitā pratikūlatā ।।
aśeṣopāyaduḥsādhyo mitram śatrur mahān iti ।। svāmini prabhur ity asmān upālambhena takṣasi ।। svāminyā vayam āyāte kasmin nābhyantarīkṛtāḥ ।। tanum ekākinī tyaktvā sukham āsitum icchasi ।।
jīviṣyāmas tataḥ sarvāmariṣyāmo viparyaye ।। ekajīvaśarīrāyai kiṃ tubhyam api kathyate ।। idam ākhyāya te ko vā strībhyaḥ sāhasikaḥ paraḥ ।। dakṣiṇaṃ parighākāram ūrum āropitā tadā ।।
mayā dṛṣṭaḥ praviṣṭaś ca hṛdayaṃ me anivāritaḥ ।। saumyo api puṇyavān asmān nirdhūmaṃ dagdhum icchati ।। adhunā śrūyamāṇo api kiṃ vā vilapitair iti ।। upāyam etam āśaṅkya samudrotsekaduṣkaram ।।
etām āśvāsayāmi sma niḥsārair vacanair iti ।। vaśayeyaṃ tava prītyai kiṃ punaḥ puruṣeśvaram ।। rājāno api hi sāmādīn krameṇaiva prayuñjate ।। lokenālakṣitā kāṃścit sahasva divasān iti ।।
antaś cākathayat toṣaṃ vikasan mukhapaṅkajā ।। kāryasaṃsiddhasaṃbaddhair darśitāśām ayāpayam ।। moktukāmā tadā prāṇān punar utprekṣitā mayā ।। saṃpradhārya tayā sārdham upāyo ayam anuṣṭhitaḥ ।।
sa kenacid upāyena veśam āśu praveśyatām ।। manaḥśrotraharālāpo vasantam iva kokilaḥ ।। padmāvatyai tayā cāsi cetasya iti bhāṣitaḥ ।। dhūrtair asmatprayuktais tvaṃ veśam etaṃ praveśitaḥ ।।
tantrīṇāṃ varṇatantrīva madhurā padmadevikā ।। na nivedayate tubhyaṃ svārthabhraṃśaviśaṅkayā ।। asādhyāyataniśvāsā nirāśā dṛśyatām iti ।। tvadāyattaḥ sa śeṣaś ca saṃvidhattāṃ bhavān iti ।।
kuṭhāracchedyatāṃ nītaṃ bhavatībhir idaṃ tṛṇam ।। mucyatām eṣa saṃtāpaḥ siddhaṃ viddhi prayojanam ।। saṃdhātā gomukhaś ceti dhanyas trikasamāgamaḥ ।। rājahaṃso hi nalinīṃ svayam evopasarpati ।।
svāminyai kārayiṣyāmi praṇāmam acirād iti ।। kiṃ tu prastāvam āsādya yatethāḥ kāryasiddhaye ।। aniṣṭaphalatāṃ vāpi kopayitvā prabhūn iti ।। ucchiṣṭān āgataś cāsmi gṛhītvā modakādikān ।।
svayam ārabhya hastābhyāṃ yuṣmabhyaṃ prahitā iti ।। āśvāsanti kṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā mṛgā hi mṛgatṛṣṇikām ।। yuṣmābhiḥ preṣitānīti tām āśvāsitavān aham ।। alabdhāvasaraḥ kālam etāvantam ayāpayam ।।
aho saṃbhāvanā kāryā mahānāgarako bhavān ।। kim iyaṃ vañcyate mugdhā patrapuṣpaphalādibhiḥ ।। viraktam api saṃdhātum alaṃ kauśalam asti naḥ ।। phalena jñāsyasīty uktvā prastāvāvahito abhavam ।।
tan mayā kāritā yūyaṃ kṣiptvā hariśikhādikān ।। tad aryaduhitādhyāsta vidyudabhram iva dhvanat ।। yuṣmabhyaṃ darśitaṃ vandyaṃ tat tayā vandamānayā ।। unnamyatām iti mayā tatrāpīdaṃ prayojanam ।।
kṛtas toṣayatā kāntām asmākaṃ svāminīm iti ।। prajñāparākramaprāṇaṃ lakṣmīr iva narādhipam ।। naveva mālatī mālā lobhanīyaguṇākṛtiḥ ।। na hy āśīviṣadagdhaantrāḥ kṣamante divasān iti ।।
tatkathāpahṛtavrīḍaḥ prakāśam aham abravam ।। aśīrṇaṃ manmathataroḥ prakīrṇaṃ bījam etayā ।। bādhamānaṃ mano jātam ucchvasatkarkaśāṅkuram ।। kampaniḥśvāsajananān amuñjat pallavān iva ।।
na samākramya mṛdnāti tāvad darśaya tām iti ।। tvatpravīṇo aham ity uktau tau ca bhūpatinā kila ।। yasya yā kuśalā śiṣyā sa nartayatu tām iti ।। nṛtyantīṃ nṛpatir draṣṭā tatra draṣṭāstha tām iti ।।
ity adhyāsitacetasā katham api prakrāntayā cintayā paryaṅkāṅkavivartinārtatanunā nītā triyāmā mayā ।। saṃprasthāpya manaḥ pūrvaṃ nṛpāsthānam agām aham ।। praṇamya tadanujñātaṃ mañcāntaram aseviṣi ।। nṛtyācāryau namaskṛtya mahīpālam avocatām ।।
draṣṭum icchatha yāṃ pūrvam ājñāpayata tām iti ।। gomukhaḥ sa ca yām āha sā pūrvaṃ nṛtyatām iti ।। sa suyāmunadanteti tadupādhyāyam ādiśat ।। raṅgaśeṣas tu niśceṣṭaḥ suṣuptāvasthāṃ gataḥ ।।
manonetrāṅgasaṃcārair anāhāryair acintayam ।। kuta eva parājetum abalā bālikā priyā ।। paṅkāvilajalāṃ paśyet tathādhyāsam ahaṃ priyām ।। aśaktaḥ prekṣituṃ tena raṅgān nirgamyatām iti ।।
vatsarājakulāt tena muhūrtaṃ sthīyatām iti ।। jīvalokam iva jyotsnā priyā raṅgam arañjayat ।। mudrikālatikā ceti sa vihasyedam abravīt ।। eṣā naḥ svāminī devī vāmato mudrikālatā ।।
dṛṣṭā kena śarajjyotsnā khadyotaprabhayā jitā ।। dṛṣṭā saṃbhāvayāmy asyās tena nṛttaguṇān iti ।। tāvaj jaya jayety uccair vimuktaḥ prekṣakair dhvaniḥ ।। dainyavepathuvaivarṇyaviṣādaiḥ sahajair iva ।।
svam āvāsaṃ vrajāmi sma kāntācintāpuraḥsaraḥ ।। na hy ādeśam upekṣante tvādṛśā mādṛśām iti ।। śraddhāsyati na me vākyaṃ vipralabdhā hi sā mayā ।। marubhūtika evātra yogya ity ayam uktavān ।।
apāyaśatam ālokya kadācij jālam ālikhet ।। yatpradhānastriyas tatra rājaputraḥ pravartyate ।। vihanyād api naḥ kāryaṃ tasmād eṣa na yujyate ।। tasmād evaṃvidhe kārye niyogaṃ nāyam arhati ।।
abhyastasāhasas tasmād eṣa prasthāpyatām iti ।। prāptaṃ hariśikho apṛcchat kiṃ vṛttaṃ bhavator iti ।। āyāty abhimukhī yaiva saiva yāti parāṅmukhī ।। na spraṣṭavyo na saṃbhāṣyo gomukhaḥ pāpavān iti ।।
kakṣyādvāraiḥ praviṣṭau svaḥ sthānam aryasutāsthitam ।। dhūrtenānena cāturyād gomayaṃ pāyasīkṛtam ।। tam eva paśyatānena vācālena guṇīkṛtam ।। saṃbhrāntaś ca vilakṣaś ca tadā tām āha gomukhaḥ ।।
sevakaḥ paricittajñaḥ svāminaṃ kopayed iti ।। kathaṃ niṣkāraṇo nāma kim idaṃ laghu kāraṇam ।। tvayā nartayatā kāntā kim iyaṃ sukham āsitā ।। paśyann abhimukhaṃ prītyā sa tathā vimukhīkṛtaḥ ।।
tvam icchasi jayaṃ yasyāḥ kim asau na parājitā ।। uktavān paśyatānarthaṃ doṣo bhūto guṇo api naḥ ।। kadācid itarāṃ naiva paśyed vṛttakutūhalaḥ ।। pakṣapātān narendreṇa dṛṣṭā madanamañjukā ।।
norvaśīm api paśyet saḥ kuto madanamañjukām ।। mayopāyaḥ prayukto asau katham ity avadhīyatām ।। kṛtānukaraṇaiḥ sākṣād bharatenāpi nṛtyatā ।। sahajair iva vaivarṇyavivādasvedavepanaiḥ ।।
bhaktyārādhitabhartāraḥ sevakā hanta duḥsthitāḥ ।। saṃdeśaśravaṇāt tena saṃmānayata mām iti ।। īṣadvihasitajyotsnāsalilasnapitādharā ।। na hi vatseśvarāsannāḥ śrūyante strīsuhṛddruhaḥ ।।
tat kṣamasva na hi svāsthābādhante tvādṛśām iti ।। saṃdehaś ced iyaṃ mudrā tadīyā dṛśyatām iti ।। koṭiḥ kim iti nānītāna hi te kṣīṇamṛttikāḥ ।। na hy ārabhyamahākāryāḥ pramādyanti sacetasaḥ ।।
svāminā preṣitaḥ prītyā dṛśyatāṃ marubhūtikaḥ ।। yat saṃdiśati naḥ svāmī yuṣmabhyaṃ tan niśāmyatām ।। krīḍatāsmadvidhair eṣa vilakṣaḥ kriyatām iti ।। iyaṃ prasādhyate yāvat tāvad āstāṃ bhavān iti ।।
āha prakṛṣṭapramudā praphullanayanotpalā ।। tenāpi bhūmipataye vṛttānto ayaṃ niveditaḥ ।। jīvalokasukhāny eṣa tasmād anubhavatv iti ।। iyam āyāti te paścād yātu tāvad bhavān iti ।।
sayāno gomukhaḥ prāha laghu śrāvaya mām iti ।। sa praviśyoktavān dvāre devī kiṃ vidhṛteti mām ।। kuru nāgarakaṃ tāvat tvaṃ mām ity aham uktavān ।। yad etad ghuṣyate loke tad etat tathyatāṃ gatam ।।
iyaṃ hi mokṣavidyeva prayogāvṛttisādhanā ।। tat tad evānukuryās tvaṃ dakṣo hi labhate śriyam ।। sukhaṃ supyāstam ity uktvā yathāsvaṃ sasuhṛdgataḥ ।। kṛtaṃ tathaiva ca mayā vanditena ca vanditā ।।
tad evānukaromi sma nartanācāryaśiṣyavat ।। smitvā sotkamparomāñcaṃ gāḍham aṅgam apīḍayat ।। aśarīrasya kasyāpi gato bhūtasya vaśyatām ।। pradoṣa eva kṣaṇadā kṣīṇā kṣaṇavad āvayoḥ ।।
mātur evānayad gehaṃ manmānasapuraḥsarām ।। dineṣu mama saṃprāptaḥ senānīr idam abravīt ।। mauhūrtānumato rājā rātreḥ śāntipuraḥsaram ।। yuṣmābhir api kartavyaṃ yat tad ājñāpyatām iti ।।
iti tasmin nate mahyaṃ gomukhena niveditam ।। tenaiva sahitā yūyaṃ gantāraḥ śanakair iti ।। pratiṣṭhe sasuhṛt prātaḥ pṛṣṭhato janasaṃhateḥ ।। divasaṃ gamayāmi sma taṃ triyāmāmukhotsukaḥ ।।
niśāyāṃ yātakalpāyām apaśyaṃ rudatīm imām ।। yadā noktavatī kiṃcit tadānyā dārikābravīt ।। gaṇikāśabdadoṣas tu nainām adyāpi muñcati ।। tasyāś cāmaradhāriṇyā bhavitavyaṃ kilānayā ।।
viṣapānakṛtotsāhā hātum icchaty asūn iti ।। nityotkṣapitam akṣībaṃ tyaktvā sthāsyāmy avedanaḥ ।। vṛttāntam evam ākarṇya bhīṣaṇaṃ sabhiyo abhavan ।। vayam eva visaṃ pūrvaṃ pibāmaḥ kalpyatām iti ।।
yo hi mūlam anarthasya sa tāvat pāyyatām iti ।। abravīd gomukho vakti kiṃ mayātaḥ prayojanam ।। aham adhyetum ārabhdo vaidyād prāṇapradād iti ।। preryamāṇaṃ galāṣṭrābhiḥ śīghram ānaya taṃ śaṭham ।।
।। svāminyā saha saṃyogaḥ so ayam evaṃ vijṛmbhate ।। jvariṣyāmīti saṃcintya maṇḍaṃ pibati muṇḍitaḥ ।। tatraiva vidyāma nyañco pāsyāmas tyajyatāṃ tvarā ।।
vijñāpayatu tenāsya dattaḥ pūrvam ayaṃ varaḥ ।। siddhiṃ yāsyati cāvaśyaṃ mā sma śaṅkāṃ karod iti ।। mātur evānayan mūlaṃ prāviśāma tataḥ purīm ।। gomukhena yad ākhyātaṃ tat kāryaṃ sādhyatām iti ।।
gatvā rājakulaṃ tasmād āgatyedam abhāṣata ।। śālīnena mayāpy uktaṃ modako dīyatām iti ।। yācate sma prahīṇatvād gatvā gatvā mahīpatim ।। dinarajanīvihāraviparītam aham caritai rathacaraṇāhvayasya caritāni viḍambitavān ।।
vādī jita ivācchāyas trapayā gomukho abravīt ।। tato api vandituṃ devyau narendrāntaḥpuraṃ gataḥ ।। kiṃkāraṇaṃ vadhūr adya nāsmān āyāti vanditum ।। kopitā vā bhaved bhartrā śiṣṭā duścaritair iti ।।
nāsti naḥ svāminīty uktvā devyor nipatitā puraḥ ।। rājā ca śrutavṛttāntaḥ sāsthāno dhairyam atyajat ।। kathaṃ jānāsi nāstīti pṛṣṭācaṣṭa niśāmyatām ।। tathaiva kagiti ghrāto gandho asmābhir amānuṣaḥ ।।
śūnyām īkṣāmahe śayyām aśrīkāṃ nalinīm iva ।। na kvacic ca vicinvatyaḥ paśyāmaḥ svāminīm iti ।। idaṃ tad āgataṃ manya durvidyādharaceṣṭitam ।। harmyāgre krīḍayāmi sma candrikāsaṅgaśītale ।।
ekām eva mayā labdhāṃ sutāṃ durlabhikām iti ।। avātarad divaḥ ko api divyagandhasragambaraḥ ।। gambhīradhvanivitrastatanayām idam abravīt ।। tato muñca nayāmy enāṃ nyāsabhūtā hi kanyakā ।।
sarvavijñeyavijñānamanojvalitadhīr iti ।। prayatnād dhairyam ādhāya pragalbheva tam abravam ।। na punar dīyate tāvad bālikā śaiśavād iti ।। dṛśyamāno mahāvegaḥ kṣaṇenāntarhito abhavat ।।
vidyādharādhamenāsau nītā yadi bhaved iti ।। yad atrānantaraṃ nyāyyaṃ tad anuṣṭhīyatām iti ।। preritaḥ pavaneneva prabalena balāhakaḥ ।। tiṣṭha tiṣṭha kva yāsīti prālapaṃ gaganonmukhaḥ ।।
yathānilatuṣārābhyāṃ śiśire kamalākaraḥ ।। kim etad iti pṛṣṭena vṛttānto ayaṃ mayoditaḥ ।। viṣādākulito rājā prasthito yuṣmadantikam ।। sarvathā khyāpitaṃ lokair bhavatāṃ nītikauśalam ।।
vipralabdho asmi yuṣmābhir devyā vāsavadattayā ।। apanītā vadhūḥ kasmād bālān mama sutād iti ।। yuṣmān dṛṣṭvā hi sa śiśuḥ prāṇān api parityajet ।। āsīnān āsane tena nivṛtya sthīyatām iti ।।
anāthāpi na vaḥ kācit kenacit paribhūyate ।। nāsty asau yo na cāsmābhir īkṣitaś cāracakṣuṣā ।। tena vidyādhareṇāsau hṛteti hṛdaye mama ।। kadācit kupitā bhartre tatrāsīta vadhūr iti ।।
sādhubhiḥ kathyamānāni pañca sthānāni tad yathā ।। duṣṭasaṃcāraśūnyāni mandiropavanāni vā ।। prastāve yan mayā pūrvaṃ śrutaṃ tad avadhīyatām ।। āsīd yā caritākāraiḥ sāvitrīm atiricyate ।।
brahmann akṛtadāro asmi sutā me dīyatām iti ।। kiṃ tu datteyam anyasmai kṣamatāṃ bhagavān iti ।। amṛtā nāma duhitā mama sā gṛhyatām iti ।। ātmānam aṅgirā mene pītāmṛtam ivāmṛtam ।।
upālabdhavatī nātham ṛṣiputrasya vallabhā ।। ahaṃ tv anicchate tubhyaṃ pitrā dattā balād iti ।। kaṃcid abhyanayat kālam ekadāstaṃgate ravau ।। apṛcchad amṛtāgatya kiṃ dhyāyati bhavān iti ।।
devīṃ vihāya sāvitrīṃ kim anyac cintayāmy aham ।। devatābhyo namaskṛtya śarīram udalambayat ।। vidyutpiṅgajaṭābhārāṃ sākṣamālākamaṇḍalum ।। devatāvocad amṛtām amṛteneva siñcatī ।।
straiṇam ajñānam āśritya saṃtuṣṭo hi patis tvayā ।। kiṃ tv ahaṃ brahmarudraādisaptalokanamaskṛtā ।। balena tapasā yasya na samāno bhaviṣyati ।। amṛtāpi gatāśaṅkā bhartrā saha sameyuṣī ।।
udyānaṃ praviśett tatra svayam anviṣyatām iti ।। cakṣuścetoharākārāḥ paśyan veśyāḥ samūhaśaḥ ।। api nāmāsya kasyāṃcit striyāṃ bhāvo bhaved iti ।। rater anyāsu saṃkalpaḥ pramadāsu pravartate ।।
kāntāmātur gṛhaṃ kāntaṃ kāntāśūnyam upāgamam ।। anviṣyanto bhramāma sma na cāpaśyāma tatra tām ।। pṛcchāmi sma priyāvārttāṃ sākṣiśākhāmṛgāṇḍajān ।। viḍambayann aśāstrajñam ity utkaṭarasaṃ naṭam ।।
aryaputrāryaduhitā mayā dṛṣṭety abhāṣata ।। api satyam idaṃ saumya syāt krīḍety aham abravam ।। asatye hy atra yā krīḍā tad unmattavijṛmbhitam ।। tvaritaṃ gamyatāṃ yasmān nārtaḥ kālam udīkṣate ।।
raktaṃ kusumasaṃghātam ayam ābhūmipallavam ।। tasya skandhe hriyālīnam apaśyaṃ prāṇadāyinīm ।। sadyaḥ kusumito aśokaḥ prāpya sarvāṅgasaṃgatim ।। vanadevatayodyānaṃ sakalaṃ na vijṛmbhitam ।।
subhage nirvikāratvād aṅgāratuṣabhasmavat ।। tayā cāṅgāni saṃhṛtya mā tāvad iti vāritaḥ ।। sābravīd aparodho ayam aryaputreṇa mṛṣyatām ।। aryaputrasya bhūyāsaṃ dayitā paricārikā ।।
pānaṃ hastena dāsyāmi prasīdatu bhavān iti ।। āyācitaṃ tu yakṣāya na mayā pratiyācitam ।। vṛttāntaḥ kathitaś cāyam athokto dhanadena saḥ ।। nītvā samarpaya kṣipraṃ dārakāya vadhūm iti ।।
śarīraṃ paruṣībhūtaṃ vāritā stha tato mayā ।। । tasmai yakṣāya yuṣmābhiḥ sa me saṃpādyatām iti ।। adyārabhya kulastrītvaṃ bhavatīnāṃ bhavatv iti ।।
yācñāvṛttikadarthitair bahubhir apy āptair na hi prārthakāḥ prītiṃ yānti tathā yathā tanubhir apy arthaiḥ sukhābhyāgataiḥ ।। priyāṃ navavadhūveṣāṃ pradoṣe pariṇītavān ।। tām ādāya svam āvāsaṃ pravṛttotsavam āgamam ।। abhyarcya pānadānena suduṣtoṣam atoṣayat ।।
ādāya madhunaḥ pūrṇāṃ tato mām abravīt priyā ।। eṣā dhanapateḥ śeṣā svādur āsvādyatām iti ।। nāhaṃ sevitum icchāmi kiṃ punar vyasanaṃ mahat ।। cirān niruttarīkṛtya mām anicchum apāyayat ।।
kim āsvādam idaṃ pānam iti pratyabravaṃ tataḥ ।। kṣaye kaṣāyakaṭukam avacchede manāg iti ।। pīyatām iti pītaṃ ca punas tadvacanād mayā ।। kim artham api me cittaṃ gatam asvasthatām iti ।।
gamiṣyaty acirād eva cittaṃ te svasthatām iti ।। taruprāsādaśailādīn sthāvarān api jaṅgamān ।। anicchan pāyitaḥ pānaṃ tathā tām apy apāyayam ।। yad eva rucitam tābhyāṃ tat taivāsmi pravartitaḥ ।।
tena kṛtrimam evāsau kanyātvaṃ pratipāditā ।। ghrātvā hariśikho veśma saṃbhrāntamatir uktavān ।। manye aryaputrayā yūyam anicchāḥ pāyitā iti ।। bhavatāpi rucau satyāṃ sthīyatāṃ pīyatām iti ।।
pānaṃ sādhu na paśyāmi kiṃ punar mantriṇām iti ।। pālayatsu kim asmākam ātmabhir vañcitair iti ।। anuṣṭhāne punas tasya svātantryaṃ svāminām iti ।। niḥśaṅkaḥ pātum ārabdhas taṃ ca dṛṣṭvā tapantakaḥ ।।
punar uktapriyālāpo mām avandata gomukhaḥ ।। pādau saṃvāhayantaṃ me kruddho hariśikho abravīt ।। udvejayasi bhartāram apasṛtyāsyatām iti ।। svāmino niḥsapatnau tu pādāv icchāmi sevitum ।।
bhaviṣyatas tadāsmākaṃ sasapatnau bhaviṣyataḥ ।। smitasaṃdarśitaprītir abravīt sāśrulocanā ।। ālāpā nirgatāḥ saumyād gomukhasya mukhād iti ।। ko vā tavedam ākāram ujjvalaṃ kṛtavān iti ।।
ājñāpitās tava bhrātrā pānam āsevitaṃ niśi ।। svayam āsvādya tad bhrātre tvayā prasthāpyatām iti ।। pānāgārāya gamitaḥ pānādhyakṣapuraḥsaraḥ ।। matto ahaṃ preṣayāmi sma yuṣmabhyam api saṃtatam ।।
anujnātāḥ sahāmātyair gurubhir muditair iti ।। divasān gamayāmi sma prahṛṣṭaparicārakaḥ ।। yuṣmābhiḥ sukhasuptāhaṃ na draṣṭavyety abhāṣata ।। yat satyaṃ sutarāṃ cetaḥ kutūhalataraṅgitam ।।
pāne pariṇatiṃ yāti pratibuddhaḥ pipāsitaḥ ।। na yuktaṃ sukhasuptasya śatror api nibodhanam ।। pratibodhya jalaṃ yāce tad dhi me na virūpyate ।। yāvad anyaiva sā kāpi nārīrūpaiva candrikā ।।
mānuṣī syāt kulastrī syād gaṇikā syād iyaṃ na hi ।। tasmād vidyādharī prāptā kāpi kenāpi hetunā ।। gāḍhaṃ saṃvāhayāmi sma tasyāś caraṇapallavau ।। mām ālokya tathābhūtaṃ bhītā bhūmāv upāviśat ।।
tvādṛśām anukampyo hi balināṃ pramadājanaḥ ।। evaṃ kāriṇam apy eṣā saṃbhāvayati mām iti ।। lajjām apaharantīva tvaritedam abhāṣata ।। tvadguṇasmaraṇavyagrā nayate divasān iti ।।
jyotsnā hi sphuṭadhavalāpi kaumudīndor andhānāṃ bahalatamomalīmasaiva ।। tathāpi tu vinodena tiṣṭhāmaḥ kathyatām iti ।। yasmāt tena viśuddhyarthaṃ svānam ācaritaṃ tayā ।। śūrapaṇḍitavittāḍhyavidyādharakulālayaḥ ।।
yaḥ kuberādhikasvo api niḥsva eva dinātyaye ।। tṛṇāya manyate sthairyād yā devīṃ pṛthivīm api ।। prauḍhāyā iva kanyāyāḥ pitarau sadṛśaṃ varam ।। ārādhayitum ārabdhau tayā coktaṃ prasannayā ।।
bhavitā bhavatoḥ putraḥ putrakau duḥkham ujjhatam ।। śūraḥ sāṅga ivānaṅgo vidyādharapatiḥ patiḥ ।। trivargam akṣataṃ devī pṛthivīva surakṣitā ।। tasmān mānasavegākhyaḥ putraḥ pitrā prasādhitaḥ ।।
nāma vegavatātmīyam asau vegavatī tataḥ ।। nītavantau ciraṃ kālam ekāharniśasaṃmitam ।। bhadrāsanastham ātmānaṃ dadarśa ādarśamaṇḍale ।। mṛṇāladhavalaṃ keśaṃ dṛṣṭavān ātmamūrdhani ।।
pṛṣṭo mānasavegena kim etad iti vegavān ।। tapāṃsi vā niṣevante vedāntavihitāni vā ।। pālitair hi mṛgendro api kānanair eva pālyate ।। rājā mandasukhotkaṇṭhaḥ pratiyātas tapovanam ।।
na nivṛttā yadā devī tadopāyaṃ prayuktavān ।। na me saṃpādayaty ājñām aho dharmaḥ satām iti ।। pādayoḥ patitā patyur vyajñāpayad asau śanaiḥ ।। upāsyāḥ pāvanatamaṃ sa kālaḥ kathyatām iti ।।
bhartāraṃ vegavatyāś ca dṛṣṭvā draṣṭāsi mām iti ।। uktā vegavatī mātrā pitaraṃ praṇatābravīt ।। kalpavṛkṣaprasūtāni phalāni kusumāni vā ।। tat tan mānasavegas te bhrātā dātāsyatām iti ।।
gurusattvarajastamaḥkalaṅkāṃ prakṛtiṃ hātum agād vanaṃ narendraḥ ।। śaktitrayaprayogajñaḥ kṛtavān acalācalām ।। āṣāḍhaṃ vāyumukteti sakhīparivṛtāgamat ।। uttiṣṭhākāśamārgeṇa gacchāmo malayācalam ।।
netrāpidhānikākhyānaputrikākandukair iti ।। alabdhakulavidyāyāḥ sakhi tan mṛṣyatām iti ।। ādhatāmbarapakṣāḥ khaṃ haṃsakanyā ivāsthitāḥ ।। tena coktāṅkam āropya mātaḥ kiṃ dīyatām iti ।।
siddhavidyābhir adyāhaṃ sakhībhir hāsitā yataḥ ।। bhrātā visarjitāsārabālālaṅkāravañcitā ।। gatā vegavatīṃ draṣṭum āṣāḍhaṃ sasakhī sakhīm ।। sapakṣā rājahaṃsīva gatā prati himācalam ।।
kim ayaṃ kṣipyate kālo vidyā me dīyatām iti ।। gurukāryakriyāvyagraṃ kiṃ na paśyasi mām iti ।। apatan mātur utsaṅge saṃtapteva vaśā hrade ।। acireṇa pitur mūlaṃ dārikāṃ nayataṃ yuvām ।।
bhrātaras tu dviṣanty eva bhrātṝn ekodarān api ।। mārgāyatanamārgeṣu sāmbhaḥsu gamitaśramām ।। te apaśyaṃs tatra vṛndāni tāpasānāṃ tapasyatām ।। brahman brūhi tam uddeśaṃ yatrāste vegavān iti ।।
anugacchati gacchantam aṃśumantaṃ ca cakṣuṣā ।। aṅgaṇe krīḍataḥ prītāv imau ca śikhipannagau ।। tasyāhlādayituṃ cakṣur eṣa mandāyate raviḥ ।। kāyakleśaṃ vahann āgād vaikhānasamṛgāvṛtaḥ ।।
abravīn mantriṇau nāyaṃ mama tātaḥ sa vegavān ।। prabhāsayanti dhāvantīṃ puraḥ sāmantasantatim ।। tyaktavairaiḥ sahāyāti nūnaṃ ko apīndrajālikaḥ ।। tādṛśā eva dṛśyante tathā cetthaṃ ca sādhavaḥ ।।
aṅkam āropitā pitrā rūḍhadarbhāṅkuravraṇam ।। śirovāgbhir avandetām atha vegavatoditau ।। janarañjanamātraṃ hi gataṃ tad rājyanāṭakam ।। rājño mānasavegasya rājyaṃ no varṇyatām iti ।।
tam apekṣya tu rājānaḥ śeṣāś chattraviḍambakāḥ ।। vidyālābhārtham ity uktaṃ tasmai tābhyāṃ savistaram ।। yuvābhyāṃ nītipannābhyāṃ sa bālaḥ pālyatām iti ।। kalpitāhārakartavyā phalamūlajalānilaiḥ ।।
ārādhayad durārādhān asau vaikhānasān api ।। hā sarpeṇāsmi daṣṭeti sākrandāgamad āśramam ।। mā rājadārike bhaiṣīr ity uktvā parivāritā ।। amuṣmin mallikāgulmae iti tebhyo nyavedayat ।।
rājaputri na sarpo ayam ayaṃ sarpāntakaḥ śikhī ।। tvayā sarpa iti jñātaṃ tasmād āśvasyatām iti ।। vicitrair nartito mārgais tayā kuṭṭitatālayā ।। militāḥ sarvae evāsthus tapovananivāsinaḥ ।।
viśrāntam upagamyedam avocaṃs taṃ tapasvinaḥ ।। vayam ārādhitāḥ prītās tad vidyāṃ labhatām iti ।। tato gṛhṇātv iyaṃ vidyāḥ pañcāṅgaparivāritāḥ ।। tad asyāḥ kulavidyānām alaṃ bhavatu siddhaye ।।
balaṃ caturguṇaṃ tasmād bāleyaṃ pratipadyatām ।। rājyasya daśamaṃ bhāgaṃ sa madīyasya bhokṣyati ।। sāpi labdhābhyanujñānā vegenodapatan nabhaḥ ।। piśaṅgabhavatī yāntī śyāmalām ambarasthalīm ।।
avātarat tadāsthāne haṃsīvāmbhojakānane ।। āliṅgyotsaṅgam āropya gamitā mātur antikam ।। apṛcchad api kalyāṇi kuśalī vegavān iti ।। yāsau vegavatī sāhaṃ tasya vegavataḥ sutā ।।
nītā mānasavegena kāpi bhūmau varāṅganā ।। kṣīṇadoṣaguṇā sādhvī kāmastutikathām iva ।। balād bhoktum upakrāntas tayā coktaṃ sphurad ruṣā ।। kiṃ tu vegavataḥ sādhoḥ putratvaṃ tena mucyase ।।
adhīrahṛdayāḥ prāyas trāsagamyā bhavādṛśāḥ ।। bhavataḥ śatadhā mūrdhā dagdhabuddheḥ sphuṭed iti ।। api notsahate draṣṭuṃ kuta eva niṣevitum ।। protsāhyatāṃ yathā kṣipram upasarpati mām iti ।।
aśokavanikāmadhye dṛṣṭā madanamañjukā ।। mlānacampakamāleva purāṇakadalīpuṭam ।। uṭajābhyantare nyastaḥ sajalaḥ kalaśas tayā ।। kas te mānuṣakeṇārthaḥ kuru vidyādharaṃ patiṃ ।।
vidyādharās tu vidyānāṃ prabhāvān nirupadravāḥ ।। yo vidyādhararājānāṃ rājā sphītaśriyām iti ।। tathā tathābhavat tasyāḥ prītisphītākṣam ānanam ।। tathā tathābhavat tasyāḥ krodhajihmākṣam ānanam ।।
gṛhṇāti sma tadā śokaḥ saniśvāsāsravepathuḥ ।। alaṃ bhagini saṃtapya jīvitaṃ rakṣyatām iti ।। aśakyaṃ tu bhayaṃ bhīmam āhṛtaṃ mandayā mayā ।। kulavidyādhanair yaś ca tuṅgair api na mādyati ।।
tataḥ sāntaḥpurāmātyarāṣṭraḥ somānvayo nṛpaḥ ।। yad ādiṣṭaḥ sphuṭādeśair asau vidyādharādibhiḥ ।। vidyādharanarendro ayaṃ kartā vāntaviṣān iti ।। vidyādharanarendraḥ syād uta na syād asāv iti ।।
dūtikā matsamā nāsti svayam eva vrajāmy ataḥ ।। tava priyāya kiṃ vārtā tvadīyā dīyatām iti ।। tulyam evāvayoḥ kāryaṃ śaktau satyāṃ kim āsyate ।। īdṛśaṃ tvādṛśī karma kāryate katham anyathā ।।
daṣṭukāmeva capalā bhīṣaṇāśīviṣāṅganā ।। aryaputreṇa vā dagdhadāruṇā gatidāruṇā ।। asaṅgā hi gatiḥ sakhyāḥ kāntaṃ yāntyāḥ smṛter iva ।। apaśyam aryaputraṃ ca hā kvāsīti pravādinam ।।
