ajjukārūpayā tubhyam ātmā saṃdarśito mayā ।। sa doṣaḥ kanyakātvasya viśuddhakulajanmanaḥ ।। sa ca saṃskartum ātmānaṃ kvātra yakṣaḥ kva cājjukā ।। tatra yat kāraṇaṃ tac ca prāyaḥ pratyakṣam eva ca ।।
tat kutūhalavṛddhyarthaṃ vāmaśīlā hi bālatā ।। nītā mānasavegena lakṣmīr iva durātmanā ।। ānayāmi parair nītāṃ śuddhā nītir iva śriyam ।। bhartuḥ kārayituṃ karma bhāryāṃ tuṅgakulodbhavām ।।
na hi tāmraśikhaṇḍānām adyāpi sphurati dhvaniḥ ।। priyasamaraparāvarodharuddhān ahataripuḥ katham āhareya dārān ।। prabhāte mām avandanta na tu vegavataḥ sutām ।। asmadāsannam āsīnāṃ bhaktyā vegavatīṃ tataḥ ।।
vandyāvandyavicāre hi paṇḍitāḥ samadarśinaḥ ।। vandyalakṣaṇayuktāṃ yo vandyām api na vandate ।। nanu mandamate lokaḥ pūjyapūjitapūjakaḥ ।। candrāsannair hi nakṣatrair lokaḥ kāryāṇi kāryate ।।
ahaṃ vegavatīvṛttaṃ tadvarṇitam avarṇayam ।। vandato muditā gatvā senābhartre nyavedayan ।। harṣadundubhivṛndais tu nadadbhir vṛtraśatrave ।। pramodadhvanite yātaṃ tanyamāne divāniśam ।।
idānīm eva devībhyāṃ devo vijñāpito yathā ।। kasyāścid api nāsmabhir dṛṣṭaḥ pariṇayotsave ।। naravāhanadattasya vivāhaḥ kāryatām iti ।। mamāpi hi manasy āsīd ayam eva manorathaḥ ।।
pitāhaṃ varapakṣe asya samastam avarodhanam ।। rumaṇvadādayaḥ pakṣe tasyā evaṃ bhavantv iti ।। nīto ahaṃ citravinyāsaratnamaṅgalamaṇḍalam ।। jyeṣṭhāmbābhavanaṃ nītā kelikolāhalākulam ।।
maṣīkālamukhoraskaḥ kārito jyeṣṭhayāmbayā ।। aryaputra khalīkāraṃ paśyatemaṃ mamedṛśam ।। kva yāsi jālma labdho asi preṣitas tvaṃ caraḥ kila ।। asyāḥ saubhāgyam utpādyam avaśyaṃ kārmaṇair mayā ।।
yayā hastatale bhartā gurudhairyo api nartitaḥ ।। kiṃ mayā preṣitaḥ kaścid bhavān iva caras tayā ।। devyāḥ niṣkramitaḥ svasmād aham antaḥpurād iti ।। tām anekaguṇāṃ prāpañ jyeṣṭhāmbāpreṣitāś carāḥ ।।
mayā vegavatīpāṇir gṛhīto mantrasaṃskṛtaḥ ।। anyādṛśaprapañceva dṛṣṭā vegavatī mayā ।। śayanaṃ ca navoḍheva sevate sma parāṅmukhī ।। vrīḍākrīḍākṛtā pīḍā durbhagā tyajyatām iti ।।
aryaputra kutaḥ krīḍā gurvājñeyaṃ garīyasī ।। duṣkarā kṣiptavelāpi vadhūkābhūmikā kṛtā ।। tasmād guruniyogo ayam alaṅghyaḥ kṣamyatām iti ।। anayaṃ kṣaṇasaṃkṣiptām āyātām api yāminīm ।।
tvarāvān skhaladālāpo mām avocat tapantakaḥ ।। bhrāmyatā nagarodyāne dainyamlānānanendavaḥ ।। anyad uccalitāḥ sthānaṃ vihāyemāṃ purīm iti ।। krodhān mānasavegena mama sakhyo vivāsitāḥ ।।
nayanonmeṣamātreṇa paśya mām āgatām iti ।। āsīnā cāsane svasmin sakhībhiḥ parivāritā ।। sadyaḥ svarbhānumuktasya tārābhartur iva prabhā ।। prītisnigdhaviśālākṣaḥ sapraṇāmam abhāṣata ।।
catasraḥ kila tiṣṭhanti bhaginyaḥ kanyakās tava ।। putrās tiṣṭhanti catvāraḥ śastraśāstrakalāvidaḥ ।। tatas tā dārikās tebhyaḥ putrebhyo me dadātv iti ।। devenānugṛhītāsmi prasādaiḥ phalitair iti ।।
ahaṃ ca varapakṣe tu tātaḥ sāntaḥpuro abhavat ।। tām adyāpi na paśyāmi prāpyāpi śriyam īdṛśam ।। agrahīṣata sasvedān ambhoruharucaḥ karān ।। rājarājagṛhāṇīva gatāḥ pitṛgṛhāṇi te ।।
yātā yasya yathā rātriḥ sa tathā varṇayatv iti ।। tathaiteṣāṃ gatā rātrir mā sma gacchad yathā punaḥ ।। avehi mantriputreti bhāryayā bhartsitaḥ spṛśan ।। dāruṇām anayad rātriṃ nidrayāpi nirākṛtaḥ ।।
śūro aham iti bhāryāyāḥ pādasthānaṃ na muktavān ।। prakṣālanād dhi paṅkasya dūrād asparśanaṃ varam ।। pragalbhā ramayiṣyanti kathaṃ vidyādharāṅganāḥ ।। bhāryayā yo atisaubhāgyād gṛhād api nirākṛtaḥ ।।
sa kathaṃ paravṛttāntaiḥ kṣapāṃ kṣapitavān iti ।। ramamāṇaḥ kṣaṇaṃ sthitvā sasuhṛt pānam ācaram ।। sabhāryāḥ suhṛdas te api tābhir eva sahāgatāḥ ।। sa tayā sā ca tenaiva pānam āsevatām iti ।।
śobhājitamṛṇālinyāṃ pānabhūmāv upāviśat ।। gṛhītas tarhi niḥśaṅkaṃ mayā hariśikhaḥ svayam ।। tapantakasya gṛhiṇīm agṛhṇān marubhūtikaḥ ।। abravīt pariśeṣo ayaṃ kim anyat kriyatām iti ।।
vayaṃ ca sahitā dāraiḥ krīḍantaḥ sukham āsmahi ।। mayānunīyamānāpi suptā vegavatī pṛthak ।। sahasā pratibuddhaś ca sphurallocanatārakaḥ ।। kenāpy apaśyam ātmānaṃ nīyamānaṃ vihāyasā ।।
ko nu mā nayatīty āsaṃ saṃdehādhīnamānasaḥ ।। tasmād vidyādhareṇāhaṃ gṛhīto duṣṭabuddhinā ।। hastapādāstramitrasya paṅgor iva mudhā vadhaḥ ।। mariṣyāmīti nirdhārya taṃ tāḍayitum udyataḥ ।।
svasyāḥ susadṛśaṃ jāteḥ karma vyavasitaṃ tvayā ।। mantrayantritavīryasya tasmāc cintaya devatām ।। tasmād dadāmi te abhīṣṭaṃ dvayor anyataraṃ varam ।। kiṃ mahāsāgarādhāraiḥ pāṭyase makarair iti ।।
arāter api niryātā bhāratī svacchakomalā ।। tato me śatrumitreṇa bhaved upakṛtaṃ mahat ।। taṃ tam eva kilāpnoti tadā tadbhāvabhāvitaḥ ।। tayānantaram evāsau sukṛtī saṃprayujyate ।।
śṛṇomi sma prabhātendoḥ paśyāmi sma tanuprabhām ।। nivārabāṇanistriṃsaprabhādalitacandrikā ।। lokān iva didhakṣantī pralayānalasaṃtatiḥ ।। krodhānalam avicchinnaiḥ sthūlaiś ca niravāpayat ।।
mūrdhni cāñjalim ādhāya lajjādīnam abhāṣata ।। yuvarājaṃ mahārāja mā vadhīr bhaginīpatim ।। svadārasahitas tasmād akṣato mucyatām iti ।। svasāram abravīd vācā siṃhaphūtkāraghorayā ।।
dhik tvāṃ śāradacandrābhamanaḥputrikapāṃsanīm ।। tāṃ ca tvāṃ ca tatas tasya gamayiṣyāmi pṛṣṭhataḥ ।। tenāpi tvaritenāham abhramadhye nipātitaḥ ।। bhagavatyāryaputro ayaṃ svaputra iva rakṣyatām ।।
śanaiḥ śanair mahīṃ yāyāt tathāyaṃ nīyatām iti ।। hantuṃ vegavatīm eva pravṛttaḥ prārthitas tayā ।। nipatanti na nistriṃśāḥ śūrāṇāṃ tvādṛśām iti ।। vajrasthambhacchidādakṣām asidhārāṃ nyapātayat ।।
apaśyaṃ yuddhasaṃnaddhāś caṇḍikāgaṇikā iva ।। rambhāsthambham ivāsāram alunād asidhārayā ।। utpannau sakalāv eva śarīraśakaladvayāt ।। tathā mānasavegau dvau prāgalbhetām itas tataḥ ।।
kṣaṇād vegavatīnāṃ ca yudhyamānaiś caturguṇaiḥ ।। proṣitāmbhasi gambhīre patitaḥ kūpasāgare ।। saṃjayasya vacaḥ kaṣṭe vartamānasya saṃkaṭe ।। patitaḥ sātyakānīke duṣkṛtī narake yathā ।।
upāyaṃ cintayann eva smarāmi sma kathām imām ।। ekataḥ pūrvajas teṣāṃ madhyamāntyau dvitatritau ।। gurave dātum icchāmaḥ kāṅkṣitāṃ dakṣiṇām iti ।। utpādyatām apatyaṃ ca kratubhiś cejyatām iti ।।
tenoktam alam etena graheṇa bhavatām iti ।। tadā kruddhena guruṇā yācitā dakṣiṇām imām ।। kumbhodhnīnāṃ sahasraṃ me datta sthāta ca mā ciram ।। jñātāḥ kila kuvereṇa kauverīṃ prasthitā diśam ।।
dattvā prasthāpitāḥ prītās tuhinādrer avātaran ।। prāptāś caṇḍeśvarāsannāś caṇḍārkakiraṇāḥ sthalīḥ ।। lobhanīyam idaṃ dravyaṃ na parityāgam arhati ।। agnipraveśaṃ kurvīta tathedaṃ naś cikīrṣitam ।।
ramaṇīyavipākaṃ ca vākyaṃ naḥ kriyatām iti ।। na hi svārtheṣu muhyanti buddhayas tvādṛśām iti ।। yad atra yuktaṃ tad brūtāṃ kim udāste bhavān iti ।। pitāpi hi viṣaṃ khādan naiva putrair upekṣyate ।।
buddhivṛddhena hi grāhyaṃ bālād api subhāṣitam ।। kāryaṃ cen mahyam ātmīyam aṃśam āryaḥ prayacchatu ।। pratijñābhāravikṣepād yāsyāmi laghutām iti ।। dugdhagardhāndhabuddhitvāt pramāpayitum icchataḥ ।।
adṛśyamānapānīyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kūparasātalam ।। teṣām anyatamaḥ pānthaḥ kūpe loṣṭum apātayat ।। babhañja sa ca saṃdehaḥ pathikānāṃ nyavartata ।। pānthair uttārayām āsa rajjubhir bhāṇḍamaṇḍalam ।।
uttāryottārya pānīyaṃ kṛtāḥ snāpitapāyitāḥ ।। kūpae eva tritaṃ tyaktvā sagoyuthau palāyitau ।। nirāśiś cintayām āsa kṣaṇam uttārakāraṇam ।। māhendrīm akarod iṣṭiṃ manasaiva mahāmanāḥ ।।
dhanuṣmantas taḍitvanto ghanā jalam apātayan ।। prataran prataran dhīraṃ golehyād utthitas tritaḥ ।। apavargam ivādrākṣīn mūrtimantaṃ tridaṇḍinam ।। na dṛṣṭāv evamākārau sagoyūthau dvijāv iti ।।
yau tvāṃ pātālagambhire kūpe bhrātaram aujjhatām ।। yāv evaṃ ninditācārau praṣṭavyau kuta eva tau ।। duṣṭamaskariṇaṃ dhik tvāṃ sādhunindāviśāradam ।। tādṛśā eva jānanti sādhavaṃ na bhavādṛśāḥ ।।
jātaṃ vikasitajyotiḥ kirīṭābharaṇaṃ śiraḥ ।। kṛtaivamādikākāraḥ sa jātaḥ sarvathā hariḥ ।। bhrātarau me sapāpau ced apāpau bhavatām iti ।। gurū me gurave gās tāḥ prītau vitaratām iti ।।
paryāptam iti tenokte prītaḥ śakro divaṃ yayau ।। tasmāt pātālagambhīrād avaṭād uttithas tritaḥ ।। yājakais tu vinā yajñaṃ kṣatriyasya virudhyate ।। iti ceti ca nirdhārya smṛtyāmitagatiṃ gataḥ ।।
kaṣṭām āpadam āpanno vidhaye māṃ smarer iti ।। na tu pratyupakārāśārujājarjaritaṃ dhṛtam ।। apaśyam aham ātmānaṃ taṃ cāmitagatiṃ puraḥ ।। yuṣmatsmaraṇapūto ayaṃ janaḥ kiṃ kurutām iti ।।
vegavatyāḥ sahāyatvam ācareti tam ādiśam ।। kartum icchati yo mohān mahāgauriṃ sa rakṣati ।। ājñāsaṃpattimātreṇa bhṛtyād bhartā hi bhidyate ।। śatror galadgalasirārudhireṇa mūrdhnā nābhyarcitaṃ madasilūnaśirodhareṇa ।।
ārohad ambaraṃ kāle mandendugrahacandrike ।। na pṛcchāmi sma panthānaṃ deśaṃ nagaram eva vā ।। aṭavīṃ siṃhamātaṅgapuṇḍarīkākulām agām ।। apaśyaṃ lohitāyantīṃ prācīm aruṇaśociṣā ।।
vivādidhvanighaṇṭānām apaśyaṃ maṇḍalaṃ gavām ।। jātāśvāsamatir gacchan kṣaṇenāraṇyam atyajam ।। apaśyaṃ dhūsaracchāyān gacchan dinakarodaye ।। ālavālaparikṣiptamūlam udyānam āsadam ।।
pṛṣṭavān asmi kasyedam udyānam iti so abravīt ।। asmadādīn abodhāndhān saṃdihann iva pṛcchati ।। krīḍanti tena devena svayaṃ vijñāyatām iti ।। praviśyāpaśyam udyānamandiraṃ tuṅgatoraṇam ।।
antare vetram ādhāya tiṣṭheti dvāry adhārayat ।। nivārayasi yo mohād enam ambaracāriṇam ।। evaṃ vā praviśan dhīraṃ dharaṇīdhīradhīr iti ।। viśantaṃ nānujānāmi kiṃ punaḥ saumyam īdṛśam ।।
praviśaty eva pāruṣyamātrasārā hi mādṛśāḥ ।। prāviśaṃ nisvanadvīnaṃ vinītāṇḍajavānaram ।। apaśyam amarākāraṃ naraṃ nāgarakeśvaram ।। kaccid vā pratyavekṣyante bahukṛtvaḥ kalā iti ।।
avakṣiptaṃ hi dṛśyāni manaḥ paśyati nekṣaṇe ।। vīṇātaś cakṣur ākṣipya mayi nikṣiptavān asau ।। mām upāveśayat prītas tasminn eva śilāsane ।। prakṣālya ca svayaṃ pādau dattārghaḥ samupāviśat ।।
bhūṣitaḥ katamac cedaṃ puraṃ saccaritair iti ।। tvādṛśāṃ devaputrāṇām ajñānaṃ tu na yujyate ।। agrato bhāvitaṃ deśaṃ nābuddhvā saṃprapadyate ।। na jñātā pathikeneti duḥśliṣṭam iva dṛśyate ।।
ajñānacchadmanā channaḥ krīḍituṃ madvidhair iti ।। dvijo ahaṃ vatsaviṣaye vasataḥ pitarau mama ।। śrutvā dārair asaṃtuṣṭo yakṣīṃ kāṃcid asādhayam ।। yad vā yad rucitaṃ tasyai tatra tatrāramāvahi ।।
pātālamantram ārādhya ramayāmy asurīm iti ।। ānīya nabhasā nyastaḥ pure asmin bhavatām iti ।। paścāt tāpagṛhītā tu na sā yusṃān vimokṣyati ।। aṅgā janapadaḥ sphītaś campā ceyaṃ mahāpurī ।।
prasiddhaḥ priyavīṇatvād vīṇādattakanāmakaḥ ।। gāḍhaṃ parikaraṃ badhnan dhāvamānaḥ sa cāgamat ।। svāmipravahaṇaṃ prāptam iti dattakam abravīt ।। dattavān dattakas tasmai śīghrapreṣaṇakāriṇe ।।
pāvanair dāsabhavanaṃ pādanikṣepaṇair iti ।। gṛhītacārusaṃcāraṃ campām abhimukho agamam ।। ciraṃjīvadbhir āścaryaṃ pṛthivyāṃ kiṃ na dṛśyate ।। kva ca kasyāpi pānthasya rajjubhāge vyavasthitaḥ ।।
yena lokottamasyāsya rajjubhāge vyavasthitaḥ ।। nanu cāsya vasanto api sārathyena vikathyate ।। hālikān halamūleṣu vīṇāvādanatatparān ।। vitantrīs tāḍayadvīṇāḥ karṇaśūlapradāyinīḥ ।।
vīṇāvayavasaṃpūrṇām apaśyaṃ śakaṭāvalīm ।। vyastapadmanidhānābhaṃ prāpnomi sma vaṇikpatham ।। vīṇāvikṣiptacetasko vīṇā me dīyatām iti ।। vaṇijo anye kim utsannāyena khādasi mām iti ।।
nikṛṣṭajanmakarmāṇaḥ saktā vīṇām avādayan ।। śātakumbhamayaiḥ kumbhair ambhogarbhaiḥ samaṅgalam ।। utthāsnur iva medhāvī viśālaṃ hṛdayaṃ śriyaḥ ।। adyārabhyāsya yuṣmābhir ājñā saṃpādyatām iti ।।
ājñāpayata yuṣmakāṃ kaḥ pākaḥ sādhyatām iti ।। brāhmaṇāś ca ghṛtakṣīraguḍādimadhurapriyāḥ ।। nanu hastapuṭagrāhyaṃ pāyasaṃ sādhyatām iti ।। annasaṃskāraśāstrajñāḥ kāṃ diśaṃ yāntu saṃprati ।।
karmakaryo api tāny asmin gṛhe prāyeṇa jānate ।। anarthakāni jātāni caritārthāni pāyase ।। ālekhyayakṣam ādāya yakṣīkāmukam āgataḥ ।। gamitaḥ preṣyatāṃ yena mādṛśo apīdṛśām iti ।।
mamāṅgaṃ gandhatailena mṛdnāti sma yathāsukham ।। kṛtvā devapraṇāmaṃ ca prāyaṃ bhojanamaṇḍapam ।। sabhrātṛbhāgineyādipaṅktimadhyae upāviśat ।। pāyasenenduvarṇena sūpakāreṇa pūritā ।।
mahāsāramusārasthe sthāpite madhusarpiṣī ।। madhumāṃsocitaḥ kvāhaṃ kva cedaṃ ghṛtapāyasam ।। vicārya pāyasagrāsaṃ dagdho asmīti nirastavān ।। śītapānīyagaṇḍūṣair mukhaṃ muhur aśītayam ।।
nāyaṃ vipraḥ kathaṃ vipraḥ pradviṣyād ghṛtapāyasam ।। niśvāso asya mayā ghrātaḥ śanakair niścarann iti ।। kampayitvottamāṅgaṃ ca taṃ bruvantaṃ nyavārayat ।। pānakasyāpi pānena goṣṭhī saṃmānyatām iti ।।
tat pītaṃ pānasādṛśyāt pānabuddhyaiva pānakam ।। sevitvāhāram agrāmyam udatiṣṭhaṃ sadattakaḥ ।। kāntam adhyāsi paryaṅkaṃ nyastaṃ tatraiva maṇḍape ।। mukhasya gandharāgau ca tāmbulenodapādayam ।।
vīnonmattir iyaṃ kasmāc campāyāṃ kathyatām iti ।। tasya gandharvadatteti sutā trailokyasundarī ।। abhiprāyeṇa kenāpi na kasmaicit prayacchati ।। tena śulkam upanyastaṃ duḥsaṃpādaṃ surair api ।।
yo anuvādayitā vīṇāṃ pariṇetā sa tām iti ।। na kaścid yo na campāyāṃ vīṇayonmattakaḥ kila ।। ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe gate māse sā tad gāyati gītakam ।। na cāpi vīṇayā kaścid anugacchati tām iti ।।
vīṇādattakam abrūtāṃ sthavirau vetradhāriṇau ।। yadi sajjā suhṛdgoṣṭhī samasyā kriyatām iti ।। kalyā gandharvadattā vā sva eva kriyatām iti ।। rūpaṃ gandharvadattāyākīdṛg ity atha so abravīt ।।
utkṛṣṭavismayavimohitamānasena rūpaṃ nirūpayitum eva mayā na śakyam ।। samākarṇyaiva karṇābhyāṃ mano nītaṃ vidheyatām ।। draṣṭuṃ gandharvadatteti tena coktaṃ na śakyate ।। yadi cecchatha tāṃ draṣṭuṃ gāndharvaṃ śikṣyatām iti ।।
gāndharvaśabdas tat tasmād asmākaṃ kāryatām iti ।। naṣṭaśrutisvarajñāno bhūtiko nāma durbhagaḥ ।। alaṃ me nāradīyena kṛtaṃ gandharvadattayā ।। anyāyāgatam aiśvaryaṃ nindanty eva hi sādhavaḥ ।।
apūjayan mayā cāsau na draṣṭum api pāritaḥ ।। vīṇādattakadattāyāṃ pīṭhikāyām upāviśat ।। bhavān asyopapannasya nāradīyaṃ karotv iti ।। na ca pārayate dātuṃ dāridryāt kākaṇīm api ।।
na cāsminn ekam apy asti yady asti pratipadyatām ।। ko yakṣīkāmukaṃ śakto daridram iti jalpitum ।। sa yakṣīkāmukaḥ kasmād daridra iti bhaṇyate ।। patite droṇamegho api na tiṣṭhati jalaṃ sthale ।।
durvyavasthitatantrīkāṃ vīṇāṃ mahyam upānayat ।। bhūtiko māṃ dhig ity uktvā vīṇādattakam uktavān ।। vīṇāgrahaṇam apy eṣa na jānāti sukhaiditaḥ ।। ālekhyavādakāḥ ke api na dṛṣṭā naṣṭadṛṣṭinā ।।
sa niṣādo niṣādaṃ me ṣaḍja ity upadiṣṭavān ।। catasraḥ pañca vā tantryaś chinnāś caḍ iti visvarāḥ ।। akṛtvā kiṃ karoty asya nāradīyaṃ bhavān iti ।। śrutivāsitakarṇatvān mṛdu vīṇām avādayam ।।
kim etad iti jalpanto mām aikṣanta savismayāḥ ।। kākatālīyam ity uktvā gata eva sadakṣiṇaḥ ।। āvasaṃ śayanāvāsaṃ mālāghūpādhivāsitam ।। bhāsvadvajraśilāpādam āseve śayanaṃ tataḥ ।।
rūpājīve śanaiḥ pādau samavāhayatāṃ mama ।। vacobhiḥ kila te cittaṃ madīyaṃ hartum aicchatām ।। rāsabhīr asitānīva virasāni svakarṇayoḥ ।। atha prasupta evāsmi nirāśe te ca jagmatuḥ ।।
dṛṣṭatattva ivāvidyāṃ nidrām atyajam utkaṭām ।। vīṇādattakavīṇāyāṃ tato dṛṣṭiṃ nyapātayam ।। vīṇā ca vādanīyā syāc cirotsṛṣṭā ca sā mayā ।। bhaktyā mātuḥ sapatnīva nisargakuṭilā hi sā ।।
jijñāse tāvad ity enāṃ vicāryāhaṃ gṛhītavān ।। vyavasthāpayituṃ tantrīḥ karaśākhabhir aspṛśam ।। samudrasena godatta dhāva dhāva sakhe drutam ।। sarasvatī bhagavatī vīṇāṃ sārayati svayam ।।
samāptasāraṇāyās tu kīdṛṅ nāma bhaviṣyati ।। netraśrotrāṇi no yānti pavitrakaratām iti ।। prāvṛtya saśiraḥpādaṃ kāyaṃ nidrāṃ kilāgamam ।। kathaṃ sarasvatī kṣudrair dṛśyate asmadvidhair iti ।।
mām anulbaṇaveṣaṃ ca vanditvā dattako abravīt ।। tad gandharvasamasyāyai yuṣmābhir api gamyatām ।। yena vo rocate gantuṃ tena prasthīyatām iti ।। ahaṃ tu pādacāreṇa gacchāmi śanakair iti ।।
prasthitaḥ pādacāreṇa sanāgarakamaṇḍalaḥ ।। yakṣīkāmukarūpo ayam anartho asmān upāgataḥ ।। āśādīrghāsu rathyāsu caraṇaiḥ saṃcarāmahe ।। apaśyaṃ veśmanāṃ mālās tasyaiva sirasām iva ।।
kokilāsubhagālāpāḥ śṛṇomi sma kulāṅganāḥ ।। yakṣīkāmukam āyātuṃ sakhyaḥ paśyata dhāvata ।। ākāśāt pātitaḥ prāpto dattakena sujanmanā ।। kruddhayā mugdhayā vāpi yayā svārtho na cetitaḥ ।।
kva yakṣīkāmikaḥ kvāyaṃ kāmaḥ kāmī rater iva ।। nayanotpalamālābhir arcyamānaś ca yātavān ।। aṅgaṃ gandharvadattāyās teṣām iva manorathāḥ ।। sphuraddivyaprabhāvāt tu na vidma kiṃmayair iti ।।
āsanānāṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiṃ mahāpaṭṭorṇaveṣṭitam ।। aho mahākhalīkāro yakṣīkāmukam āgataḥ ।। samāyātāś catuḥṣaṣṭis tāvanty evāsanāny api ।। yat satyaṃ lajjito asmīti tataś coktam ṛjur bhavān ।।
tena gandharvadattāpi sulabhā kim utāsanam ।। dattavān svayam ākṛṣya mahyam ātmīyam āsanam ।। tiṣṭhanti sma sthitā eva bhṛtakā iva bhartari ।। sa tad adhyāsta śeṣāś ca yathāsanam upāviśan ।।
gṛhād asurakanyānāṃ mahāsurapurād iva ।। tāsāṃ pratyekam ekaikā teṣāṃ pādān adhāvata ।। tayā svedajalenaiva dhautaḥ ślathaśarīrayā ।। visrastahastayā hastād bhṛṅgāraḥ pātitas tayā ।।
prāṃśuprākāragarbhasthāḥ śrutihārigiraḥ striyaḥ ।। śulkaṃ gandharvadattāyāvīṇāvādananāmakam ।। na yakṣīkāmukād anyaṃ prāpnuyād bhartṛdārikā ।। hyo yasmād bhūtikenāsya nāradīyaṃ kṛtaṃ kila ।।
ayaṃ nāsulabhībhūtaḥ śulkadoṣān na labhyate ।। anātmajño balāt ko api gale tāṃ lambayiṣyati ।। prajāpatiś ca durlagnaḥ sarvathā śivam astv iti ।। jvalanmaṇiśilāstambhāṃ viśālāṃ prāviśaṃ sabhām ।।
upatyakāsthalī meroḥ phullaiḥ kalpadrumair iva ।। nirgataḥ kañcukī prerya tiraskariṇikāmbaram ।। vijñāpayati vaḥ śreṣṭhī svāgataṃ guṇarāgiṇām ।। śātakumbhamayaiḥ pūtaṃ gaṅgāmbhaḥkalaśair iva ।।
tato gandharvadattāyai nirdeśo dīyatām iti ।। hrītāḥ sadiśam ākāśam apaśyan proṣitottarāḥ ।। samare kātarasyeva sannacakṣuḥkapolakam ।। sa yadā yātum ārabdhas tadāhūya mayoditaḥ ।।
āgacchatu kim adyāpi dṛṣṭair nāgarakair iti ।। jātam ucchvasitaṃ svinnakapolasthalapīvaram ।। yakṣīkāmuka vandyo asi sarvathā śobhitaṃ tvayā ।। avagrahe hi jīmūto visphūrjann api śobhate ।।
tādṛśaṃ yadi vijñānaṃ bhavet kiṃ na bhaved iti ।। uddāmitamukhā loke sukhaṃ jīvanti nistrapāḥ ।। madhye mahāmanuṣyāṇām evam uddāmayen mukham ।। kva ca priyaguṇā yakṣī guṇa ṛddhiḥ kva cedṛśaḥ ।।
utkaṭena hi nāmnāpi prāyas tuṣyanti ḍiṇḍikāḥ ।। ko jānāti manuṣyāṇāṃ caritaṃ gūḍhacāriṇām ।। yathā paricitaśrīkas tathā māṃ prati śobhate ।। devī gandharvadattāgād abhibhūtasabhāprabhā ।।
pravrajyām āsthitā nūnam idānīm apsarogaṇāḥ ।। candralekheva saṃdhyābhram adhyāsta caturantakam ।। bālāyāḥ śaśilekhāyāḥ puṇḍarīkākarā iva ।। paribhūtavatī goṣṭhīṃ sabhāstambhāvalīm iva ।।
śrūyatāṃ śreṣṭhino vākyaṃ bho nāgarakakuñjarāḥ ।। yo vo vādayituṃ śaktaḥ sa kiṃ tiṣṭhati ḍhaukatām ।। sā hi yuṣmākam asyāś ca lajjākhedaprayojanā ।। yuṣmān ātmānam etāṃ ca sa kleśān mocayatv iti ।।
tvaṃ naḥ pūjyaḥ pravīṇaś ca tasmād utthīyatām iti ।। saṃbhāvitatamas teṣāṃ gatvā vīṇām avādayat ।। saṃpādayati śabdo abhūd uccakaiḥ sādhu sādhv iti ।। are jñātaṃ mayedānīṃ tenaivāmī vṛthāśramāḥ ।।
tripiṣṭapaṃ tribhiḥ krāntaṃ vikramaiś cakrapāṇinā ।। krāmantaṃ gaganaṃ vegāt triś cakāra pradakṣiṇam ।। nārāyaṇastutiṃ nāma gītaṃ gītakam adbhutam ।। arjunena tatas tasmād virāṭasutayā kila ।।
iti kramāgataṃ tātas tātād āgamitaṃ mayā ।। svargān nānyatra gāndhāra ity āhur nāradādayaḥ ।। tad asaṃpādayann eva jāyate doṣavān asau ।। puro nāgarakāṇāṃ ca yathāsāmarthyam utsahe ।।
smayamāno vilakṣyatvāt svam evābhajatāsanam ।। raṅgo bhaṅgam agṛhṇāt sa nigṛhyajyeṣṭhamallavat ।। dṛṣṭvā saṃbhāvitājñānaṃ lajjayāgrāhi dattakaḥ ।। tenoktaṃ saṃkaṭāsthānād anyatra sthīyatām iti ।।
pathā sakṛt pravṛttāyāḥ kiṃ karoty avaguṇṭhanam ।। tathā gandharvadattāpi dhṛṣtam ājñāpitā mayā ।। hā kaṣṭaṃ vañcito asmīti paścāt tāpena khedyate ।। tatra nirlajjatāślāghī lajjayaiva hi lajjate ।।
aho sāhasam ity uktvā tūṣṇīṃbhāvam upeyivān ।। pārśve gandharvadattāyādattam āsanam āsthitaḥ ।। aparānīyatām ārya naitāṃ spṛśati mādṛśaḥ ।। jaḍatāṃ gamitā yena paṭutantrīparaṃparā ।।
mām ālokya tathābhūtam uktaṃ nāgarakair iti ।। yena sāhasam ārabdhaṃ svaguṇākhyāpanopamam ।। karaśākhāś ca no jātāna ca saṃbhāvanedṛśī ।। kadā vādayitā vīṇāṃ vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।।
prītim utpādayiṣyāmi tāval locanayor iti ।। tāvad gandharvadattāyārūpaṃ paśyāmy avāritaḥ ।। īdṛśī tādṛsī dṛṣṭā rūpiṇī yuvatir mayā ।। kiṃ tat satyaṃ mṛṣety etad devair vijñāyatām iti ।।
tantucakraṃ bhayodbhrāntalūtāmaṇḍalasaṃkulam ।। vepathusvedaromāñcalajjāvidhuram ākulam ।। keśadūṣitatantrīkā prathameva vivarjitā ।। kacchapākāraphalakām ādāya svayam āgataḥ ।।
gandharvadattām iva tām adadāt subhagasvanām ।। abhuktāmbarasaṃvītaṃ pīṭhapṛṣṭham adhiṣṭhitam ।। tantrībandhā yathāsthānam asaran dhaivatādikam ।। gandharvadattām avadaṃ bhīru saṃgīyatām iti ।।
tathā ca dhṛṣṭam ādiṣṭā bālāśālīnatāṃ gatā ।। tad eva gītakaṃ divyam ahaṃ mandam avādayam ।। lokaṃ pāvayituṃ puṇyā prāvartata sarasvatī ।। upary upari pāṇyantaiḥ pāṇibhir yojitaṃ mayā ।।
tadgītamātraviṣayaśrotramātrajagad tadā ।। paṭubhir dundubhidhvānair abhibhūtaṃ vimāninām ।। kañcukī cetanāprāptān abhāṣata sabhāsadaḥ ।। gītaṃ yad anayānena kiṃ tat saṃvāditaṃ na hi ।।
dharmyaśulkārjitām eṣa kanyakāṃ labhatām iti ।। bahiṣkṛtā nāgarakānāstikās tridivād iva ।। svabhyastaguṇavaiphalyaṃ guṇinaḥ kān na tāpayet ।। parīkṣya bahuśo rājñā sacivo guṇavān iva ।।
yakṣīkāmuka devas tvam amānuṣaparākramaḥ ।। kṛcchrām āpadam āpannālīlayaiva tvayoddhṛtāḥ ।। ātodyāṅgārtham utkhātāḥ prarohantu yathā purā ।। kumāryaḥ pariṇīyantāṃ prasūyantāṃ kulastriyaḥ ।।
guruvaktrābhisaṃkrāntān svasiddhāntān adhīyatām ।। sacampāmagadhāś cāṅgāḥ svasthāṅgāḥ śeratām iti ।। vīṇādattakam ālokya prāvocan nīcakaistarām ।। ślāghyo gandharvadattāyāḥ karaḥ saṃskrīyatām iti ।।
avocaṃ smitasaṃkīrṇām anāsthāmantharāṃ giram ।। pariṇetuṃ na me yuktam asavarṇām imām iti ।। yuṣmākaṃ hi savarṇeyam utkṛṣṭā vā bhaved iti ।। ayaṃ yasmād asaṃbaddham abuddhir iva bhāṣate ।।
tato mat katham utkṛṣṭā brāhmaṇī brāhmaṇād iyam ।। tathā sati kathāpy eṣā kriyamāṇā virudhyate ।। yena dharmārthaśāstrārthakṣuṇṇadhīr iva bhāṣate ।। te ca svā caiva nṛpater ity uktaṃ manunā yataḥ ।।
yasmād akhaṇḍitājñena dāpitā guruṇaiva me ।। dāpitā yena tenaiva tena tenaiva dāpitā ।। sābhilāṣā viśeṣeṇa pratyākhyānakadarthanām ।। arthitāṃ sānudāsasya tatheti samamānayam ।।
karaṃ gandharvadattāyāḥ sasaṃskāram upādade ।। tenaiva pratanūkṛtām apaharann asyāḥ krameṇa trapāṃ nirvāṇān mahatāntareṇa subhagaṃ saṃsāram ajñāsiṣam ।। yathā rativasantābhyāṃ smaraḥ sukham ayāpayam ।। sānudāso namaskṛtya vadati sma kṛtāsanaḥ ।।
yūyaṃ vijñāpitāḥ pūrvaṃ tad etad avadhīyatām ।। nāmitro nāpi madhyasthaḥ sādhor yasyābhavad bhuvi ।। bhāryā maitrīva sādhor yā śatror api hitaiṣiṇī ।। aputrān ātmanaḥ paurāḥ saputrān api menire ।।
trirātrakṣapaṇakṣamo vardhamāna ivāgataḥ ।। apṛṣṭo api yathācaṣṭa dharmān ṛṣabhabhāṣitān ।। ādideśa sphuṭadeśo bhāvinaṃ guṇinaṃ sutam ।। ādiṣṭaḥ sānunā yat tat sānudāso bhavatv iti ।।
vidyāḥ śikṣayatā nīto bālalīlānabhijñātām ।। svadārān eva savrīḍaḥ paradārān amanyata ।। pitarau suhṛdo dārāna kaścin nākulīkṛtaḥ ।। aham eva sa vo dāsaḥ sānudāsas tathāguṇaḥ ।।
sa ca mām abravīn mitra kriyatāṃ tad bravīmi yat ।। anubhūtajalakrīḍāḥ khādanti ca pibanti ca ।। sāphalyaṃ kriyatām adya rūpayauvanajanmanām ।। viphalīkṛtadharmārthāt pāpakarmā kutas tataḥ ।।
tyaktadṛṣṭasukhaḥ so api vada ko nāma paṇḍitaḥ ।। tathā hi bhīmasenasya vākyam ākarṇyatāṃ yathā ।। anāgatasukhāśā ca naiṣa buddhimatāṃ nayaḥ ।। idaṃ saṃrambhagāmbhīryaṃ śaṅkām iva karoti saḥ ।।
lābhaḥ kas tatra hānir vā rāgo ayam abhivāsitaḥ ।। tam indhayati yan mitra tatra kiṃ nāma pauruṣam ।। vairāgyavacanāmbhobhir nirvāpayati sa kṣamaḥ ।। dharmasyābhavanirbhūyāt tatphalasya sukhasya ca ।।
nekṣyate pratiṣedhāt sā katham evaṃ viḍambyate ।। viṣamūrcchāparīteva bhartur bhāryā viḍambanā ।। na yāsyāmi na dhāsyāmi dāraiḥ saha sabhām iti ।। haste sasmitam ālambya saviṣāda ivāvadat ।।
sānudāso ayam ānītaḥ sadāro dṛśyatām iti ।। pratijñākhaṇḍanamlānaṃ kathaṃ śakṣyasi vīkṣitum ।। tvayaikena pratijñāyāḥ sāphalyam upapādyatām ।। suhṛdaḥ pibataḥ paśya sadāratanayān iti ।।
tāṃ tadā dṛṣṭavān asmi sakalatrāṃ suhṛtsabhām ।। kṣiptāmbhaḥpadminīcchāyāṃ sthalīkamalinīm iva ।। kalpitaṃ dhruvako mahyam uccam āharad āsanam ।। pibataś ca madhu prītapriyākaratalārpitam ।।
gīyamānaṃ śṛṇomi sma rudantāś cālikokilāḥ ।। patitāḥ karṇikāreṣu lūnanāsā ivālinaḥ ।। asārasya hi jāyante naṭasyātyutkaṭā rasāḥ ।। utthitaḥ puruṣaḥ ko api sarasaḥ sarasas tataḥ ।।
bhoḥ puṣkaramadhu prāptaṃ mayeti ca mudāvadat ।। na puṣkaramadhu prāptaṃ tvayānartho ayam arjitaḥ ।। paramāṇupramāṇo api bindur aṃśo na jāyate ।। aparaṃ so api yāceta ratnagṛddhā hi pārthivāḥ ।।
rājann aparam apy asti tatra prāptam idaṃ yataḥ ।। abhāvam atiriktasya kenopāyena sādhayet ।। haret sarvasvam asmākaṃ tasmāt tasmai na dīyate ।। idaṃ puṣkaramadhv eṣa sānudāsaḥ pibatv iti ।।
na ca madyam iti śrutvā pītavān asmi tan madhu ।। lakṣyate na hi sādṛśyam etasya madhurādibhiḥ ।। sarvajñair api durjñānāyenāsminn ekaśo rasāḥ ।। rasite amṛtam apy asmin gacched virasatām iti ।।
bādhate māṃ pipāseti śanair dhruvakam abruvam ।। tat puropavanaṃ vegāc cakravad bhramad abhramam ।। dīnamantharam aśrauṣaṃ pramadākranditadhvanim ।। striyaṃ sākṣād ivāsīnāṃ mādhavīvanadevatām ।।
varṇyamānāpi nāsmābhiḥ kadācit pramadā śrutā ।। duḥkhasyāsya tato hetur mahyam ākhyāyatām iti ।। duḥsahasyāsya duḥkhasya nanu hetur bhavān iti ।। yadīdaṃ matkṛtaṃ duḥkhaṃ bhīru mā tvaṃ rudas tataḥ ।।
śarīrakam apīdaṃ me kvacid vyāpāryatām iti ।। anenaiva tvadīyena śarīreṇāham arthinī ।। saṃkalpajanmanānalpaṃ saṃkalpaṃ kāritā tvayi ।। śarīrasyāsya te tatra viniyogo bhavatv iti ।।
asurāntaḥpurākāraṃ prāviśaṃ bhavaneśvaram ।। sthūlodaravalīlekhāṃ śuddhasūkṣmāmbarāvṛtām ।। abravīd adhvakhinno asi putra viśramyatām iti ।। tat puṣkaramadhu svādu śīghram ānīyatām iti ।।
gṛhe puṣkaramadhv asyāduṣprāpaṃ mānuṣair iti ।। vasantakusumākīrṇaṃ prāviśaṃ vāsamandiram ।। asyai pūrvapratijñātaṃ svaśarīram upāharam ।। sāpi pratyupakārāya svaśarīraṃ nyavedayat ।।
tasya kanyāśarīrāptyā sadyaḥ pariṇataṃ phalam ।। kim idānīṃ suhṛdgoṣṭhī karītīty atha sābravīt ।। gatvā paśya suhṛdgoṣṭhīṃ madātiśayavihvalām ।। tenādṛṣṭaḥ suhṛdgoṣṭhyā viśrabdhaḥ paśyatām iti ।।
paśyāmi sma suhṛdgoṣṭhīṃ smitavyāvartitānanām ।। na dṛśyate sānudāsaḥ kva nu yāto bhaved iti ।। sānudāsena duḥsādhyā sādhitā yakṣakanyakā ।। sānudāsaḥ suhṛnmadhye vicaran puṇyavān iti ।।
bhadre katham anenoktam adṛśyo dṛśyatām iti ।। pravṛttaḥ sahasā hāsaḥ salilaugha ivolbaṇaḥ ।। mām avocad adṛśyāya yakṣībhartre namo astu te ।। drākṣāmadhu tvayā pītaṃ sādhitā ca vilāsinī ।।
suhṛdvaidyagaṇenādya kuśalena cikitsitaḥ ।। suhṛdo api kṛtasvārthāḥ sarve yāntu yathāyatham ।। jñātakāntāsavasvādo na tebhyaḥ kupito abhavam ।। vidūṣitamadhusparśāḥ pravrajanti mumukṣavaḥ ।।
na prāṇimi vinā tasmād dhiṅ nikṛṣṭaṃ ca mām iti ।। madamandam ātmabhavanāni nāgarāḥ priyayā sahāham api tanniveśanam ।। prasanno dhruvakādīnāṃ suhṛdām atyavāhayam ।। dhanarāśiḥ parikṣīṇaḥ kālena mahatā mahān ।।
duḥśravaṃ śrāvito mātrā pituḥ svargādhirohaṇam ।। samāhvāyyāvadat putra mitravarmāham eva te ।। sa hīha paraloke ca sukhāya prāṇinām iti ।। pitryaṃ śreṣṭhipadaṃ kṛtvā gṛhaṃ yāhīty abhāṣata ।।
saśokā gaṅgadattāpi sā samāśvasyatām iti ।। anya evāyam āyātaḥ kuṭumbabharadāruṇam ।। na hi vānaraśāvasya yuktā syandanadhuryatā ।। mārgam āsevatāṃ sāpi mātṛmātāmahīgatam ।।
na hi vedam adhīyānaḥ śūdraḥ sadbhiḥ praśasyate ।। itīdaṃ vacanaṃ viṣṇoḥ sāpi saṃmānayatv iti ।। na tu śokopataptāyāgaṇikāyāḥ sabhājanam ।। ayam āgata evāsi tyaja niṣṭhuratām iti ।।
doṣam utprekṣamāṇo api gata evāsmi tadgṛham ।। krandatparijanā kṛcchrāt parisaṃsthāpitā mayā ।। śarāvaṃ madirāpūrṇaṃ nyasyati sma gṛhāṅgaṇe ।। putra duḥkhavinodārthaṃ tarpaṇaṃ kriyatām iti ।।
nūnam asmān iyaṃ vṛddhā mugdhān ākṛṣṭum icchati ।। nirdākṣiṇyā ca devī śrīr iti jāto asmi śaṅkitaḥ ।। prāyaḥ samānaśīleṣu sakhyaṃ badhnanti jantavaḥ ।। dānaṃ hi tatra dātavyaṃ yatra cittaṃ prasīdati ।।
triphalāvirasāsvādaṃ pānam āsevitaṃ mayā ।। gaṇikāmātur ādeśam om iti pratyapūjayam ।। pitṛśoko api balavān avārohat tathā tathā ।। madirāmandirān madyam āharanti sma saṃtatam ।।
gāyanti sma hasanti sma kecit tatrārudann api ।। divasān gamayāmi sma surāsmaraparāyaṇaḥ ।। śvaśrūs tvām āha rūkṣo asi gātram abhyajyatāṃ tava ।। tasmād iyam api sneham aṅgeṣu nidadhātv iti ।।
skandhaḥ kaṭukatailena mrakṣitaś ca tayā mama ।। abhyaṅgaḥ kriyate tāvad bhavān avataratv iti ।। śilpinas tatra cāpaśyaṃ ratnasaṃskārakārakān ।। śreṣṭhiputra pravīṇo asi tvatto lajjāmahe vayam ।।
sarvajñānām api trāsāt prasaranti na pāṇayaḥ ।। alaṃkaraṇakarmedam āśu niṣṭhāṃ vrajatv iti ।। pañcebhyo api purebhyo aham upāyair avatāritaḥ ।। sicyase gomayāmbhobhir iti nirdhārito bahiḥ ।।
bandinaḥ paṭhataḥ ślokam uccakair uccarann iti ।। parimaṇḍalagrahapatiprabhāprabhair guṇakesarāṃśuvisaraś ca rājase ।। raṇḍāputrasya yasyaite śrūyante bandibhir guṇāḥ ।। veśanārīgrahasthena svayaṃ khyāpayatā guṇān ।।
svagṛhābhimukhaṃ prāyāṃ pauradhikkārakāritaḥ ।। sa evāmīlayad dṛṣṭiṃ hā kiṃ dṛṣṭam iti bruvan ।। tatra gomayapānīyaṃ pātayanti sma nāgarāḥ ।। apūrvapuruṣākrāntaṃ svagṛhadvāram āgamam ।।
tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti ruṣṭena dvārapālena vāritaḥ ।। bhadra sarvaṃ na jānāmi tat tvam ākhyāyatām iti ।। tiṣṭhaddauvārikadvāram aśaṅkaḥ praviśer iti ।। tenoktaṃ kaccid āyuṣmān sānudāso bhavān iti ।।
lajjamānaḥ sthitas tūṣṇīm atha tenoditaṃ punaḥ ।। spṛhayaty anapatyābhyo yā strībhyaḥ putravaty api ।। saṃhatāv api dharmārthāv ucchinnau svakulocitau ।। saha pautreṇa vadhvā ca kutrāpy anyatra tiṣṭhati ।।
āste mitravatī yatra tad ayaṃ pṛcchyatām iti ।। hā kaṣṭam iti kṛtvoccair duḥkhaskhalitam abravīt ।। daridravāṭake tāta jananī tava tiṣṭhati ।। caṇḍālavāṭakādūraṃ dakṣiṇenety abhāṣata ।।
daridrān dṛṣṭavān asmi kṣayakṣīṇān mṛtākṛtīn ।। dṛṣṭavān asmi bahubhir bālakaiḥ parivāritam ।। dadāti sma tatas tebhyaḥ svāḥ sa kulmāṣapiṇḍikāḥ ।। kulmāṣapiṇḍikāṃ hṛtvā kṣudhitatvād abhakṣayat ।।
agacchat kuṭikām ekāṃ saṃkārasthagitājirām ।। anantapaṭalacchidrapraviṣṭātapacandrikām ।। dāsyā ca pratyabhijñāya mitravatyai niveditam ।। gāḍhanidrāprasupteva nākampata na cāśvasīt ।।
anuṣṇāśītasaṃsparśair mām asnāpayad aśrubhiḥ ।। alaṃ vā vistaraṃ kṛtvā mūrtām iva daridratām ।। tadduṣṭaceṭikādattam ādarāt svayam ambayā ।। ānītoṣṇodakaṃ dātum ālukā paragehataḥ ।।
athāsyāḥ svāminī caṇḍam ākrandat taḍitodarī ।। śūnyam adya jagajjātam adya mātā mṛtā mama ।। tena tvām anuśocāmi dvitīyāṃ jananīm iva ।। śāṭakaṃ pāṭayitvāham ardhaṃ tasyai vitīrṇavān ।।
kāñjikavyañjanaṃ kṛcchrād bhuñje kodravaudanam ।। śrūyamāṇam api hy etad duḥkhāyaiva bhavādṛśām ।। jātadurvāravairāgyaḥ prātar mātaram abravam ।। gṛham mayā praveṣṭavyaṃ na praveṣṭavyam anyathā ।।
duḥkhakarmavinodena gamayer divasān iti ।। jīvayāmi sukhāsīnaṃ karmabhir garhitair iti ।। yaḥ śaktaḥ puruṣas tasya ślāghyam ekasya jīvitam ।। nanu tātasya dārāḥ stha sumerugurucetasaḥ ।।
daridravāṭakād ghorān nirayāṃ nirayād iva ।। tāmraliptīṃ vraje putra yatrāste mātulas tava ।। tyājyās tu nijaśatrutvāt prājñena pitṛbāndhavāḥ ।। sā nivṛttā pravṛtto ahaṃ pathā prāgdeśagāminā ।।
skandhāsaktajaraccarmasthagikāpacanālikān ।। karuṇāgocarībhūtam abhāṣanta parasparam ।। kva sādhuḥ sānudāso ayaṃ kveyam etādṛśī daśā ।। avipannaguṇānāṃ hi kiṃ vipannaṃ mahātmanām ।।
etasmād asahāyatvān mā sma śaṅkāṃ karor iti ।। agacchan kaṃcid adhvānam acetitapathaklamam ।। sarvopari sthite bhānau saṃprāpaṃ sumahatsaraḥ ।। tat kodravānnam asnehalavaṇaṃ bhuktavān aham ।।
sānudāsā kva yāsīti vyāharan māṃ sasaṃbhramāḥ ।। dhik pramādahatān asmān bhavatā chalitā vayam ।। bhavatā ca na saṃbhuktam etad asmād anarthakam ।। anyathāsmābhir apy adya sthātavyaṃ kṣudhitair iti ।।
sāyāhne prasthito grāmam agacchaṃ siddhakacchapam ।। praṇipatyābravīd ehi svagṛhaṃ gamyatām iti ।। svayaṃ prakṣālayat pādau vārito api kuṭumbikaḥ ।। dhāturaktam adāt sthūlaṃ prakṣālaṃ paṭaśāṭakam ।।
śayanīye niṣaṇṇaṃ mām avocat sa kuṭumbikaḥ ।। bhānoḥ svarbhānunā grāsaḥ kasya nekṣaṇagocaraḥ ।। sahasrāṇi samṛddhāni mādṛśām anujīvinām ।। tena tvadīyam evedaṃ yat kiṃcid draviṇaṃ mama ।।
bahusattvopakāriṇyaḥ śākhā iva vanaspateḥ ।। tāmraliptīṃ prayātāsi tāvad viśramyatām iti ।। prātiṣṭhe saha sārthena tena siddharthakena ca ।। śṛṇomi sma pracaṇḍānāṃ ḍiṇḍikānāṃ vikatthitām ।।
khaṇḍacarmeti me nāma muṇḍāḥ pāśupatā vayam ।। na nayeyaṃ yadi svargaṃ gaccheyaṃ nirayaṃ tataḥ ।। pratyagrais tarpayiṣyāmo mahiṣacchāgaśoṇitaiḥ ।। āvasāma kṛtāpuṇyāś caṇḍāṃ vaitaraṇīm iva ।।
kālarātrir ivāsahyā pulindapṛtanāpatat ।। apākrāman parityaktaśastralajjāyaśodhanāḥ ।। saṃbhramabhrāntadigbhāgaḥ kāndiśīkaḥ palāyitaḥ ।। gahanāntaṃ dināntena vanāntagrāmam āsadam ।।
iti roditum ārabdhā vṛddhatāghargharadhvaniḥ ।। vṛddhāṃ duḥkhitakām asvāṃ tyaktvā deśāntaraṃ gataḥ ।। tat prayāgagatenāpi na pāpam apacīyate ।। mām ārādhayamānena svagṛhe sthīyatām iti ।।
manye mūrtimatī kāpi vipattir iyam āgatā ।। saṃtatāḥ saṃnidhīyante prājñānām iva saṃpadaḥ ।। putra svaputrasādṛśyāt tvaṃ mayetthaṃ kadarthitaḥ ।। tatrākarod akhedaṃ māṃ aṅgābhyaṅgāśanādibhiḥ ।।
campāyāṃ sānudāsasya gṛham amba vrajer iti ।। tāmraliptīṃ vrajāmi sma paribhūtāmarāvatīm ।। yaṃ yam eva sma pṛcchāmi sa sa evaivam abravīt ।। durvidagdhajanālāpo grāmyanāgarako bhavān ।।
ācaṣṭe sma tadā khinnaḥ sann upāviśam āpaṇe ।। udvigna iva vicchāyaḥ kiṃ nimittaṃ bhavān iti ।। udvegasya nimittaṃ tat tenāpi hasitoditam ।। gṛhaṃ hi gaṅgadattasya na pṛcchanti yathāsthitāḥ ।।
na sa jānāti dhūrto vā gaṅgadattasya mandiram ।। pravṛddhāṃś ca viśuddhāmśu gaṅgadattasya tad gṛham ।। gaṅgadattagṛhadvāram anayat prītayācakam ।। antaḥkakṣāntarasthāya mātulāya nyavedayat ।।
athāntastāragambhīraḥ pravṛttaḥ kranditadhvaniḥ ।। gaṅgāyāṃ gaṅgadattena pitre dattaṃ jalaṃ mama ।। kālastokaṃ nayāmi sma viṣabhinnam ivāmṛtam ।। bhāgineyārthaye yat tvāṃ tad anuṣṭhātum arhasi ।।
guṇadraviṇarāśes tad utpannaṃ mitravarmaṇaḥ ।। draṣṭuṃ tvadvirahamlānāṃ mātaraṃ parigamyatām ।। akṣayaprabhavo hy asyāgaṅgāyā himavān iva ।। vijñātasāṅgavedārthaḥ kaḥ paṭhen mātṛkām iti ।।
sāre arthe dṛḍhanirbandhaṃ mā māṃ vyāhata mātula ।। svayam eva pravṛttas tair nivartyeta kathaṃ tataḥ ।। etat sahastapādāya mādṛśe nopadiśyate ।। nanu mātulamātraiva klībasattvaḥ sa jīvyate ।।
āptair akārayad bhṛtyaiś cakṣūrakṣitam ādṛtaiḥ ।। iti lokād idaṃ śrutvā palāynaparo abhavam ।। adṛṣṭaḥ kenacid gatvā vinayenābhyavādayam ।। tṛṣṇādāsīvidheyā hi kiṃ na kurvanti pātakam ।।
sarvaratnaparīkṣādikalākulaviśāradaḥ ।। tvādṛṅnātho hy anatho api mukhyo nāthavatām iti ।। śraddadhāti sma duḥsādhyāṃ mayi sarvajñatām api ।। adhunā bhavatā tāta tataḥ prasthīyatām iti ।।
praśaste tithinakṣatre bohittham amucad vaṇik ।। mahārṇavanabhastalaṃ lavaṇasindhunauchadmanā viyatpatharathena tena vaṇijas tataḥ prasthitāḥ ।। locanonmeṣamātrena yojanānāṃ śataṃ gatam ।। viśīrṇabandhanaḥ potaḥ paṭṭaśaḥ sphutati sma saḥ ।।
daivāt phalakam ālambya prāpaṃ toyanidhes taṭam ।। udbhrāntodbhrāntadikkatvād bhrāntavān sindhurodhasi ।। yatrākrāntāḥ saritvantaḥ śailopāntāḥ samantataḥ ।। āraṇyakair araṇyānyo bhajyante yatra kuñjaraiḥ ।।
śilāpihitapūrvāṅgīm aṅganām asmi dṛṣṭavān ।। ṛjutānirvikāratvān mām asau trastam aikṣata ।। na hi rūpaṃ mayā dṛṣṭaṃ nāryāḥ kasyāścid īdṛśam ।। mām ihaikākinaṃ dṛṣṭvā prāptā naktaṃcarāṅganā ।।
randhreṣu praharantīti yat tan mām idam āgatam ।। prasthitaś cintayitvā ca sā ca mām ity abhāṣata ।। bohitthavyasanabhraṣṭāṃ viddhi māṃ mānuṣīm iti ।। trātārau jagato vande pārvatīparameśvarau ।।
nirnimeṣā yato yac ca paricittajñamānasā ।। niścityeti parāvṛtya bibhyantīm idam abravam ।। nirgatyātmānam ācakṣva divyā cet pāhi mām iti ।। śilānuṣṭhitavastrārdhe pūrvakāye nyapātayat ।।
nanu mānuṣayoṣaiva varāky eṣā nirambarā ।। idaṃ vassveti tām uktvā tasyai tasyārdham akṣipam ।। tataḥ svajaghanasphītām adhyaśeta śilām asau ।। bhadre kasyāsi kā veti tām apṛccham avāṅmukhaḥ ।।
labdhabandhur ivāraṇye viśrabdhārabdha bhāṣitum ।। rājarājagṛhākāragṛhe rājagṛhe pure ।। yā prakṛṣṭe api saubhāgye patiṃ devam ivārcati ।। jyeṣṭhaḥ samudradinnaś ca tatsanāmā ca kanyakā ।।
sutāya sānudāsāya sā ca pitrā pratiśrutā ।। sakalaṃ ca kalājālaṃ vedeti jagati śrutiḥ ।। ko hi nāma kalāśālī karma tādṛśam ācaret ।। samabrāhmaṇacaṇḍālaiś cauraiḥ sārthavadhe hataḥ ।।
sāgarasya kuṭumbaṃ tat prasthitaṃ yavanīṃ prati ।। medinīmaṇḍaladhvaṃse jantūnām iva maṇḍalam ।। na tasyai nirdayenāpi sindhunā dattam antaram ।। sāgareṇa nirastā ca mandabhāgyāham eva sā ।।
iti cintāvinodāham ihāse priyajīvitā ।। prajñātaiḥ phalamūlaiś ca puṣṇāmi viphalāṃ tanum ।। mauktikasya guhākoṇe rāśiḥ prāṃśur mayā kṛtaḥ ।। iti pṛṣṭasya me cittam iti cittam abhūt tayā ।।
anyad eva kim apy eṣā mayi saṃbhāvayiṣyati ।। vipanmagnām upekṣeyaṃ puruṣaḥ san striyam satīm ।। pitrā ceyaṃ pratijñātā tena vyarthā vicāraṇā ।। mitravarmeti yaḥ svastho yaśasādyāpi tiṣṭhati ।।
sa tābhyām ekaputratvāj jñāpitaḥ sakalāḥ kalāḥ ।। suhṛdbhir dhūrtacittajñair dāsyā saṃgamitaḥ saha ।। sātha mānarthakaṃ jñātvā nirvāsayitum aihata ।। kiṃcit pṛcchāmi yat tan me yūyam ākhyātum arhatha ।।
prāsādāgre yad uktāḥ stha dāsyā tat kathyatām iti ।। abhyaṅgaḥ kriyate tasmād bhavān avataratv iti ।। kim uktāḥ śilpibhir yūyam iti pratyabruvaṃ tataḥ ।। tasmād asmāt purāt ṣaṣṭhat pañcamaṃ gamyatām iti ।।
sārthadhvaṃsāvasānāntaṃ pratyuktaṃ sakalaṃ mayā ।। mām āliṅgad apāṅgena sānaṅgābhyaṅgacāruṇā ।। sātha prasārayat svinnaṃ sphurantaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ karam ।। nṛtyatsu sphuṭaraṭiteṣu nīlakaṇṭheṣv ālambe karam ibhatālutāmram asyāḥ ।।
sarvam ekapade naṣṭaṃ sādhāv apakṛtaṃ yathā ।। cintitāṃs tān hasāmi sma pratyutpannamahāsukhaḥ ।। nārikelādibhiś cāṅgam apuṣāvopabṛmhibhiḥ ।। rājahaṃsāv ivotkaṇṭhau prītau samacarāvahi ।।
saphaladrumasaṃnāhaiḥ kareṇukalabhāv iva ।। nityam aṅgam anaṅgāṅgaiḥ samaskurva sacandanaiḥ ।। devam ātmabhuvaṃ dhyāntau jātau svaḥ kāmayoginau ।। bhinnapotavaṇigvṛttam aryaputra samācara ।।
jvalano jyālyatāṃ rātrau tuṅge sāgararodhasi ।। svadeśam ānayed āvāṃ dharmo ayaṃ vaṇijām iti ।। āptānām upadeśo hi pramāṇaṃ yoṣitām api ।। madgupaṅktir ivāgacchad upanaukāruṇodaye ।।
prāgvātālīm ivāmbhodaḥ prātiṣṭhaṃ dūram antaram ।। kātarāṇām iva vrāte sthirasattvam avasthitam ।। kailāsae iva śubhāgraṃ mahāpadmamahānidhim ।। bāṣpavaddṛṣṭikaṇṭhena bhāṣitaṃ praskhaladgirā ।।
kiṃ tvayā tāta pṛṣṭena mitravarmasuto bhavān ।। vistareṇa mayā tasmai sarvapūrvaṃ niveditam ।। ātmā sāgaradattaś ca mitravarmā ca me yataḥ ।। bahunāvikayā nāvā taṭād ānīyatām iha ।।
avagrahahṛtāmbhaskaṃ taḍāgam iva riktakam ।। naṣṭāśvadagdharathavad yogaḥ ślāghyo ayam āvayoḥ ।। pūrvaṃ saṃmantritārghas tvaṃ dharmo ayaṃ vaṇijām iti ।। samudradinnayā pādau vāṇijasya ca vanditau ।।
tena dattāni vadatā vadhūs tvaṃ me suteti ca ।। preritaṃ yānapātraṃ ca tad vipannaṃ ca pūrvavat ।। nigṛhītāḥ śikhāmadhye muktāḥ katipayā mayā ।। bhagavatyaḥ sadā bhaktam upatiṣṭhata mām iti ।।
paṭṭaśliṣṭā mayā dṛṣṭā saṃnikṛṣṭāgatā priyā ।। capalena taraṃgeṇa balād apahṛtābalā ।। cetaye yāvad ātmānaṃ loṭantam udadhes taṭe ।। prakrāman vilapāmi sma nirjane niravagrahaḥ ।।
kālākālavidāśūnyaṃ cetanāṃ dhig acetanām ।। sādho sādhvī vipadbandhuḥ priyā me mucyatām iti ।। siraḥ kaṇḍūyamānena tāḥ spṛṣṭāḥ pāṇinā mayā ।। tat kiṃ parīkṣitaṃ tāsāṃ yā na dṛṣṭāḥ parīkṣakaiḥ ।।
yad etad draviṇaṃ nāma prāṇā hy ete bahiścarāḥ ।। velākulena yāmi sma dhīradhīr draviṇoṣmaṇā ।। nārikelajalocchinnapipāsāvedanaḥ kvacit ।। panasakramūkārāmair nītadṛk phalabandhuraiḥ ।।
kvacic campakaṣaṇḍeṣu gamayan gamanaśramam ।। dhāvaddhenudhanoddhūtadhūlīkaṃ grāmam āsadam ।। dhanninuṃ colliditi ca bravīti sma hasan sa saḥ ।। jāmāteva cirāt prāptaḥ priyaḥ prītyāsmi satkṛtaḥ ।।
deśo ayaṃ katamaḥ sādho katamad vātra pattanam ।। mahāpadmanidhiprāptiramyaṃ yatrārthidarśanam ।। viśramya rajanīm atra prātar gantāsi tām iti ।। saṃkṣiptā ca nirastā ca yāpitā yāminī mayā ।।
pānthasaṃhātasaṃbādham apaśyaṃ sattramaṇḍapam ।। abhyaṅgocchādanācchādabhojanādyaiś ca satkṛtān ।। pṛṣṭo asmi sattrapatinā śayyāsthaḥ śarvarīmukhe ।। sānudāsa iti prāṃśuḥ śyāmas tāmrāntalocanaḥ ।।
kasya vā sānudāso asāv iti tenoditaṃ tataḥ ।। guṇavān bhāgineyo asau gataḥ potena sāgaram ।। praviśīrṇaḥ payaḥpūrṇaḥ payodhara ivāmbare ।। krūrāśīviṣayoṣeva gaṅgaddattam amūrchayat ।।
pravartitāni sattrāṇi velātaṭapureṣu ca ।। pānthaḥ kaścit kvacit satre pravṛttiṃ kathayed iti ।। ācakṣva nas tato dīnājanatā jīvyatām iti ।। asmai yad aham ātmānam ācakṣe apahatatrapaḥ ।।
sānudāsaḥ punaḥ potam āruhya gatavān iti ।। prāyaṃ pūritasarvecchāṃ cintāmaṇiśilām iva ।। agastyapītapānīyasāgarākāram āpaṇam ।। tasya caiktaraḥ kretā vikretānyataras tayoḥ ।।
ucitaṃ bhūṣaṇasyāsya mūlyam ākhyāyatām iti ।। tau māṃ niścalayā dṛṣṭyā dṛṣṭavantam apṛcchatām ।। manyāvahe vijānāti mūlyam asya bhavān iti ।। naivedam atidurjñānaṃ kiṃ mudhevākulau yuvām ।।
tasmād adhikam ūnaṃ vā kretṛvikrāyakecchayā ।। yadīyaṃ mūlyam etasya dhanaṃ dhanyās tato vayam ।। sadaiva me manasy āsīd ayam eva manorathaḥ ।। api nāma labheyāham idaṃ koṭyeti cetasi ।।
ko hi mānuṣadurbodham idaṃ budhyate mānuṣaḥ ।। dravyasyāsya parīkṣārthaṃ parikrāntā samantataḥ ।। ajānan kākinīty anyo na kiṃcid iti cāparaḥ ।। etad ekārthayor āsīd abhīṣṭam ubhayor api ।।
ayutaṃ me suvarṇānāṃ sasārābharaṇāmbaram ।। parīkṣito asmi ratnāni varjitāni parīkṣakaiḥ ।। viśālaṃ bahuśālaṃ ca prītaḥ prādāt sa me gṛham ।। dharmeṇaiva ca māṃ kaścin na parīkṣām akārayat ।।
kena nāmālpamūlyena mahālābho bhaved iti ।। tasya kailāsakūṭābhān sapta kūṭān akārayam ।। pradīpaśikhayā kūṭāgamitā bhasmakūṭatām ।। prakṣipyate sa tatraiva sakuṭumbo raṭann iti ।।
udīcīṃ diśam uddiśya kāndiśīkaḥ palāyitaḥ ।। durgād utkramya supto ahaṃ vaṭamule mahāśramaḥ ।। janatādhvanim aśrauṣam abhito vaṭam utkaṭam ।। jvalati jvalane kṣipto nirghṛnair draviḍair iti ।।
adrākṣaṃ pathikākalpāñ jalpato gauḍabhāṣayā ।। rakṣomukto hi nāśvasyāt ko vā dṛṣṭvā narān naraḥ ।। parito mām upāsīnāḥ samapṛcchanta viśramāḥ ।। mayāpi kathitaṃ tebhyaḥ pāṇḍyadeśapurād iti ।।
sānudāso vaṇigdṛṣṭas tato naḥ kathyatām iti ।। bhavantaḥ katamat tatra pṛcchantīty ucyatām iti ।। gaṅgadatto guṇān yasya na na veda bhavān api ।। vyāpinyā kīrtitān kīrtyā na jātās te atha vā mṛtāḥ ।।
adhyāste pāṇḍyamathurāṃ kṛtakarpāsasaṃgrahaḥ ।। āhūyāha sma suhṛdaḥ prītāṃś ca paricārakān ।। tān ahaṃ suhṛdaḥ sphītais toṣayāmi dhanair iti ।। yadi cāsau tvayā dṛṣṭas tad ācaṣṭāṃ bhavān iti ।।
na tv apūrṇapratijñena mātur ānanam īkṣitum ।। karpāse jvalati kṣiptaḥ pāṇḍyair niṣkaruṇair iti ।। iti saṃmantrayante sma viṣādakṣāmavācakāḥ ।। tasmai tanmṛtyuvṛttāntaṃ kathaṃ śakṣyatha śaṃsitum ।।
campāyāṃ tāmraliptyāṃ ca jīvitavyaṃ na kenacit ।। gaṅgadatto api tadvārttām anyato labhatām iti ।। stuvanto devatāḥ svāḥ svāḥ paryakrāman pradakṣiṇam ।। sotsāhair api durlaṅghyaṃ jālaṃ jālmaiḥ prasāritam ।।
sānudāsaḥ sa evāhaṃ vidheyo bhavatām iti ।। asmatsaṃprāptiharṣeṇa jātāḥ kaṇṭhopakaṇṭhagāḥ ।। harṣārdrāḥ samakūrdanta tālakṣobhitakānanāḥ ।। bahukṛtvaḥ parikramya mām avandata mūrdhibhiḥ ।।
nidhilābhād iva prītās tāmraliptīm aneṣata ।। hṛṣṭaḥ pratyudagacchan māṃ mātulaḥ sphītaḍambaraḥ ।। samāsena tavākhyāmi vākkuṇṭhānām ayaṃ vidhiḥ ।। sindūrapāṭalitakhaṇḍanaṭair naṭadbhir nagnāṭakair api narendrapatheṣu gītam ।।
madhurair upapannaiś ca vacanair ity abodhayat ।। ātmanāyāsiteneti prāg abhūs tvam upekṣakaḥ ।। avaśyabharaṇīyaiś ca rakṣyaiś ca paravān bhavān ।। asārathāv iva rathe dhruvaṃ yan na bravīmi tat ।।
svakuṭumbam anukaṇṭhaṃ kuru yāhi gṛhān iti ।। suvarṇabhūmaye yāntam anantaiḥ saha vāṇijaiḥ ।। taṭe bohittham ujjhitvā prātiṣṭhāmahi rodhasā ।। āvasāma nagendrasya lohitāyati bhāsvati ।।
ity asmān anuśāsti sma sārthavāhaḥ kṣapākṣaye ।। grīvāsu tailakutupān samāsajata vāṇijāḥ ।। hastair vetralatā gāḍham ālambyārohatācalam ।। pramīto himavaty asmin sa prayāti parāṃ gatim ।।
suvarṇāśāpravṛttānāṃ mahān iva vināyakaḥ ।। hemagardhagrahagrastais tathaiva tad anuṣṭhitam ।। kṣuraprakṣuritajyākaḥ kṣoṇīṃ śūra ivāgamat ।। nirupya ca jalaṃ tasmai tatraivāneṣmahi kṣapām ।।
gavāśvājaiḍakākārapāṣāṇakulasaṃkulām ।। mā mā spṛkṣata vāry etad bho bho tiṣṭhata tiṣṭhata ।। atha vā svayam evaināṃ suhṛdaḥ kiṃ na paśyatha ।। arvākkūlaṃ nudaty enān paṭuḥ parataṭānilaḥ ।।
eṣām anyatamaṃ gāḍhaṃ gṛhṇīdhvaṃ maskaraṃ karaiḥ ।। parasminn āpagapāre śanakair avarohata ।। sa tataḥ patito gacchec chailasthiraśarīratām ।। kuśalaiḥ kuśalenāśu nirviṣādaiś ca laṅghyate ।।
praviveśāvicāryaiva tathāsmabhis tad īhitam ।। śilābhūtāṃ tanuṃ tyaktvā gatiṃ māheśvarīm agāt ।। tasmai salilam anyasya amadāma nyavasāma ca ।। bhujaṃgasyātisaṃkṣiptām adrākṣaṃ padavīṃ tataḥ ।।
andhāndhakārasaṃghātavitrāsitatamonudam ।। ārdraśuṣkair araṇyānī sadhūmā kriyatām iyam ।। chāgān vikretum āyānti kirātāḥ parito diśaḥ ।। khaṇḍataṇḍulasindūralavaṇasnehanair api ।।
atigāhata cādhvānaṃ kālabhrūdaṇḍabhaṅguram ।। anenaiva nivarteran pathā pānthāḥ kadācana ।। rasātalaṃ praveṣṭavyaṃ sasuvarṇamanorathaiḥ ।। chāgapaṅkter avasthānaṃ na nivartitum antaram ।।
anubhūtasamīkena paṅkteḥ prasthīyatāṃ puraḥ ।। na parābhāvyate yāvad apareṇa pareṇa saḥ ।। dṛśyamāno viśeṣeṇa bhṛguḥ pātārthinām iva ।। āgacchan mlecchapṛtanā chāgapūgapuraḥsarā ।।
snātvāvandanta kradantaḥ pānthāḥ śaṃkarakeśavau ।। raṃhasiny api niṣkampā nivāte naur ivāmbhasi ।। āceraś cābhavat ṣaṣṭhaḥ pṛṣṭhato anantaro mama ।। vaṃśānāṃ tāḍyamānānāṃ puraḥ ṣṭhā ṣṭhoditasvanaḥ ।।
majjatāṃ dhvāntajambāle me me hā heti ca dhvaniḥ ।। ekaśeṣāsmadīyā yā saptamapramukhā sthitā ।। ekakaḥ puruṣaś cāyaṃ paraḥ svar nīyatām iti ।। hatasvapānthasārthatvād anātho mām anāthata ।।
śākhācchedena nocchedam atyantaṃ kartum arhasi ।। andhayaṣṭhis tayos tasmād bhrātar māṃ mā vadhīr iti ।। dhig dhig eva suvarṇaṃ tat prāpyaṃ prāṇivadhena yat ।। prāṇā yasyopayujyante pitror duścakṣuṣor iti ।।
ambūkṛtam acovan māṃ vācā niṣṭhuramandayā ।। kva kṛpāṇocitaḥ kālaḥ kva kṛpā kṛpaṇocitā ।। ekasya kṣudrakasyārthe yaḥ ṣoḍaśa jighāṃsati ।। ahate tu sahānena bhavatā ca hatā vayam ।।
ātmā tu satataṃ rakṣyo dārair api dhanair api ।। sa pārtham iva māṃ viṣṇuḥ karma krūram akārayat ।। caraṇeṣu paracchāgaṃ sukumāram atāḍayam ।। pānthasāṃyātriko magnaḥ sahaiva dhanatṛṣṇayā ।।
bhāratād iva saṃgrāmāt saptaśeṣā hatodyamāḥ ।। aśrumiśrāṃ pramītebhyaḥ prādāma salilāñjalim ।। śarīravedanā nāsti dehināṃ hi kṣudhāsamā ।। mandanidrākulākṣān naḥ prabodhyāha sma nāyakaḥ ।।
sīvyantām ajinair bhastrās teṣāṃ viparivartitaiḥ ।। yathā tāsām asṛkklinnaṃ yad antas tad bahir bhavet ।। hemabhūmer imāṃ bhūmim āgacchanti vihaṃgamāḥ ।। suvarṇabhūmaye yānti tat tat saṃpādyatām iti ।।
tyajyatāṃ tat suvarṇaṃ yac chinatti śravaṇe iti ।। tāritaś chāganāgena hanyāṃ taṃ nirghṛṇaḥ katham ।। yena tenaiva dattebhyas tebhyo hanyāṃ suhṛttamam ।। ayaṃ tu sānudāsīyaḥ sudūre mucyatām iti ।।
daṇḍālambitakṛttiś ca pratāgatyedam uktavān ।। tadīyaṃ cedam ānītam ajinaṃ dṛśyatām iti ।। uktaṃ nāsau tvayā muktaḥ prāṇair muktaḥ priyair iti ।। yuktihīnaṃ tad asmābhir nabhogamanam iṅgitam ।।
śāradair iva jīmūtaiḥ sāśam ākāśam āvṛtam ।। śakraśastraśikhākṛttapattracakra ivābhavat ।। ākrāman sapta saptāpi garutmanta ivoragān ।। niraṃśatvān nirāṃśaso mām evācchetum aihata ।।
yathāmbaracaratrāsi daśakaṇṭhajaṭāyuṣoḥ ।। kaccic ca skhalitas tasyāḥ khastaḥ śaṃkaram asmaram ।। kuṭṭitaṃ tat tayoś carma jātaṃ titaujarjaram ।। patitaḥ sarasi kvāpi śobhāvismitamānase ।।
snātas tarpitadevaś ca paścād amṛtam āharam ।। apūrvabahuvṛttāntaṃ dṛṣṭavān asmi tad vanam ।। asipattravanāpetaḥ saṃcarann iva nandane ।। apuṣpaḥ phalahīno vā yatraiko api na pādapaḥ ।।
bhṛṅgānīkaiḥ sadā yatra kṛṣṇakalmāṣapallavāḥ ।। śaśorṇasukumāraiś ca tṛṇair bhūṣitabhūtalam ।। vratayanti dayāvantaḥ parṇapuṣpajalānilān ।। kasyāpi caraṇaiḥ kṣuṇṇām adrākṣaṃ padavīm iva ।।
vāmanobhayarodhaskām agambhīrāmbhasaṃ nadīm ।। uttīryācarya ca snānam ārciṣaṃ devatāgurūn ।। tapaḥkānanam adrākṣaṃ baddhaparyaṅkavānaram ।। ājyāhutistimitanīrasadāruyoni kuṇḍodarāhitam ivāhavanīyam agnim ।।
sāntasaṃtāpakasparśam uṣṇāṃśum iva haimanam ।। kuśalaṃ sānudāsāya śreṣṭhine bhavatām iti ।। sarvaṃ paśyati yenārthaṃ māṃsacakṣur agocaram ।। tat kīrtitam anenādya na kadācid api śrutam ।।
vrīḍāmantharam āha sma smitveti munipuṃgavaḥ ।। nāmamātrakathā nāticitraṃ hi tapasaḥ phalam ।। yathā vadhukayodyāne saṃgato gaṅgadattayā ।। vimuktas tvam iha prāptaḥ sarvaṃ tad viditaṃ mama ।।
laṅghitāś ca sudurlaṅghyāḥ śailakāntāranimnagāḥ ।। mitravaty eva tat sarvaṃ mātā te kathayiṣyati ।। tac ca saṃprāptadeśīyam ato mā viṣadad bhavān ।। suprāpaṃ prājñasotsāhaiḥ suvarṇaṃ kva gamiṣyati ।।
ahaḥkatipayāny asminn āśrame sthīyatām iti ।। vāneyam āharann annaṃ kṛṣṭapacyam ahaṃ dviṣan ।। tuṅgaparyaṅkam adveṣaṃ gaṅgadattāniveśanam ।। daridravāṭakasthāyāḥ satataṃ mātur adhyagām ।।
suvarṇaprāptaye prāptā yā vipat saṃpad eva sā ।। mūrtaṃ puṇyam ivādrākṣaṃ vimānaṃ merubhāsvaram ।। sendracāpād ivāmbhodāt krāntāt saudāmanīlatā ।। vihāyastalam ākrāmann indor iva marīcayaḥ ।।
pramodagadgadālāpaḥ pramṛṣṭākṣīm abhāṣata ।। asmān api tiraskṛtya śraddhayārādhyatām iti ।। vandyamāno mahāgauryā krīḍayā pramatho yathā ।। śrūyatām iti bhāṣitvā tayor vṛttam avartayat ।।
vidyādharabharadvājo yad vidyāsādhanodyataḥ ।। āsanenācalābhena calatā calitaḥ kila ।। viṣādākulacetasko duḥkhaṃ jīvati vāsavaḥ ।। hariṇā suprabhādiṣṭā gandharvādhipateḥ sutā ।।
atiśeṣe tvam ity eṣā pratītiḥ piṣṭapatraye ।। tathā te rūpasaubhāgye saphalībhavatām iti ।। śṛṅgārair aicchad ākraṣṭuṃ satattvālamabanaṃ manaḥ ।। tadā karmakarīkarma nirvedād akarod asau ।।
toṣito ayam avocat tāṃ varaḥ kas te bhavatv iti ।। tan me bhagavatā dhairyāt saubhāgyaṃ durbhagīkṛtam ।। saubhāgyamātrakaṃ straiṇaṃ kāmakāmeṣu bhartṛṣu ।। jagato api varas tasmād bhavān evāstu no varaḥ ।।
cetaścakṣupriyāt puṃsaḥ kīdṛśo anyo varād varaḥ ।। vaśitvād rāgam ālambya saubhāgyaṃ me dadātv iti ।। ciram ārādhito bhaktyā virakto api hi rajyate ।। vardhitā ca vinītā ca vidyāsu ca kalāsu ca ।।
abhāṣata bharadvājaṃ nāmāsyāḥ kriyatām iti ।। iti tasyāḥ kṛtaṃ nāma bharadvājena sārthakam ।। nāmnā gandharvadatteti vitta mām eva tām iti ।। jātarūpaśilājālajyotir ujjvalitadrumam ।।
kalyāṇaṃ kāñcanaṃ cāsminn asmatkalyāṇakāraṇam ।। viśālā parṇaśālāsau śilābhiḥ pūritā mayā ।। kim etad iti tasyai ca yathāvṛttaṃ nyavedayam ।। āyuṣman na hiraṇmayyaḥ śilā eva hi tāḥ śilāḥ ।।
bhāsvadbhāsābhibhāvinyā muktaṃ rātrau vijṛmbhate ।। paśyante ca diśaḥ pītās tṛṣṇātimiramīlitāḥ ।। acirāt saṃvidhāsyāmi tat tyajākulatām iti ।। tā mayā duḥkhaduḥkhena sarvāhṇena nirākṛtāḥ ।।
yad bravīmi tad ākarṇya tvam anuṣṭhātum arhasi ।। sa tathaiva yatas tasmād asmākam iyam ātmajā ।। na hi sāgarajanmā śrīḥ śrīpater anyam arhati ।। cihnair yaiś ca sa vijñeyaḥ kriyantāṃ tāni cetasi ।।
puras teṣām iyaṃ gāyād geyaṃ nārāyaṇastutim ।। vādayet tac ca yas tasmai dadyāḥ svatanayām iti ।। vīṇāvādanaparyantaṃ tat tat tena niveditam ।। khedocchedāya tac campāṃ pratiṣṭhethāṃ yuvām iti ।।
yāmatrayaṃ triyāmāyāyāpayitvā prasuptavān ।। saveṇunisvanaṃ svānaṃ manaḥśravaṇavallabham ।। nidrātyājanadakṣāṇi bandināṃ vanditāni ca ।। paryaṅkam adhitiṣṭhantam adrākṣaṃ ratnapiñjaram ।।
mṛṣṭahāṭakadaṇḍālītaṭite paṭamaṇḍape ।। vīṇāparicayavyagrām āsīnāṃ suprabhāsutām ।। goṇībhir hemapūrṇābhiḥ pūrṇaṃ paṭakuṭīkulam ।। samāhitaiś ca sīmāntān saṃkaṭān auṣṭrakaukṣakaiḥ ।।
svapne api na narair dṛṣṭā samṛddhiḥ kaiścid apy asau ।। gandharvanagaraṃ māyā svapno vāyaṃ bhaved iti ।। aprameyaprabhāvaṃ hi sadbhiḥ sucaritaṃ tapaḥ ।। bhūmer anyatra sarvatra satpātrādau nidhīyatām ।।
āyasthānaṃ hi te asty eva munikāñcanaparvataḥ ।। sārthasthānād itaś campā nanu krośeṣu pañcasu ।। niścayātmikayā sadyaḥ prajñayeva nivartitaḥ ।। dhūrtaṃ tādṛgvidhair eva suhṛdbhiḥ parivāritam ।।
adhyasthāpayam ātmīyāṃ śayyāṃ gatavilakṣatam ।। suhṛdgaṇam anujyeṣṭham udāraiḥ paryatoṣayam ।। pravṛddhapramadonmādā campā taṃ sārtham āvṛṇot ।। amṛtaiva janaḥ kaścic cirāt kaścid udaśvasat ।।
sphītair hemātisargaiś ca pauraśreṇim avardhayam ।। uddhṛtās te viśeṣeṇa dāridryanirayān mayā ।। daridravāṭakād ambā svam evānīyatāṃ gṛham ।। tataḥ śataguṇenāpi kretur niṣkretum arhasi ।।
draṣṭuṃ śaknoti yas tasya kṣudrakān dhig asūn iti ।। kena bhāgīrathī dṛṣṭā vicchinnajalasaṃhatiḥ ।। ujjvalā tu tvayedānīṃ kumudvatyā ivendunā ।। suprātaḥ prāviśaṃ campāṃ dhanādhipa ivālakām ।।
gatvā narendram adrākṣaṃ surendram iva bhāsvaram ।। asāv api mudāhūya mām āśliṣad akaitavam ।। satkṛtyājñāpayat putra jananī dṛśyatām iti ।। duṣpūraṃ pūrayāmi sma rājñas tṛṣṇārasātalam ।।
paṭhadbhiś ca tato viprair ātmīyam agamaṃ gṛham ।। paurair harṣakṛtotsāhair na kṣuṇṇaḥ katham apy aham ।। pūrṇād ivāndhatamasāni tuṣārakānter āryāt pṛthag janaśatāni hi saṃbhramanti ।। sāpi sārdhapayaḥpātrā patati sma mamopari ।।
anayat pāṇinākṛṣya gṛhābhyantaramaṇḍapam ।। sphītaiḥ parijanaṃ ca svaṃ vibhavaiḥ samayojayam ।। prāviśaṃ mātur ādeśād āvāsaṃ gurucārutam ।। apaśyaṃ prathamāṃ jāyāṃ karaśākhāvṛtānanām ।।
gaṅgadattā mayā dṛṣṭā śliṣṭabhittiḥ parāṅmukhī ।। smaranti hi tiraskārān munayo api garīyasaḥ ।। sindhurodhaḥ smarāmi sma phullanānālatāgṛham ।। sthitaprasthitagītādi viśrabdhācaritaṃ mayā ।।
hṛdayād vyāvṛtād yena kvāpi priyatamā gatā ।। adhunā niranukrośā sā praviṣṭānivāritā ।। praviśed api nāmeyaṃ durghaṭo ayaṃ manorathaḥ ।। taraṃgapāṇinākṛṣya hṛtā pāpena sindhunā ।।
praviśya tvarayāliṅgad aṅgais tuṅgatanūruham ।। tām eva dhyātavān asmi sindhubhaṅgāgratāraṇīm ।। tām evāśvāsayāmi sma mā sma bhīrur bhaver iti ।। vipannavahanaḥ kaṣṭe na tu kṣārāmbhudhāv iti ।।
gṛhaṃ tat paritaḥ paśyann apaśyaṃ vanitādvayam ।। vakṣaḥsthāpi satī nāsau dorbhyām āliṅgitā mayā ।। asrāvitā mamāgacchad ambātrāsākulekṣaṇā ।। ambā śayanam adhyāste śeṣās tv āsata bhūtale ।।
akālajñā hi mātāpi putreṇa paribhūyate ।। nanu sarvajñakalpasya bhāryāhaṃ mitravarmaṇaḥ ।। vyanaśiṣyan mahat kāryaṃ tac cedam avadhīyatām ।। vardhitaḥ śikṣitaś cāsi pitrā vidyācatuṣṭayam ।।
kuṭumbapālanālāpas tava jāto atidurbhagaḥ ।। suhṛdbhir dhruvakādyais tvam udyāne madhu pāyitaḥ ।। tayā tathā kṛtaś cāsi yathā vettha tvam eva tat ।। jananyai gaṅgadattāyāḥ kathito bhūbhṛtaiva saḥ ।।
tad evaikam asau rājñā kalpitaś cāraṇādibhiḥ ।। paurṇamāsī kṣapā kena dṛṣṭā dhvāntamalīmasā ।। balāv iva mahīpāle balirājyaṃ na durlabham ।। mama khaṭvātale tasmiñ chayitaṃ gaṅgadattayā ।।
atrāntare niṣaṇṇeyaṃ matkhaṭvātalabhūtale ।। bhāṇḍāgāre tava nyastam aśeṣaṃ kṛtalekhakam ।। smṛtvā mithyātiraskāraṃ na tiraskāram arhati ।। kātarā pramadābhāvāt prāṇān api parityajet ।।
sīdad gurutarārthānāṃ kaḥ kālo nāma kāryiṇām ।। vadhūḥ samudradinnāpi yathāyātā tathā śṛṇu ।। prayuktās te nṛpeṇaiva sa ca siddhārthako vaṇik ।। tāmraliptīpraveśāntaṃ śiṣṭaṃ siddhārthakena tat ।।
yathā samudradinnāyāḥ pāṇir ālambitas tvayā ।। vṛttaṃ karpāsadāhāntaṃ tāmraliptyāgamaś ca yaḥ ।। khyāpitaṃ yāvad ācero bhavantaṃ kvāpi nītavān ।। nairāśyakṛtanirvedāt paralokotsukābhavam ।।
samudradinnayā sārdhaṃ syālau prāviśatāṃ tataḥ ।। vilakṣyāvīkṣamāṇau mām ābhāṣyesam avocatām ।। sa ca yauvanamūḍhatvāt svīkṛto gaṅgadattayā ।। na śakyate yad ākhyātuṃ pulindaiḥ kila tat kṛtam ।।
niṣpratyāśaṃ kuṭumbaṃ naḥ prasthitaṃ yavanān prati ।। saṃbhāvyavyasanadhvaṃsaṃ samagāhāma sāgaram ।। mṛgendra iva nāgendraṃ prasphurantaṃ prabhinnavān ।। ārūḍhāḥ paṭṭapṛṣṭhāni prāpitā jaladhes taṭam ।।
bhrāntamegha ivodbhrāntā vyomni sārasakanyakā ।। yavanastham agacchāma mātāmahagṛhaṃ tataḥ ।। samṛddhe sarasīvāsīt tṛptaṃ haṃsakadambakam ।। āsāte kim udāsīnau bhavantau sthavirāv iva ।।
svajanānnena jīvantau kum ucyethe janair yuvām ।। gṛhītvā yānapātreṇa sindhur uttāryatām iti ।। śliṣṭapaṭṭām athādrākṣva tarantīṃ rudatīṃ striyam ।। āropayata bohittham ity avocāva vāhakān ।।
mātaḥ kasyāsi kā veti sā ca nīcair avocata ।। kaccit sāgaradattasya bhavantau tanayāv iti ।। kaccit samudradinnāsi sundarīty avadāva tām ।। sāparāṅmukhayor jaṅghe bāhubhyāṃ gāḍham āśliṣat ।।
dhikkāraḥ sāgaraṃ pāpaṃ yena tau kvāpi yāpitau ।। āpannapriyadārāṇāṃ naiṣa dharmaḥ satām iti ।। niḥsnehīkṛtacetaskāv abhāṣāvahi tām iti ।। āryaputraḥ punar yas te sa nau niścīyatām iti ।।
āvāṃ mā bhaiṣṭam ity uktvā svaṃ vṛttaṃ vṛttam abravīt ।। yasmai dattāsmi yuṣmābhis tam adrākṣaṃ vipadgatam ।। jāyante hi supuṇyānām utsavā vyasaneṣv api ।। tathā yathā priyatamau nāsmaraṃ pitarāv api ।।
prasthitau svaḥ svadeśāya vipannaḥ sa ca pūrvavat ।। saṃpraty eva taraṃgeṇa gamitaḥ kvāpi vairiṇā ।। akasmāj jātaśatrubhyāṃ bhavadbhyāṃ cāham uddhṛtā ।। śīte śītalayiṣyāmi muñcataṃ māṃ yuvām iti ।।
utpannaparamānandāv āliṅgāma parasparam ।। bhaviṣyati tathā bhūyaś citraṃ hi caritaṃ vidheḥ ।। parisaṃsthāpayantau tām atarāva mahodadhim ।। sahasraguṇalābhaṃ tad āvābhyāṃ parivartitam ।।
sarvam arpitam āvābhyāṃ tubhyaṃ tat parigṛhyatām ।। evaṃ samudradinnā ca tvatputrasya nidarśanam ।। āgamiṣyati tad devi muñca kātaratām iti ।। susatkāraprayuktau tau yathāgatam agacchatām ।।
daivapauruṣayuktasya śrīr iva ślāghyajanmanaḥ ।। rakṣantyā gurumāninyā carite caritaṃ mayā ।। pitrā tulyo bhavatv eṣa śāpo nāśaṃsitas tava ।। devatānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca yātv ānṛṇyaṃ bhavān iti ।।
।। campāyāṃ ramamāṇasya kālaḥ kaścid agād mama ।। sahasā pramadāveṣam apaśyaṃ puruṣaṃ puraḥ ।। ayuktendradhanuśchāyaśṛṅgāragalakaṇṭhikam ।।
prakṣālya caraṇau bhaktyā svālaṃkārair alaṃkṛtaḥ ।। yathā kesariśāvasya gandhahastijighāṃsayā ।। eṣa strīpuruṣaḥ śocyo yo na strī na pumān iti ।। vadatā nihato asīti vimuktaḥ śikhipicchakaḥ ।।
nāgeṣur iva karṇāstraḥ kirīṭāgraṃ kirīṭinaḥ ।। niḥsthāmnaḥ kuñjarasyeva vidhānaṃ vinaśiṣyataḥ ।। dhūmrachāyaḥ śanair jalpan dhig dhiṅ mām iti nirgataḥ ।। savāḍavam upāsarpan nimnageva mahārṇavam ।।
yat pureva pragalbheyam upasarpati mām iti ।। kiṃcid vijñāpayāmy eṣa yātu vaḥ krodhapāvakaḥ ।। vidyādharapater bhrātā gaurimuṇḍasya sādhakaḥ ।। samāpte asminn avighnena vandhyāḥ syur no manorathaḥ ।।
tasyai varaṃ mahāgaurī dayate śāpam anyathā ।। vihantā sarvasiddhīnāṃ nāsti vighnavināyakaḥ ।। tuṣṭayā toṣitā gaurī mayā yūyaṃ ca roṣitāḥ ।। gaurībhraṣṭā mahāvidyā vidyeva tanumedhasaḥ ।।
yan mayā roṣitā yūyam etan me mṛṣyatām iti ।। dayitāmantravādinyā hṛdayād apasarpitaḥ ।। āsīnaḥ sānudāsena kadācid iti bhāṣitaḥ ।। tena dohadakaṃ pṛṣṭā bhāryāvocat trapāvatī ।।
krīḍeyaṃ saha yuṣmābhir jale jalanidher iti ।। saraḥ sāgaravistāram avandhyājñena khānitam ।। vimānākārapotasthau tau rājānau viceratuḥ ।। āhṛṣṭaparapuṣṭeṣu divaseṣu mahībhujā ।।
sā ca yātreyam āyātā ramyāmṛtabhujām api ।। asmadādiparīvārais tataḥ sā dṛśyatām iti ।। nirgacchāmi sma campāyāḥ pauranetrotpalārcitaḥ ।। pakkaṇaṃ dṛṣṭavān asmi rājarājapurojjvalam ।।
kālam apy ujjvalāyāmaṃ ghanāghanam ivāmbudam ।। dīptasaudāmanīcakrāṃ prāvṛṣeṇyām iva kṣapām ।। nīlanīrajamāleva komalānilalāsitā ।। iyam eva tatas tanvī kṣiptakuṅkumagauratā ।।
mālayeva palāśānām aṃśumantaṃ suvarcalā ।। nitāntasnigdhayā prācīṃ prabhayeva divākaraḥ ।। tayā mama mayā tasyānītāḥ prāṇā vidheyatām ।। mātaṅgīṃ manasāgacchaṃ śarīreṇa mahāsaraḥ ।।
tatrasthenaiva no dṛṣṭaḥ saṃsāra iva yoginā ।। mandamandaparispandas tāmramaṇḍalatām ayāt ।। aprasādyaiva tāṃ bhānuḥ pratīcim upasarpati ।। mātaṅgīm anusarpāmi yathā rājā tathā prajāḥ ।।
tam evānugamiṣyāmi na devacaritaṃ caret ।। pūrvam eva sayānena nagarīm abhinīyatām ।। parādhūsarayanty asyāḥ sotpalāmalakāvalīm ।। purastād aham āyāmi saha nāgarakair iti ।।
dārike dve parāvṛtya vanditvā mām avocatām ।। vinodayatam ālāpair yuvām aparuṣair iti ।। paṭuvegena yānena pakkaṇāntikam āgamam ।। gacchantam iva nirvyājam āgacchantaṃ samaikṣata ।।
tatas tad api saṃprāptaṃ javena kulaṭādvayam ।। śreyāṃsi bahuvighnāni bhavantīti tathaiva tat ।। nidrām abhilaṣāmi sma mātaṅgīsaṃgamāśayā ।। prayukte mayi ye dāsyau te pānīyam ayācata ।।
upaveśya puro akleśair apṛcchad bandhakīdvayam ।। dṛṣṭo ayaṃ taraleneti tatas tābhyāṃ niveditam ।। netrābhyām animeṣābhyām aryaputras tayā yathā ।। jāgratha svapithety uccair jāgramīti mayoditam ।।
tathā nalinikāṃ nūnaṃ kartum icchasi mām iti ।। bharadvājasutākhyātum upākrāmata vṛttakam ।। nagaraṃ kānanadvīpaṃ mahendranagaropamam ।। putro manoharas tasya saṃjñāyāpi manoharaḥ ।।
nānāruciṣu sattveṣu kasyacit kiṃcid īpsitam ।। vasantam iva taṃ premṇā na kadācid amuñcatām ।। kumārāvasathasthāya samitrāya niveditam ।। agrāmyo dhīravacanaḥ kasmād api didṛkṣate ।।
vilepanam upādatta dhūpaṃ ca tvarito adahat ।। śiro nipīḍya pāṇibhyāṃ saṃkocyāṅgam apāsarat ।। āghrātena śiraḥśūlam utpannam iti cāvadat ।। manoharaṃ muhuḥ paśyan svayaṃ dhūpam ayojayat ।।
sumanogandhasaṃvādī dhūpo ayaṃ dāhyatām iti ।। pratīto gandhaśāstrajñaṃ sumaṅgalam apūjayat ।। dinais tricaturair eva caturaḥ paryatoṣayat ।। manoharām agād draṣṭuṃ yakṣasattrāṃ manoharaḥ ।।
yakṣīpratikṛtir dṛṣṭā vinyastā citrakarmaṇi ।। citre nyastāpi sā tena citte nyastātirāgiṇā ।। sumanogandhadhūpādyais tām evaikām asevata ।। nitambād ambaraṃ tasyāḥ sa kilākraṣṭum aihata ।।
viṣṇor vakṣa iva śyāmam asevata nabhastalam ।। yakṣī yakṣapateḥ śāpāt prāptālekhyaśarīratām ।। śāpāntam arthitenāham iti nidhyāya dhīritā ।। sa eva kṛtaśāpāntas tava bhartā bhaviṣyati ।।
sadṛśo varadānena śāpo api hi mahātmanām ।। śailaṃ śrīkuñjanāmānaṃ yakṣāvāsaṃ vrajer iti ।। taṃ cālokya tathāvasthaṃ viṣādaṃ bakulādayaḥ ।। alam ākulatāṃ gatvā sulabhā sukumārikā ।।
yuṣmatsaṃbhogam icchantī na tathā kathayed iti ।। siddhayātraṃ parāvṛttam apaśyat potavāṇijam ।। pṛṣṭas tena bhavān kiṃ kim āścaryaṃ dṛṣṭavān iti ।। dṛṣṭaṃ kiṃ nāma nāścaryam āścaryanidhir ambudhiḥ ।।
sāndrahemaprabhāpiṅgaṃ tuṅgaśṛṅgasrajaṃ nagam ।। vṛddhair eṣa samākhyātaḥ śrīkuñjaḥ śṛṅgavān iti ।। rājaputro api rājānaṃ natvā vāṇijam anvagāt ।। rājaputrād gṛhaprāptād āḍhyaḥ ko nāma na traset ।।
na satkārakhalīkāram arhanti śiśavo guroḥ ।। sa kutūhaline mahyaṃ spaṣṭam ākhyāyatām iti ।। śrīkuñjaṃ sahitaṃ cihnair ity ākhyātuṃ pracakrame ।। marutā tyājitasthairyo yātaḥ potaḥ svatantratām ।।
citrākārān apaśyāma prāṇino jalacāriṇaḥ ।। yūthaśaḥ prastutakrīḍān unmajjananimajjanaiḥ ।। dhvanimātrakabhāṣāṇāṃ dvaṃdvāni paśudharmaṇām ।। pakṣacchedabhayālīnān nagān iva mahārṇavāt ।।
yasyāghrāṇāya saṃpannaṃ manye ghrāṇam ayaṃ jagat ।। dūrād girim apaśyāma ratnakūṭasthakiṃnaram ।। vṛddhair eṣa samākhyātaḥ śrīkuñjaḥ śṛṅgavān iti ।। sahasāgaradigdeśaṃ spaṣṭaṃ saṃpuṭake alikhat ।।
bakulādisahāyo asāv agāhata mahārṇavam ।। āsīdad acireṇaiva potena diśam īpsitām ।। manaścakṣuḥśarīraiḥ saḥ śrīkuñjaṃ yugapad gataḥ ।। ākāśāśaviśāloccaṃ potaḥ sopānam āsadat ।।
tena śailāgram ārohad dharmeneva tripiṣṭapam ।। saṃkalpacakṣuṣā paśyann agacchat sukumārikām ।। yayāsminn āhitaṃ prema narāmarakumārake ।। yo vṛtaḥ sahajāhāryaiḥ śarīrādiguṇair iti ।।
sve saṃkalpamaye yakṣīṃ vakṣasīva manoharaḥ ।। svinnakaṇṭakite pāṇau gṛhītvāntaḥ praveśitaḥ ।। raktākṣaṃ śātakaumbhābhaṃ samadaṃ medurodaram ।। śvaśrūḥ paśyety anujñātaḥ praviveśāvarodhanam ।।
śvaśrūśvaśurayos tasya pitāmahyo api yoṣitaḥ ।। anujñātaś ca sasnehaṃ prāviśat kanyakāgṛham ।। divyastrīsaṃprayogāś ca manoharamano aharan ।। atītā divasāḥ pañca kumāra pratigamyatām ।।
sthātuṃ mānuṣamātreṇa pañcamād divasāt param ।। vahanasvāminaṃ pañca pratīkṣante dināni te ।। svargataś cyavamānasya dhyāmadhyāmābhavat prabhā ।। adyārabhya gamiṣyāmi tavaivāhaṃ gṛhān iti ।।
tatraiva suhṛdo apaśyad divyaratnāmbarasrajaḥ ।। tena te kathayanti sma yathā yūyaṃ tathā vayaṃ ।। asmān upacaranti sma surān iva surāṅganāḥ ।। sevamānā vayaṃ devaṃ devatām amṛtā gatāḥ ।।
tāsām evānubhāvena saṃterus te mahodadhim ।। prāviśaṃs tadviyogārtaṃ śūnyarājapathaṃ puram ।। avaguṣṭhitamūrdhānaṃ paśyati sma manoharam ।। gatvā dhyānaparāsthānaṃ mahīpālam atoṣayat ।।
mā vocad dārakaṃ kaścit kva gato abhūd bhavān iti ।। so api tasyāṅkam āropya harati sma vilakṣatām ।। gandhaśāstraphalaṃ sāraṃ dhūpam āyojyatām iti ।। sugandhitāpradhānaṃ ca ratam āhur aninditam ।।
sa kardamasamas tāsām ato asau yakṣakardamaḥ ।। dhanurvedasya kṛtsnasya viddhasāraṃ hi sauṣṭhavam ।। dhūpasnānīyagandhādi yathādeśam ayojayat ।। āsannadayitāśūnyāṃ duḥkhaśayyām asevata ।।
preritaḥ paṭunānyena samīreṇeva toyadaḥ ।। praviśya sahasāchyāsta paryaṅkaṃ sukumārikā ।। sasahāyāham āyātā yāta viśramyatām iti ।। yathā tathāvidhotkaṇṭhe tathāgamayatāṃ niśām ।।
prabhāte rājaputrāya rātrivṛttaṃ nyavedayan ।। iti saṃvatsaro yātas tābhis teṣām acetitatḥ ।। svādhīnānāṃ parādhīnaiḥ saha saṃgatir īdṛśī ।। sakhīsahitayā varṣaṃ gṛhītabrahmacaryayā ।।
svagṛhāya gamiṣyāmi tatra gacched bhavān iti ।। ninditāmṛtapānena kiṃ punar darśanena te ।। khaṃ paśyantam apaśyaṃs tam iyaṃ yātīti vādinam ।। toṣagadgadavāg uccair abhāṣata sumaṅgalaḥ ।।
dṛṣṭamārgā muhūrtena yāmas taṃ guhyakācalam ।। saṃgamāśādhanaprāṇāyāpayāma samām iti ।। sa ca potaḥ samīreṇa dūraṃ hṛtvā vipāditaḥ ।। tāṃ na cetitavān eva vipattiṃ māradāruṇām ।।
caurasainyena saṃyamya tasyālaṃkaraṇaṃ hṛtam ।। veṣṭitaṃ kuṭṭitaṃ baddham udbaddhaṃ pādapeṣu ca ।। kariṇīpṛṣṭham āropya sasainyaḥ prasthitaḥ puraḥ ।। manoharaḥ puraṃ prāpat kuṅkumāliptacatvaram ।।
āgacchat kalarāsānāṃ nānāpattrisrajām iva ।। viśālamaṇḍapāsīnaṃ śakrākāraṃ narādhipam ।। gāḍham āliṅgya tenāpi ciraṃ prītyā nirūpitaḥ ।। kutaḥ sumaṅgalād anyaś cakṣuṣmān iti bhūpatiḥ ।।
bhaved aham iva bhraṣṭaḥ potabhaṅgabhayād iti ।। apaśyan natamūrdhānaṃ sa tam eva sumaṅgalam ।। bhujau me bakulāśokau kaccit kuśalināv iti ।। yathā cāham ihāyātas tathāśrotuṃ prasīdata ।।
dṛṣṭam eva hi yuṣmābhir nṛpaś caiṣa puraṃdaraḥ ।। sa yena yūyam ānītāḥ sāgaropāntakānanāt ।। yasyā na pramadāloke na cāsti sadṛśo varaḥ ।। guṇarūpāntarajñānaśālinaḥ prahitā hatāḥ ।।
tadā mām ayam āhūya sadainyasmitam uktavān ।। nātho api bhava nas tāta saṃkaṭād uddharann itaḥ ।। ādareṇa tam anviṣyes tyaja śrīmadirārujam ।। durgatebhyaḥ sudūreṇa śocanīyaḥ satām iti ।।
mahī sāṣṭādaśadvīpā parikrāntā varārthinā ।। tadā tyaktumanaḥ prāṇān prāvivikṣaṃ mahodadhim ।। yuṣmadguṇakathāsaktāḥ saṃtatāḥ sādhusaṃpadaḥ ।। jyotsnayeva tamorāśir yuṣmatkīrtyā nirākṛtaḥ ।।
ātmāpi gandhaśāstrajñas tadā vaḥ śrāvito mayā ।। rañjayanti manaḥ kṣipraṃ guṇair api nirākṛtāḥ ।। suhṛdbhiḥ saha yuṣmābhir ahaṃ jijñāsitas tadā ।। dhūpaṃ tat phalake nyastām apaśyaṃ bhartṛdārikām ।।
ātmano rājaputryāś ca vidhātuś ca kṛtārthatām ।। yāvad yuṣmadguṇair eva hṛtaḥ sādhumanoharaiḥ ।। pāpam adhyācaranty eva bhṛtyā bhartṛpriyepsavaḥ ।। sevācārāpadeśena gataiva sukumārikā ।।
saṃnidhāpitapotena samudram avatāritāḥ ।। vipannavahanas tatra na ca kaścana vidyate ।। idaṃ ca puram āyātāyathā yūyaṃ tathā vayam ।। na hi śrīḥ svayam āyāntī kālātikramam arhati ।।
yathākāmam upābhuṅkta karī kamālinīm iva ।। patyus te dayitā yakṣī maivaṃ naiṣīd asāv iti ।। unnidraiva sanidreva suptā kila pṛthak kṣaṇam ।। śayitaṃ pṛthag āsādya manoharam apāharat ।।
yuṣmān api hared eṣā tathā mātaṅgakanyakā ।। na hi caṇḍālakanyāsu rajyante devasūnavaḥ ।। na me nalinikāvārttā virasāntā bhaved iti ।। iti jihmaṃ puras tasyāḥ kāmukācāram ācaram ।।
madaṃ vidhatte madirā prakṛtyā kim aṅga kāntānanasaṅgaramyā ।। divasāṃś ca nayāmi sma subhagānilacandanān ।। aryaputra vicitraṃ vaḥ krīḍāsthānam upāgatam ।। nāgarair devi devīti vandyamānā varārthibhiḥ ।।
tava bhartre mayā dattā kanyājinavatīti mām ।। dṛṣṭvā svāminam āyāmi tat kṣaṇaṃ kṣamyatām iti ।। tenāgacchatu sātraiva madvacaś cedam ucyatām ।। praṣṭavyāḥ santi cāsmākaṃ tāvat pṛcchāmi tān aham ।।
tvādṛśātithisatkāraḥ kāraṇaṃ śreyasām iti ।। mām abhāṣata bhāratyā gambhīrabhayagarbhayā ।। aho mahākulīnānām ācāraḥ sādhusevinām ।। devī vāsavadattā vā kiṃ vā magadhavaṃśajā ।।
āha yat santi me kecit tāvat pṛcchāmi tān iti ।। kim evam apamānyante guravo gurusevibhiḥ ।। acirād yāsyatīty etat sa evānubhaviṣyati ।। dagdhvā campaikadeśaṃ sā maholkeva tirohitā ।।
indrajālābhiyuktā vā māyākārī bhaved iti ।। asmaddhṛdayasaṃtāpī paritāpajvaro abhavat ।। asmadaṅgapariśvaṅgair nāsyās tāpo nyavartata ।। nirambudāmbaracchāyaiś channam ambaram ambudaiḥ ।।
samārohāma harmyasya sāndraśubhrasudhaṃ śiraḥ ।। pāścātyamarudādyotijaḍaṃ jalam adhārayam ।। śanakaiḥ śāntasaṃtāpāṃ bhāradvājīm ahāsayat ।। jale rantum ivoṣṇāṃśuḥ prāviśat paścimārṇavam ।।
praśāntāgantusaṃtāpā śītapīḍāturābhavat ।। viśītāṃ kṛtavān asmi tāpaśītāpahāribhiḥ ।। prāsādāt prāsravat toyaṃ sumeror iva nirjharaiḥ ।। munipītāmbudhicchāyaṃ harmyāgraṃ tad adṛśyata ।।
dānaiḥ paricarāmi sma samānaiḥ paricārakān ।। upāyi prabalāṃ nidrāṃ sukhaduḥkhābhibhāvinīm ।। gambhīrekṣaṇam adrākṣaṃ naraṃ vyāttāsyakandaram ।। kvāpi māṃ netum icchantaṃ netum aicchaṃ yamālayam ।।
na taṃ tatra nihanmi sma bhīṣaṇāraṭiśaṅkitaḥ ।। sa māṃ sopānamārgeṇa prāsādāgrād avātarat ।। kakṣārakṣās tam adrākṣur na niryāntam acetanāḥ ।। kavāṭasaṃpuṭas tatra śanair aghaṭayat svayam ।।
prahāraḥ sa tu me jāto jānupīḍāprayojanaḥ ।। kulaputraḥ sa tatra sma kiṃcit kālaṃ na gacchati ।। apaśyaṃ dvīpināṃ kṛttīs tathedam abhavan mama ।। āstīrṇāni kim arthaṃ vā kenāpi viśikhāsv iti ।।
saṃtatair vitatā rathyā pradīpārciḥkadambakaiḥ ।। prāsāde kvacid aśrauṣaṃ vacaḥ kasyāpi kāminaḥ ।। nākarṇayasi kūjantam ulūkaṃ subhagadhvanim ।। ayaṃ naḥ sukhahetūnām agraṇīḥ suhṛdām iti ।।
utkaṇṭhāgarbhakaṇṭhena nīlakaṇṭhena kūjitam ।। duṣṭasya caṭakasyāsya mastakaś chidyatām iti ।। ājñātam anayor nyāyye saṃmānanavimānane ।। ekaparyaṅkasuptāpi suptā bhartuḥ parāṅmukhī ।।
trastayātaḥ parāvṛtya gāḍham āliṅgitaḥ patiḥ ।। ulūkabhayapūrvo api kāntāśleṣo abhinanditaḥ ।। yenāsya vimukhī kāntā trāsād abhimukhī kṛtā ।। patyuḥ kaṇṭhaṃ parityajya sthitā bhūyaḥ parāṅmukhī ।।
yenāsyābhimukhī kāntā kūjatā vimukhī kṛtā ।। kṛtanigrahayor vācaṃ kulaṭāviṭayor yathā ।। āghrātā mama sā nāsā tvatkṛte vikṛtā kṛtā ।। karṇau mama tathā bhūtau bhavatāṃ bhavato yathā ।।
kṛtaghna tvam apīdānīm avajānāsi mām iti ।। mayāpi nanu yat prāptaṃ tvadarthaṃ tan na dṛśyate ।। samastās tarpitā yena dakṣiṇābhir dvijātayaḥ ।। yena cāsisanāthena nikṛttāḥ kariṇāṃ karāḥ ।।
ātmaśeṣaparastrīṇāṃ yena bhuktāḥ payodharāḥ ।। kṛttaḥ śastreṇa saṃdhānād bandhanād iva pallavaḥ ।। yena krāntā samudrāntā tīrthasnānāya medinī ।। vapraprākāraparikhāḥ śatakṛtvo vilaṅghitāḥ ।।
pādo me yādṛśo jātas tādṛśaḥ kasya kathyatām ।। sa guṇān pāṇipādasya gaṇayen mandadhīr girā ।। ātmanaḥ pāṇipādasya praśaṃsāmi guṇān iti ।। āgatas taṃ likhāmy āśu datta me vartikām iti ।।
āgacchaṃ nagarīdvāram uttaraṃ pretavāhanaḥ ।। uttareṇa hi nīyante na dvāreṇa jighāṃsitum ।। kṣīṇamāṃsakam adrākṣaṃ bālakaṃ gatajīvakam ।। śoṣitaḥ śuṣkaraivatyā varāko ayaṃ mṛtaḥ śiśuḥ ।।
atrāsye maraṇād enam iṣṭvā krūragrahān iti ।। puruṣaṃ proṣitaprāṇam athedam abhavan mama ।। nāyam anyatamenāpi kena nāma mṛto bhavet ।। nidrāsukham upāsīnaḥ pratibuddhaḥ pipāsitaḥ ।।
gavākṣasthodapātrastham udakaṃ pītam ātmanā ।। svaviṣānaladāhāndhaḥ praviṣṭaḥ prāg bhujaṃgamaḥ ।। tena pītena mūḍho ayaṃ sadyaḥ prāṇair viyojitaḥ ।। prākāraśṛṅgarandhreṇa nikṣiptaḥ parikhātaṭe ।।
mantramaṇḍalamudrāṇām upāṃśusmaraṇād iti ।। aśokaśākhiśākhāyām udbaddhāṃ kām api striyam ।। nīlārdhorukasaṃvītaviśālajaghanasthalām ।। cīnapaṭṭāṃśukanyastam anarghyaṃ ratnamaṇḍanam ।।
parāmṛśya bahūn pakṣān idaṃ niścitavān dhiyā ।। na vimānitavān etāṃ patiḥ parihasann api ।। gṛhītaṃ nāma kasyāścit pramadāyāḥ pramādinā ।। gāḍhaṃ tāḍitayā krūraṃ kṛtaṃ karmedam etayā ।।
nāsti yas tānitasnehāl lālayaty eva kevalam ।। dṛśyante hy avasīdanto dhīmanto apy atilālitāḥ ।। tat taskarakarasparśaparihārārtham etayā ।। alaṃkāro apy asatkāraḥ saṃkāra iva dṛśyate ।।
citānalālokahṛtāndhakāram agaccham ujjīvajanādhivāsam ।। dīnabhīṣaṇaphetkārāḥ kukkuraiḥ kharabukkitaiḥ ।। paritaḥ kuṇapaṃ nṛtyaḍḍākinīmaṇḍalaṃ kvacit ।। mahāmāṃsaṃ mahāsattvāḥ krīyatām iti vādinam ।।
sādhakaṃ siddhinistriṃśam utpatantaṃ nabhaḥ kvacit ।। yātrāṃ yā gacchatā dṛṣṭā sā dṛṣṭā sthavirā mayā ।। haṃkārāntena mantreṇa juhvatī naraśoṇitam ।। guruharṣavi।ālākṣī karmaśeṣaṃ samāpayat ।।
svāgataṃ candravaktrāya kumāro mucyatām iti ।। yena kākamukhasyāsya mukham etena tulyate ।। dakṣiṇābhimukhas tāram āraṭyāpatitaḥ kṣitau ।। śmaśānam āgato asmīti khedaṃ mā manaso gamaḥ ।।
samātṛpramathānīkas trisaṃdhyaṃ saṃnidhīyate ।। na hy anyatra tuṣārāṃśur anyatrāsya marīcayaḥ ।। prāptāḥ pretavane siddhiṃ tasmān nedam amaṅgalam ।। na hi niṣkāraṇaḥ khedas tvādṛśām upapadyate ।।
śarīrīva mahadbāhor mahāsiṃhaḥ patir mama ।। sā dineṣu gamiṣyatsu vijñātā bhavatā svayam ।। phalabhāram ivānantaṃ dhanaḥ kusumasaṃcayaḥ ।। rātriṃ divam asūyanti yasyai tridaśakanyakāḥ ।।
bhāradvājīdvitīyas tvaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ pravahaṇāśritaḥ ।। durlabhe bhavati strīṇāṃ dṛṣṭe tvādṛśi yādṛśī ।। yadā nākathayaj jñātā mantraśaktyā mayā tadā ।। pautryāḥ prāṇaparitrāṇaṃ kariṣyantyā bhavān vṛtaḥ ।।
sādhayitvā tathā pretaṃ tvam ihānāyito mayā ।। mālām adhārayanto api labhante hi divaukasaḥ ।। athādṛśyata tatraiva sāpy anāgatm āgatā ।। varaṃ pāṇau gṛhāṇeti tām avocat pitāmahī ।।
sphurantaṃ sphuratāgṛhṇād dakṣiṇaṃ dakṣiṇena sā ।। apaśyaṃ kuṅkumābhe api svakare varṇasaṃkaram ।। tatas tām avadaṃ devi jano ayaṃ paravān iti ।। āvartayantam utkāntiṃ candrakāntākṣamaṇḍalam ।।
gaurimuṇḍo mahāgaurīm ārādhayitum icchati ।। yāv etau pārśvayor asya bhujāv iva mahābalau ।। so ayam aṅgārako yo asau jahāra kusumālikām ।। dviṣantam antaraṃ prāpya bhavantaṃ hantum icchati ।।
anantāś ca mahāntaś ca bhaviṣyantaś ca śatravaḥ ।। tvām etadviparītāriṃ pāntu devagurudvijāḥ ।। caṇḍasiṃhasahāyo api mahad asya prayojanam ।। idānīṃ caṇḍasiṃho api sumahābalamātṛkaḥ ।।
vimānam aham adrākṣam avarūḍhaṃ vihāyasaḥ ।। kham agacchann ivāgacchaṃ vahaneneva sāgaram ।। lokālokādiparyantam ādarśaparimaṇḍalam ।। sa tu nāsti pradeśo asya yo vimānair anāvṛtaḥ ।।
nikṛṣṭasyāpi devasya vimānaṃ yojanāyatam ।। gacchāmi sma vimānāni paśyann āyānti yānti ca ।। kasyām api diśi sphītam adṛśyata puraḥ puram ।। śṛṅgāt prāgacalasyeva sahasrakaramaṇḍalam ।।
śarīram iva mātaṅgyāḥ śarīreṇa nirantaram ।। āgamat puruṣas tasmāt prabhāva iva dehavān ।। kathitaṃ dhanamatyāhaṃ caṇḍasiṃham avandiṣi ।। aṅgair aṅgaṃ samāliṅgya snehādraiḥ karkaśair api ।।
jyogbhartar jaya deveti sa mām uktvedam abravīt ।। āliṅganaṃ tu bhartṝṇāṃ bhṛtyaiḥ paribhavo mahān ।। mahatī devatā hy eṣā tvādṛgrūpeṇa tiṣṭhati ।। caṇḍasiṃhapuraṃ tāvat tumulotsavam āsadam ।।
citraṃ citrair mahāratnair indrāṇījaghanocitaiḥ ।। avaśyādheyaśobhānām ākhyātaṃ rāmaṇīyakam ।। na stanyam api yāvante jananīr api bālakāḥ ।। sakalāḥ sakalā vidyā mātṛkevānuśīlitāḥ ।।
prakṣayo na ca jāyante rathyāḥ prāsādasaṃkaṭāḥ ।। sa tasmin mokṣaśāstreṣu śrūyate kapilādibhiḥ ।। akalmaṣaguṇāt tasmād ramaṇīyatamaṃ kutaḥ ।। anyeṣām api siddhānām īdṛśāny adhikāny api ।।
prāviśaṃ kanyakāgāraṃ hasitāmbaramandiram ।। kim artham api cāhutā mātrājinavatī gatā ।। nāgataiva tad āsīn me tvarāturamater matiḥ ।। samastair asamastaiś ca ramayanti priyāḥ priyān ।।
aham apy eṣa tiṣṭhāmi duḥkhasaṃtaptamānasaḥ ।। vivāhavighnasaṃbhrāntam aikṣe sāntaḥpuraṃ puram ।। jyeṣṭhakṛṣṇacaturdaśyām ārdrasthe tārakāpatau ।। phalguṇīṣu vivāho ayaṃ rājñā kārayitāvayoḥ ।।
tad brāhmeṇa vivāhena sūnoḥ saṃskāram icchati ।। tāṃ prāpaṃ kanyakām ante tapaḥsiddhim ivepsitām ।। tayā saha prāvṛṣamāsi ramyām aśuklapakṣāntaniśām ivaikām ।। anuyuktā mayā kaccin nṛpaḥ kuśalavān iti ।।
nivedayitum ārabdhā śrūyatāṃ bhartṛdāraka ।। svais tyaktaḥ sāparādhatvāt kiṃcit kālam ihāsthitaḥ ।। āsīnāṃ pitur utsaṅge dṛṣṭvā rājānam uktavān ।। madīyaguṇasaṃkhyā ca buddhaiva bhavatām iti ।।
kiṃ tu komalajanmeyaṃ prauḍhā tāvad bhavatv iti ।। āyoṣidbālagopālam ālāpaḥ śrāvitaḥ pure ।। diṣṭyā vṛddhir bhavaty adya mameva bhavatām iti ।। vismṛtopakṛtaḥ krodhād āha rājānam atrapaḥ ।।
yad dattvā tanayāṃ mahyam anyasmai dattavān iti ।। sutā vā vyavahāro vā yuddhaṃ vā dīyatām iti ।। labdhum arhati dīrghāyur vyavahāras tu dīyate ।। vāyumuktamahādhyakṣaṃ saptaparṇapuraṃ gataḥ ।।
tatraiva sahitau yātaṃ rohiṇīśaśināv iva ।। megharājyā yathākhyātaṃ jitaḥ sa capalas tathā ।। sāntvabālātapasparśān mukhāmbhojaṃ vikāśitam ।। saptaparṇapurodyāne saptaparṇapure sthitā ।।
yāvad emi sakhīṃ dṛṣṭvā vanditvā ca gurūn iti ।। sthūlamauktikavarṇāni saptaparṇāni dṛṣṭavān ।। bandhūkataralaṃ hāram utpalaiś churitodaram ।। kusumaiḥ kalpayāmi sma kambūnūpuramekhalāḥ ।।
nirjitaḥ sa durātmeti hṛṣṭā mām apy aharṣayat ।। anuyogam upekṣante vivakṣanto api vācakāḥ ।। vāyumuktā sakhī dṛṣṭā kanyāntaḥpuravartinī ।। pradhvanantīṃ śṛṇomi sma bherīṃ bhairavagarjitām ।।
sakhī svāṃ dārikām āha yāhi vijñāyatām iti ।। vardhase devi diṣṭyeti mām uktvoktavatī punaḥ ।। vāyumuktākṣadarśanāś ca samāyātāḥ sabhāsadaḥ ।। āryaveṣaḥ sa tān āha puraḥ sthitvā nirāsanaḥ ।।
anyasmin dattavān yatra nāgaraṃ pṛcchyatām iti ।। megharājyā yad ākhyātaṃ tad evākhyātam āha ca ।। pṛcchyantāṃ te api teṣāṃ ced aviruddhā pramāṇatā ।। nṛpater manukalpasya kim etasya parīkṣayā ।।
pratyakṣasyānumānena pramāṇatvaṃ pramīyate ।। arthī vikacikaḥ kanyām anyāṃ mṛgayatām iti ।। utpatya nabhasā gacchann uccair āha sabhāsadaḥ ।। aham eva hi kartavye kartavye buddhivān iti ।।
kasmin punar asau kārye kartavye buddhimān iti ।। śarīraśaradākārataskarām idam abravam ।। tavāropitam aṅgeṣu subhagāṅgi virājate ।। mām avocad vidhūyāṅgam asūyāmantharasmitā ।।
na hi dṛṣṭaṃ vinābhyāsāt kriyākauśalam īdṛśam ।। kā hi durlabham ātmānaṃ kitavaiḥ paribhāvayet ।। upāyair durnivartyaiva prāṇāmaśapathādibhiḥ ।। naukeva pratikūlāśu kuśalaiḥ parivartyate ।।
yadi vipratyayaḥ kaścid bhartāraṃ kiṃ na paśyasi ।। tat kṛtaṃ durvidagdhena yena bhāryaiva roṣitā ।। sutarāṃ tena tenāsya daurbhāgyam upacīyate ।। mā ciraṃ putrakāḥ sthāta bhāryājñātigṛheṣv iti ।।
asnigdhasmitayā hā hā kim etad iti bhāṣitam ।। anayaṃ vepamānāṅgīm āliṅgyotsaṅgam aṅganām ।। aryaputra prasīdeti vyāharat tāram āturā ।। paritaḥ sphuritasphītamaṇḍalāgrāṃśumaṇḍalam ।।
te paśyata iyaṃ kāntā hriyate dhriyatām iti ।। saṃbhāvitasvasāreṇa mayāsāv iti bhartsitaḥ ।। kāko api hi nabhaścārī na ca muñcati nīcatām ।। na tena paribhūtaḥ syāt kesarī dharaṇīcaraḥ ।।
paritaś cakitaḥ paśyan sāvajñānam ivābravīt ।। tvādṛśe mādṛśaḥ krudhyan kena pāpān na śocyatām ।। bhuvaḥ śyena iva śyāmām ādāyodapatad divam ।। āpatantīṃ divaṃ devīm utpātolkām ivāśivām ।।
mahākālam iva kruddhaṃ gaṇāmaragaṇānugam ।। anyatraiva gataḥ kvāpi diṅmohamuṣitasmṛtiḥ ।। cirād ākarṇito dhīrād uccakair uccaran dhvaniḥ ।। vatsalānāṃ vivatsānāṃ rambhaś ca subhago gavām ।।
kulatthasthūlapulakam urujaṅghoruvistṛtam ।। vegavaccarpaṭātāḍakiṇakarkaśakarṇakam ।। bhraṣṭaḥ panthā mamāṭavyāṃ tam ākhyātu bhavān iti ।। prage draṣṭā svapanthānaṃ tadeta svagṛhān iti ।।
mandramanthadhvanikṣiptamandarāsphālitārṇavam ।। haridgomayasaṃmārgasaṃprasāritamānasāḥ ।। yatra nābhīranārīṇāṃ paribhūtaṃ karādharam ।। lajjitāḥ paṅkajinyo api kalikāṅgulitārjitāḥ ।।
niravācyatalā rathyāḥ kūrdaduddāmatarṇakāḥ ।। sa tādṛṅmalinaḥ strīṇāṃ yatra veṣo vibhūṣitaḥ ।। gopyas tu caturācārānaṭīr apy atiśerate ।। māṃ gopaḥ svagṛhaṃ nītvā gṛhiṇīm āhvayan mudā ।।
devas te gṛham āyātaḥ sa bhaktyārādhyatām iti ।। gṛhān niragamad gaurī prakīrṇatanucandrikā ।। na tāṃ vedhāḥ kṣamaḥ sraṣṭuṃ madhūcchiṣṭamayīm api ।। na tāṃ varṇayituṃ śaktau vyāsavālmīkināv api ।।
āśiraḥpādam aśrāntā saṃvāhitavatī ciram ।। sarvam anvasahe taṃ taṃ dākṣiṇyakṣayaśaṅkayā ।। sottamāṅgeṣu cāṅgeṣu navanītam adān mudā ।। lodhrakarbūramustābhir ghṛṣṭo ahaṃ snapitas tayā ।।
vipāpmānam ivātmānam amanye madyapāyinam ।। etat te gṛham ity uktvā aṃsabhāro vrajam avrajat ।। sakleśaḥ ko nu viśvasyād dāreṣu ca pareṣu ca ।। tiraścām api dṛśyante prakāśamaraṇā raṇāḥ ।।
mayi nikṣipya yātīti vyakta eṣa sa puṃgavaḥ ।। nārītantreṣu tantreṣu kim ācāraparīkṣayā ।। dṛśyante yāḥ sadācārāḥ sā tāsāṃ bālaśīlatā ।। evaṃ gambhīradhairyeti durbodhāḥ parabuddhayaḥ ।।
sadyaḥ kāntākaṇṭhaviśleṣaduḥkham ārāt sahyaṃ cetasā yan na soḍham ।। ghorāt kāntārasaṃsārād acirad udatārayat ।। dṛśyante yasya sīmāntāḥ sīramantaḥ sasaṃkaṭāḥ ।। iti mām idam uktvāsau nivṛttaḥ kṛtabandhanaḥ ।।
sevamānaḥ prayāmi sma saṃtapto bhānubhānubhiḥ ।। sthalīr iva nidāghānte phullāviralakandarāḥ ।। sagundrāgahanānīva palvalāni vilokayan ।। kṛtahaṃsadvijātīryaiḥ sarobhiḥ prīṇitekṣaṇaḥ ।।
kṛṣṭair ākṛṣṭadṛṣṭiś ca jāhnavīpulinair iva ।। gacchan puruṣam adrākṣaṃ grāmād āyāntam antike ।। citram āryakaniṣṭhasya yūyaṃ susadṛśā iti ।। na hi tasmād ṛte kaścid asti matsadṛśaḥ kṣitau ।।
kīdṛśā vā vinodena gamayed divasān iti ।। asti sādhāraṇārthārthaḥ priyavādī prasannakaḥ ।। āgataḥ katamād deśāt kim arthaṃ vā bhavān iti ।। bhrātarau sa ca me jyeṣṭho yātrāyām anyato gataḥ ।।
chāttrāṇām atra sarveṣām upapannaḥ samāgamaḥ ।। yena yenātra vaḥ kāryaṃ tat tad ādīyatām iti ।। trastabhṛtyakṛtārādho durvāsovad vasaty asau ।। yanmātraṃ tu vijānāmi tanmātraṃ kathayāmi vaḥ ।।
ācāryā api vidyāsu tasyaiva chāttratāṃ gatāḥ ।। viśvakarmātha vā brahmā kasmān nāyam upāsitaḥ ।। utkaṇṭhaḥ sarvataḥ paśyañ jīmūtam iva cātakaḥ ।। akālakaumudī grāme sahasā jṛmbhatām iti ।।
ūrdhvacūḍaḥ sa vegena prati grāmam adhāvata ।। utthitas toṣanirghoṣas tālasaṃpātasaṃkulaḥ ।। dūrād eva yathādīrgham apatan mama pādayoḥ ।। janyate janitā prītis tena me suhṛdā yathā ।।
āliṅgya sahitas tena saṃbhavagrāmam āsadam ।। grāmīṇā janatā yāntam aṅgulībhir adarśayat ।। kṛtāsukarasatkāraḥ prerayaṃ divasaṃ kṣaṇam ।। nītavantaḥ kathaṃ yūyam iyato divasān iti ।।
pṛṣṭaḥ svavṛtta ācaṣṭa gomukhaḥ priyavistaraḥ ।। pratibuddhān na cāpaśyaṃ pāṇḍāv api divākare ।। hā śūnyam iti sākrandā nirgatā vāsamandirāt ।। vindhyākāśadiśaś caṇḍam āraṭann iva pīḍitāḥ ।।
ādityaśarmaṇā lokaḥ siddhādeśena vāritaḥ ।। na hy adarśanamātreṇa bhānoḥ saṃbhāvyate cyutiḥ ।। brahmajātir ivāvadhyā sa kasmād duḥsthatām iyāt ।। paścād vārttopalambhāya viyad ālocyatām iti ।।
utkaṇṭhāviṣayād anyat kiṃ sotkaṇṭhāya rocate ।। vicchinnābhralavākāraṃ kim apy aikṣanta pūrvataḥ ।। tāvad āsannam adrākṣaṃ puro amitagatiṃ divaḥ ।। vegavattanayāṃ devīṃ yāntīm antaḥpuraṃ prati ।।
diṣṭyāmitagatiḥ prāptaḥ prītyā saṃbhāvyatām iti ।। vidyādharo manuṣyeṇa satā saṃmānyatām iti ।। tayāmitagatir dṛṣṭyā viśrabdhaṃ dṛśyatām iti ।। prasāritabhujaḥ prahvam āmṛśat pṛṣṭhamūrdhani ।।
āhūtaḥ punar ādiṣṭam adhyāstānuccam āsanam ।। bhrātuḥ kathaya vṛttāntam iti tenoditaṃ tataḥ ।। pātito andhatame kūpe svavīryāc cotthitas tataḥ ।। iyaṃ matsahitāgatya gatā rājāvarodhanam ।।
sukhaṃ tiṣṭhati mā bhūt tad viśaṅkā bhavatām iti ।। sa mayā sahito gatvā devyau dūrād avandata ।। vistareṇa sakhe mahyaṃ bhartur vṛttaṃ nivedyatām ।। yathābhinnarahasyānām aśaṅkaiḥ suhṛdām iti ।।
na hīdaṃ śakyam ākhyātuṃ na śrotuṃ prasthitair iti ।। āsīnāya sa me vṛttaṃ yuṣmadvṛttam avartayat ।। tenaiva ca kṛtānujñaḥ prāyām aṅgārakaṃ prati ।। balavatsaṃśrayāt kena durbalena na bhīyate ।।
avasaṃ divasān etān kadācit kāśyapasthale ।। sa ca gatvā mayā dṛṣṭas tiṣṭhann avaṭasaṃkaṭe ।। yudhyāmānāṃ saha bhrātrā rakṣa vegavatīm iti ।। utkhātanijarāgeva yoginīcakravartinī ।।
bhrātaḥ prajñaptim āvartya svāmī vijñāyatām iti ।। bhavane dattakasyāste tatra saṃbhāvyatām iti ।। prāvṛḍjaḍam ivāmbhodaṃ samīraṇaparaṃparā ।। dṛṣṭavān mānuṣādṛśyāṃ devīṃ devasya saṃnidhau ।।
