jagatpatim ivānantabhujaṅgotsaṅgaśāyinam ।। rūpaṃ gandharvadattāyāḥ kīdṛg ity ucyatām iti ।। paśyāmitagate bhartur ācāram iti bhāṣitam ।। sadyo vikasitaṃ bhartur devyās tu mlānam ānanam ।।
yena gandharvadattāyārūpam eṣa praśaṃsati ।। dūre gandharvadattāstāṃ rambhām api na varṇayet ।। bahu śrotavyam atrāsti nipuṇaṃ śrūyatām iti ।। priyāṃ vegavatīṃ prāpya yat satyaṃ vismṛtaiva me ।।
adrākṣaṃ vikasantīva tuṅgībhūtais tanūruhaiḥ ।। yāvannāparam etena kiṃcid durvaca ucyate ।। viṣatoyalaveneva dugdhakuṇḍam urūdaram ।। devaḥ saṃcintya tāvatyā paścād ūhitavān idam ।।
tṛtīyāyās tatha prāptyā dvitīyā vismariṣyate ।। apurāṇeṣu rajyante svabhāvād eva jantavaḥ ।। prasahya svīkariṣyāmi kṛṣṇām iva dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। dṛṣṭyā dṛṣṭiviṣasyeva niśceṣṭā vasudhām agāt ।।
pratīkāraśatāvadhyaṃ vṛttāntaṃ taṃ na bodhitaḥ ।। vandamānā guroḥ pādān kṣapayāmi śarīrakam ।। rājadvāre śmaśāne vā yas tiṣṭhati sa bāndhavaḥ ।। duḥkhādhikaraṇaṃ tan me śarīraṃ dahyatām iti ।।
kva cāsadṛśam etat te vadanān nirgataṃ vacaḥ ।। tato naiva virudhyeran nātmānair ātmyavādibhiḥ ।। mustāgranthipramāṇena tad viṣeṇaiva labhyate ।। dharmādhikaraṇaṃ devi śarīraṃ pālyatām iti ।।
nanu saṃhara dārūṇi kiṃ cireṇeti bhāṣitam ।। aham eva tataḥ pūrvaṃ praviśāmi citām iti ।। mām anumriyamāṇas tvam ucyase kiṃ janair iti ।। jīvitaṃ tu mahādoṣaṃ tathā ca śrūyatāṃ kathā ।।
cittam ākṣiptavān asmi kathākanthāṃ prasārayan ।। badarīkhadiraprāyakāntāratarudurgamaḥ ।। durgarājaṃ yam āśritya rājabhyo api na bibhyati ।। goṣṭhaśvā iva gāyante mattā mṛgayudantinaḥ ।।
payaḥśvetapayaḥpūrair nirvāpayati jāhnavī ।। bilaṃ kṛtvā śatadvāram uvāsa kila mūṣika ।। sa bhṛtyān bibharām āsa vaikhānasa ivāśrame ।। gṛham asyāgaman mitram ākhur nagaragocaraḥ ।।
tām apṛcchat kva yāto naḥ sakhā sakhi bhaved iti ।। ayam āyāti te bhrātā sumuhūrtam udīkṣyatām ।। nidrāhārābhilāṣābhyāṃ saptarātraṃ viyujyate ।। nirātithyaś ca yāmīti vṛṣas tvam aviṣāṇakaḥ ।।
dhūmair dhūsarito bhānuḥ svarbhānutimirair iva ।। apavanta nabhasvanto gaṅgātāṇḍavahetavaḥ ।। laṅghitodbhrāntaśārdūlāḥ prādhāvann abhi jāhnavīm ।। apagantum upakrāntas tayā saṃbhrāntayoditaḥ ।।
mahāsāhasam ārabdham ātmānaṃ yena rakṣatā ।। ātmārthe sakalāṃ jahyāt paṇḍitaḥ pṛthivīm iti ।। śarīranirapekṣeṇa svaguṇā iva rakṣitāḥ ।। dāvadāhabhayād bālān paritrāyasva putrakān ।।
pañcarātraprasūtatvāt saṃcārayitum akṣamā ।। tuṅgagaṅgātaṭīṃ yena saṃcāraya sutān iti ।। muṣikām avakarṇyaiva gaṅgārodhaḥ parāgamat ।। utthitaḥ paritaḥ kacchaṃ paṭuḥ paṭapaṭādhvaniḥ ।।
sarvaṃ jvālāc chalenāṅgaṃ jihvāmayam ivābhavat ।। dagdhvā nirindhanaḥ śāntaḥ prāpya gaṅgātaṭāmbaram ।। kṣaṇena dadṛśe kacchaḥ prāṃśuvalmīkasaṃkulaḥ ।। anumāya cirāc cihnair ājagāma svam ālayam ।।
jvālāvyatikaroṣṇābhir utsvinnāṃ dhūmavartibhiḥ ।। dīrghanidrām upāsīnām asaṃmīlitalocanān ।। vilāpaikavinodā hi bandhuvyasanapīḍitāḥ ।। mahābhūtena bhūtāṅge bhavatā kim idaṃ kṛtam ।।
na punar yat tvayā pāpa duṣkaraṃ duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ।। śaraṇāgatabālastrīkṛtahatyās tu duḥkṣayāḥ ।। daśajanmasahasrāṇi tasmād ākhur bhaviṣyasi ।। tam eva capalaṃ yena sarvabhakṣaḥ kṛto bhavān ।।
mūṣikair aparaiḥ sārdham alīkam avadad vacaḥ ।। mayi prārthayamāne api kuṭumbam avasāditam ।। gaṅgākūlaṃ tribhir vāraiḥ śāvakān nayatām iti ।। apāyaśatadarśinyaḥ svacchavṛtte api buddhayaḥ ।।
nīlāviralaparṇāś ca jambūvañjularājayaḥ ।। so atidūreṇa vicchinnaḥ katham asmān dahed iti ।। evam uktaḥ prajāvatyā bhavān kiṃ kṛtavān iti ।। niṣpratyāśas tadā prāṇān ahaṃ rakṣitavān iti ।।
ākhur anyatamas teṣāṃ tam asādhum abhāṣata ।। rakṣatā sutyajān prāṇāṃs tyaktā yad dustyajā guṇāḥ ।। mīmāṃsitvā ciraṃ devāḥ sāmyam eṣām akalpayan ।। taraṃgataralāḥ prāṇāguṇā merusthirā iti ।।
ayaśomaraṇāt trastāyaśojīvā hi sādhavaḥ ।। ahaṃ jīvita ity etat ko brūyān mūṣikād ṛte ।। kuṭumbaṃ cāsya saṃskṛtya pratijagmur yathāgatam ।। āsanasthānasaṃbhāṣāsaṃbhogair varjitaḥ kṛtaḥ ।।
akṣatāṅgaḥ svayaṃ mandaḥ kiṃ vakṣyāmi puraḥ prabhoḥ ।। sādhubhir varjyamānasya naṣṭam etac catuṣṭayam ।। aṅgīkṛtam alaṃ prāṇair akīrtimalinair iti ।। tāvad āvām anuprāptāv āsthānaṃ bhavatām iti ।।
prītaḥ prītaṃ mahīpālaṃ praṇipatya tiro abhavat ।। tantreṇa saha gacchantu campāṃ hariśikhādayaḥ ।। pānthasyevāsahāyasya purādhiṣṭhānavāsinaḥ ।। tāvanty eva sahasrāṇi tādṛśām eva vājinām ।।
pattirakṣyā hi mātaṅgāḥ karmaṇyāḥ samareṣv iti ।। tantreṇa sāhitān asmān prāhiṇod yuṣmadantikam ।। ākrāmantaḥ prayāmaḥ sma svacchaśailasarijjalām ।। dhvanatpaṭahaśṛṅgaṃ ca cauracakram upāgatam ।।
dṛṣṭaḥ pulīndrabhāvena vindhyaḥ pariṇamann iva ।। saṃtatair vayam ākrāntāḥ śalabhair iva śālayaḥ ।। pratyakṣam api yad dṛṣṭaṃ na kaścit samabhāvayat ।। parāvṛtya parān eva parāghnanparamārgaṇāḥ ।।
tasya bāhusahasraṃ tu phalena samabhāvyata ।। tadvisṛṣṭān apaśyāma yugapat patataḥ śarān ।। dṛṣṭaḥ sarveṇa sarveṣāṃ pulīndrāṇāṃ puraḥ sthitaḥ ।। tadāsannavimānasthair dṛṣṭam apsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ ।।
kṛtabrahmāstramokṣeṇa droṇenāpi na yaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। niṣprayojanayatnena sve pare copahāsitāḥ ।। nīhāranikareṇeva bhāsvatkarakadambakam ।। dṛḍhaṃ marmaṇi bāṇena matturaṃgam atāḍayat ।।
sthāṇupāṣāṇagartāṃś ca yathāvegam adhāvata ।। sthita evāmucat prāṇān paścāt kāyam apātayat ।। tasyānuṣthitavān asmi saṃskāraṃ sodakakriyam ।। etaṃ grāmakam adrākṣam ārād ākulagokulam ।।
yathā gurur yathā devo yathā rājā yathāv varaḥ ।। iti mahyam iyaṃ vārttā kathitā pathikair iti ।। sarvendriyārthajanitāni hi sevyamānā dīrghāsvavṛttir iva hanti sukhāni nidrā ।। māsam āsiṣi vipraiś ca prasannaiḥ saprasannakaiḥ ।।
avimuktāvimuktatvāt puṇyā vārāṇasī purī ।। tat sarvaṃ sulabhaṃ tasyāṃ manohārivinodanam ।। vārttā hariśikhādīnām ataḥ sāgamyatām iti ।। sākrandāt saṃbhavagrāmāt prati vārāṇasīm agām ।।
vahāni kim ahaṃ yuṣmān yūyaṃ vahata mām iti ।। yūyaṃ māṃ vahatety eṣa no brūyāt katham anyathā ।। ariṣṭāviṣṭatāṃ muktvā katham itthaṃ sa vakṣyati ।। tan madīyam aśaṅkena pṛṣṭham āruhyatām iti ।।
neyaṃ saṃbhāvyate cintā jātāriṣṭe api mādṛśi ।। voḍhā bhavati tasyāsau khedavismaraṇād iti ।। ākhyātuṃ ca vijānāti yat tataḥ kathayatv iti ।। dharmārthasukhanirvāṇacikitsāḥ sahavistarāḥ ।।
prabhavaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ jagatī jagatām iva ।। sarvārthānām asau hetur guṇānām iva sajjanaḥ ।। nātisaktiś ca dāreṣu sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ viparyayaḥ ।। saṃbandhābhāvam atyantaṃ nirvāṇaṃ vidur īśvarāḥ ।।
kūṭavaidyaparityāgī rogair dūreṇa varjyate ।। asāro gurusārāṇi darśanāni viḍambayet ।। śukavāśitaniḥsāram idaṃ me mṛṣyatām iti ।। gaṅgābharaṇam ākhyātāṃ prāpaṃ vārāṇasīṃ tataḥ ।।
jaraddārusudhācitram adhyatiṣṭhāma maṇḍapam ।। muhūrtakam anutkaṇṭhair iha yuṣmābhir āsyatām ।। āgacchāmīti mām uktvā calair uccalitaḥ padaiḥ ।। tataḥ kim api niścitya nivṛtto mām abhāṣata ।।
idam ādāya gacchāmi sthātuṃ nāsyeha yujyate ।। vārāṇasī mahācaurais tīrthadhvāṅkṣair adhiṣṭhitā ।। teṣāṃ sāhasikaḥ kaścid anarthaṃ cintayed iti ।। tadābharaṇam ādāya prāviśat tvaritaḥ puram ।।
paricaṅkramaṇaśrāntau tasminn eva nyasīdatām ।। nirāyudhāsahāyaṃ māṃ muṣituṃ kila vāñchataḥ ।। gavām ivodviṣāṇānāṃ matir me mantharādarā ।। prayuṅkte nirghṛṇaḥ śastraṃ ko anyaḥ klībatamas tataḥ ।।
nirāśa iva vidrāṇo brahmacāriṇam uktavān ।। vipralabdhāḥ sukhaṃ tyaktvā mokṣamārge kila sthitāḥ ।। kaścin mahat tapaḥ kuryān mokṣārtho nas tathā śramaḥ ।। atha khāmbojaduṣprāpas tato naṣṭā mumukṣavaḥ ।।
sarvajñasyāpi sadbhāvaḥ pañcadivyapramāṇakaḥ ।। so apy asiddhaviruddhādidoṣāśīviṣadūṣitaḥ ।। sevamānā yathācchandam āsmahe viṣayān iti ।। prasāritas tvayā kasmād asāro malladaṇḍakaḥ ।।
sarvatantrāviruddhena siddhāntenaiva bādhyase ।। vitaṇḍāvādavārttārtaḥ sādhu śocyo bhaviṣyasi ।। smṛtīnāṃ viṭakāvyatvaṃ kathaṃ veda bhavān iti ।। nandīśapramukhair uktam ahaṃ jānāmi lakṣaṇam ।।
eṣa vidyādharendrāṇām indraḥ kila bhaviṣyati ।। malladaṇḍakaniḥsārān utprekṣe sakalāgamān ।। arthavanto anumīyante yācakair iva dāyakāḥ ।। śrutismṛtipurāṇādi tathā saṃbhāvyatām iti ।।
iṣṭāniṣṭaphalaṃ karma daivam āhur vicakṣaṇāḥ ।। etad daivābhidhānasya lakṣaṇaṃ pūrvakarmaṇaḥ ।। kālakāraṇasāmagrīm īśvaro api hy apekṣate ।। kuṇṭhayā gaṇḍamaṇḍānāṃ mandaceṣṭatayā samaḥ ।।
sattāmātraphalaṃ puṃsas tathā daivam apauruṣam ।। jñāpakaṃ cāsya pakṣasya śrūyatāṃ yan mayā śrutam ।। tatrāsīd vedaśarmeti caturvedo dvijottamaḥ ।। tasmād eva ca sa chātrair āhūyata dṛḍhodyamaḥ ।।
dāpitaṃ bhojanaṃ tasya ācchādanaṃ vedaśarmaṇā ।। vāsam āvasathe tasya karoti sma dṛḍhodyamaḥ ।। adhītaṃ daśabhir varṣais tena vedacatuṣṭayam ।। praśāntajanasaṃpāte pradoṣe tam abhāṣata ।।
tantrasthānam upāntaṃ ca cāṭādibhyaś ca rakṣitam ।। vaiśyakarmābhiyuktasya tasya nāmāpi nāsti me ।। paralokasamāsannā jarātandrīr ivāgatā ।। dharmasādhanam uddiṣṭam ṛṣibhis tīrthasevanam ।।
etasmān na vimuñceyur avimuktaṃ mumukṣavaḥ ।। buddhadharme praśastā hi dharmasya tvaritā gatiḥ ।। niyogenaiva kartavyaḥ patnīputraparigrahaḥ ।। na ca pratigrahād anyad viprasya dhanasādhanam ।।
sadāsīdāsam asmākaṃ dhanam ādīyatām iti ।। na vikalpayituṃ śaktaḥ kiṃ punar nyāyyam īdṛśam ।। kartāsmi bhavadādeśam ativāhya niśām iti ।। saṃpratiṣṭhāsamāno api ciraṃ bhikṣur udaikṣata ।।
taṃ gaveṣayituṃ bhikṣuḥ svayam eva tadā gataḥ ।। śanaiś caṅkramaṇaṃ kurvan nīcaiś cāmnāyamānasam ।। athārthenaiva tenārthas tathā naḥ kathyatām iti ।। vyagraḥ parijanaḥ sarvas tatra tatrābhidhāvati ।।
sā sā mām āha saṃrabdhā śivaṃ dhyātu bhavān iti ।। tenāhaṃ nāgataḥ kṣipraṃ sakāśaṃ bhavatām iti ।। yenāyam ākulo lokas tad ahaṃ kathayāmi te ।। ayaṃ parijanas tatra tatratatrākulākulaḥ ।।
sā ca rāgagrahāviṣṭā duṣṭaceṣṭā bhaviṣyati ।। itaraś cintayām āsa śaṅkākampitamānasaḥ ।। tato bhinnatamovākyam abhūtārthaṃ na jāyate ।। śeṣāṇām api mantrāṇāṃ sāmarthyam anumīyate ।।
hā daivaṃ khalam ityādi lapan nīcair vinirgataḥ ।। antarbhavanam udbhūtaḥ śvāgāraparuṣaśrutiḥ ।। pakṣadvāreṇa nirjagmur nairāśyottānapāṇayaḥ ।। amantrayata vāmasya vidheḥ kiṃ kriyatām iti ।।
siddhapravrajitādeśajātabhītir acintayat ।। daivaṃ puruṣakāreṇa janāḥ paśyantu bādhitam ।। sindhudeśaṃ parityajya de।ād deśaṃ parivrajan ayaṃ pariharāmy enāṃ dūrataḥ kardamām iti ।।
daśayojanam adhvānam ekāhena palāyitaḥ ।। gaṅgātaṭam upāgacchat tīrthopāsanakāmyayā ।। kasmiṃścid brāhmaṇagrāme kaṃcana prāviśad gṛham ।। yayāce brāhmaṇīm amba pānīyaṃ dāpyatām iti ।।
āsanodakam ādāya laghu nirgamyatām iti ।। āpiṅgāpāntakeśāntā kanyakā niragād gṛhāt ।। paṅgubhaṅgurasaṃcārā cirāt prāpad dṛḍhodyamam ।। pīṭhabuddhyā puras tasya nikṣiptaṃ jalabhājanam ।।
apareṇodapātreṇa jalam āvarjyatām iti ।। antarhasitabhugnauṣṭhī vṛddhājñāṃ samapādayat ।। āgacchati kuto deśāt kaṃ vā yāti bhavān iti ।। yac ca brūtha kva yāsīti tatra viñāpayāmi vaḥ ।।
saṃtuṣṭo grāmavāsobhir ninīṣe divasān iti ।। na hy ataptena lohena taptaṃ saṃdhīyate kvacit ।। tau ca saṃyojitau puṇyair arthināv arthinā tvayā ।। naṣṭāśvadagdharathavadyogo astu bhavatām iti ।।
antevāsigaṇaṃ cānyam asthāt saṃvatsaradvayam ।। kasmād dṛḍhodyamāyeyaṃ dīyate na tamālikā ।। dṛḍhodyame punaḥ paśya yadi kaṃcin na paśyasi ।। kena vanyaḥ karī vārīm āgataḥ svayam ujjhitaḥ ।।
yady evaṃ svayam evāyaṃ pūjyair abhyarthyatām iti ।। āmnātāś cāvabuddhāś ca vedāḥ sasmṛtayas tvayā ।। uraḥkaṇṭhauṣṭhaśoṣasya mā bhūd vaiphalyam anyathā ।। jyeṣṭhaṃ jyeṣṭhāśramasyāṅgaṃ trayī vidyeva dehinī ।।
yuktaṃ yad brāhmaṇair uktam atra tāvat kim ucyate ।। pāre sāgaravat so api dūratvāt sudurāgamaḥ ।। sūcīsūtragate daivāt tataḥ kaḥ kutra mokṣyate ।। pariṇīya ca tāṃ kanyāṃ saṃvatsaram ayāpayat ।।
jṛmbhāveditanidrāntāṃ pṛcchati sma tamālikām ।। keyaṃ bhavati te vṛddhā kāv etau baṭukāv iti ।। srutāśrukaṇikāśreṇyā kathitaṃ skhaladakṣaram ।। yasya vidyādhanais tṛptāḥ śiṣyayājakayācakāḥ ।।
duhitā gṛhajāmātre chāttrāya pratipāditā ।। sa jāmātṛtayā krodhād gamitaḥ kṛṣṇasarpatām ।। śvaśrūśvaśurayoḥ khedam ātmanaś cākarod vṛthā ।। durvāsaḥsadṛśas tāta durārādho bhavān iti ।।
ity uktvā mantharālāpaḥ sadāro gata eva saḥ ।। nirapekṣaṃ svadeśāya sindhudeśāya yātavān ।। acirān nityakāmyāni karmāṇi niravartayat ।। yamau ca tanayau jātau yamakālau kulasya yau ।।
yair mātāpitarāv eva bālair eva samāhitau ।। durvāragurupūreṇa sahasākṛṣya nīyate ।। mātāmahagṛhaṃ yāntu bālā me niviśantv iti ।। śeṣaṃ sujñānam evāsyāḥ kathāyāḥ sthīyatām iti ।।
sphuṭaṃ bhinnatamā eva bhinnājñānatamā yataḥ ।। tṛtīyaparihārāya tyajāmi pṛthivīm iti ।। nirviṇṇaś cintayām āsa kiṃcid dhavalamūrdhajaḥ ।। kālenaitāvatā nūnam akṛtyaṃ kṛtyayā kṛtam ।।
vraṇair iva visarpadbhiḥ kvāpītaṃ puruṣāyuṣam ।। puṇyaṃ svargaphalaṃ kurvann ayāmi divasān iti ।। tato vārāṇasīṃ prāpad amuñcann eva jāhnavīm ।। skhaladālāpasaṃcāraṃ mahāpāśupataṃ puraḥ ।।
madirātāmrajihmākṣāṃ vicitragalakaṇṭhikām ।। amuktanijanirmokāṃ bhujaṃgīm iva yoṣitam ।। na yāvad avimuktasya dhūpavelātivartate ।। tataḥ śuṇḍikaśāleṣu mārgayāmi surām iti ।।
papāta pādayos tasya tārākrandā kapālinī ।। parihāsaś ciraṃ caṇḍi viruddhas tyajyatām iti ।। tvaṃ tu dhṛṣṭaviṭo bhūtvā kiṃ vyāharasi mām iti ।। janair agaṇitair vyāptaḥ śramaṇabrāhmaṇādibhiḥ ।।
savedaḥ ko hi nirvedaṃ vedoktaiḥ karmabhir vrajet ।। nārcitāḥ pitaraḥ piṇḍair vāyubhūtena hiṇḍitam ।। kulāt kulam aṭantīdaṃ carāmi kulaṭāvratam ।। yair aduṣṭāḥ striyo dṛṣṭās te dṛṣṭāḥ kenacit kvacit ।।
tān eva bharamāṇena tat samucchidyatām iti ।। bhagavatyā yad uktaṃ tat tattvataḥ kathyatām iti ।। brahmasthalakavāsādi yad vṛttaṃ tan niveditam ।। raktadāraparityāgam ācaranti na sādhavaḥ ।।
tasya kṛcchratamaiḥ kṛcchrair viśuddhiḥ kriyatām iti ।। pūjyānām eva tad buddham idaṃ budhyata yādṛśam ।। iyaṃ tv aśubhasāvarṇaṃ yam upāste sa dṛśyatām ।। sukhānāṃ copahartāraṃ mahāpāśupataṃ patim ।।
ā mṛtyos tvatsamīpasthā nayāmi divasān iti ।। madīyā duhitā brahman rūpiṇī pariṇīyatām ।। tatas tasya ca tasyāś ca bhaved bhartā bhavān iti ।। parivrājakavākyaṃ hi kṛtārthīkṛtam etayā ।।
samahādraviṇaskandhām upayeme dṛḍhodyamaḥ ।। dṛḍhodyamagṛhāsannā vasatī kālam akṣipat ।। harottamāṅgalālitām upāsta jahnukanyakām ।। śūreṇa daivahariṇā prabhuṇā prasahya tasmāj jitaḥ puruṣakāragajādhirājaḥ ।।
yathā puruṣakārasya prādhānyaṃ tan niśāmyatām ।। vaṇik sāgaradattākhyaḥ sāgarāgādhamānasaḥ ।। aparaḥ prekṣitaḥ potas taraladhvajalakṣaṇaḥ ।। yāvan niryāmakān āha tāvat potau samīyatuḥ ।।
yūyaṃ ye vā yatas tyā vā tan naḥ pratyucyatām iti ।। bhavantaḥ ke kuto veti tataḥ so api nyavedayat ।। savinodau jagāhāte tau durgādhaṃ mahodadhim ।। prāptavantau parāvṛtya samudrataṭapattanam ।।
prītir naḥ sthiratāṃ yāyād yathā saṃpādyatāṃ tathā ।। tasyāś ca divasir ebhir jātam anyatarad dvayoḥ ।। putraś cet tvaṃ tatas tasmai dadyāḥ svatanayām iti ।। atha vā kim ihāścaryam ekam evāvayor vapuḥ ।।
mahāmahiṣasārthābhyāṃ yathāsthānam agacchatām ।। tatprayuktātisatkārau yayatuḥ svagṛhān prati ।। bandhubhir brāhmaṇādīṃś ca gamayām āsatur dinam ।। utsaṅge dārikā nyastā virājatkundamālikā ।।
sāpi kasyāparasyeti śanair ācaṣṭa lajjitā ।। yayoḥ syād īdṛśaḥ putraḥ pitarau tau saputrakau ।। na kīrtijananī vidyā nindyā bhavitum arhati ।। buddhavarmasakhitvaṃ ca tasyai kathitavān asau ।।
prasiddhā tasya nāmnāpi sā tataḥ kundamālikā ।। tasmin garbhe tavotpannaṃ yat tan naḥ kathyatām iti ।। lambauṣṭhaṃ bhugnapṛṣṭhaṃ ca sā taṃ putraṃ samarpayat ।। kasmād īkṣaṇikāṃ pṛṣṭvā garbha eva na pātitaḥ ।।
vikṛtākṛtinānena sa pretena nirākṛtaḥ ।। tadā kiṃ pratisaṃdeśyaṃ mayāhaṃ putravān iti ।। enaṃ kurubhakaṃ tasmai na kaścit kathayed iti ।। vyāharanti sma taṃ paurās tataḥ kurubhakākhyayā ।।
lekhaṃ sāgaradattena prasthāpitam avācayat ।। ujjayanyāḥ pariṣvajya vijñāpayati sāgaraḥ ।। rūpeṇa sadṛśī yasyāḥ pramadā na bhaviṣyati ।। kanyā ced vāmaśīlena devena muṣitā vayam ।।
śrīr utsāhasanātheva prayāti sthiratām iti ।। tasminn evaṃ gate kārye brūhi kiṃ kriyatām iti ।। kiṃ tu pṛṣṭeti vakṣyāmi pṛṣṭadhṛṣṭā hi mādṛśī ।। sahajaṃ hi tyajan vṛttaṃ durvṛtta iti nindyate ।।
ye punas tasya doṣās tān mithyā bhaṇa guṇā iti ।। āhur madhurakaṃ kecit taṃ tādṛṅmārakaṃ viṣam ।। aśvatthāmā hato drauṇir ity ūce kiṃ na pāṇḍavaḥ ।। krīḍākamalinīṃ yānti tvadvidhāḥ kṣārasāgare ।।
na vināmbhodhisāreṇa praveṣṭā dhanarāśinā ।। kṛcchrāyāsaśataprāpyāṃ na kṛcchrādhigatām iti ।। dadau sāgaradattāya saṃdeśaṃ dūtasaṃnidhau ।। utpannas tādṛśo yasya kathitā katham ākṛtiḥ ।।
svayam evāsi tān dṛṣṭā kiṃ nas taiḥ kathitair iti ।। dūtaṃ prasthāpayām āsa sapātheyapradeśanam ।। atha dūtaḥ sphuṭālāpo buddhavarmāṇam uktavān ।। jāmātaram anālokya mā smāgacchad bhavān iti ।।
taṃ me dārakam ākhyāta tadīyāṃś ca guṇān iti ।। āste mātulaśāle asau tāmraliptyāṃ paṭhann iti ।। atha tricaturāḥ prāpur dūtāś caturabhāṣiṇaḥ ।। āha saṃbandhinī yat tvāṃ sadāraṃ tan niśāmyatām ।।
adyāpi ca na paśyāmo vayaṃ jāmātur ākṛtim ।। iti lokapravādo ayaṃ bhavatāpi na kiṃ śrutaḥ ।। idam apy atidurbaddhaṃ savyājam iva vācakam ।। teṣām api paricchinnaḥ pāṭhakālaḥ kiyān api ।।
paṭhatā sakalaṃ janma neyam ity asamañjasam ।। atra vā tāmraliptyāṃ vā dārako darśyatām iti ।। tān uktvā gṛhiṇīm ūce buddhavarmā sasaṃbhramaḥ ।। dūrāśāgrastacittena pramadāvacanaṃ kṛtam ।।
kālenaitāvatā teṣāṃ katamaḥ prakṣayaṃ gataḥ ।। sutarām upacīyante śarīrāvayavā iva ।। atha vā paṇḍitenaivam upāyaś cintyatām iti ।। yady asau rocate tubhyaṃ tataḥ prastūyatām iti ।।
so api śobhanam ity uktvā tam upāyaṃ prayuktavān ।। priyālāpaśataprītam ayācata sadīnataḥ ।। ākāraś ca prakāraś ca yādṛk kiṃ tasya kathyate ।। buddhaṃ tad bhavataḥ sarvaṃ sahadūtasamāgamam ।।
atha vā svārtha evāyaṃ tava dhiṅ māṃ mudhākulam ।। śrutismṛtyāditattvajñaḥ kalāsu ca viśāradaḥ ।। tādṛśīm eva cānīya matputrāya prayacchatu ।। tasyāṃśas tava bhāvīti lajjate kathayānayā ।।
abravīt tvadvidheyaiḥ kiṃ madvidhaiḥ prārthitair iti ।। pitā śrāvitavān etaṃ vṛttāntaṃ pūrvamantritam ।। śiśubhir na vicāryāṇi tasmād evaṃ bhavatv iti ।। yajñaguptaḥ svalaṃkāraḥ saṃbandhibhyaḥ pradarśitaḥ ।।
ākāraś ca guṇāś cāsya dṛśyantāṃ yādṛśā iti ।। saha bālavasantena yad anena sameṣyati ।। dṛśyate nirguṇānāṃ hi nedṛśākāradhīratā ।। na hi kubjapalāśākhyā pārijātasya yujyate ।।
kledur ity ucyate candro mātariśveti mārutaḥ ।। āśrayasya hi daurbalyād āśritaḥ paribhūyate ।। yuvayor adya sauhārdaṃ gataṃ kūṭasthanityatām ।। vardhayāmo vayaṃ diṣṭyā sārthavāhakuṭumbinīm ।।
na hīdānīṃ vivāhasya kaścid asti vighātakaḥ ।। yajñaguptaṃ varīkṛtya varayātrāṃ vyasarjayat ।। saṃjñayā yajñaguptaṃ tu varaṃ kurubhakaṃ vaṇik ।। śreṣṭhiputro api jāmātur āsīt tatra vayasyakaḥ ।।
utkāntikāntavṛttāntāṃ yakṣasenālakām iva ।। vasantopahṛtaśrīkapurodyānamanoharam ।। atṛptadṛṣṭayo apaśyan varaṃ pauraparaṃparāḥ ।। veṇuvīṇāpravīṇaiś ca kāṃcid velām ayāpayat ।।
sajjaṃ vaḥ pānam annaṃ ca kim ādhve bhujyatām iti ।। kena kenātra bhoktavyam iti syālakam uktavān ।। yūyaṃ madhyamam adhyādhvam āsanaṃ paṭuvāsanam ।। ete jyeṣṭhakaniṣṭhau te syālakāv adhitiṣṭhataḥ ।।
tavāsyām upaveṣṭavyaṃ śeṣayā syālamālayā ।। asmābhiḥ saha yuṣmābhir na kāryaṃ pānabhojanam ।। bhujyate vāparaiḥ sārdhaṃ yāvan na pariṇīyate ।। kāryam etan na vā kāryaṃ vinādeśād guror iti ।।
durmanāyitasaṃbandhī pūtam āhāram āharat ।। gṛhaṃ sāgaradattasya pariṇetum agād asau ।। smaran guruvaco dhīryān nirvikārakaro varaḥ ।। pāṇibhyām udaraṃ dhṛtvā mumoha ca papāta ca ।।
mūkitoddāmadhūryeṇa kranditena vijṛmbhitam ।। uccair bhartṛsamāvasthām ākrośat kundamālikām ।। jitapradyumnarūpo ayaṃ patir utsādito yayā ।। yayā tvaṃ sakalaṃ janma draṣṭavyāmṛtayā mṛtā ।।
dūrāntaragariṣṭho hi nārīṇāṃ jīvitāt patiḥ ।। śaktā vidhavikāṃ draṣṭuṃ jyeṣṭhā kālasya sā svasā ।। hṛdayodarasaṃdhiś ca jāmātuḥ spanditaḥ śanaiḥ ।। harṣahāsāṭṭahāsānām āsīn nāntaram ambare ।।
udamīlayad ātāmre locane gurutārake ।। vṛddhatālabdhaputreṇa yo nṛpeṇāpi duṣkaraḥ ।। āmāśayagataṃ śūlaṃ bādhate guru mām iti ।। śūlasyāmanidānasya kṛtavantaś cikitsitam ।।
tasya jāgradvadhūkasya katham apy agaman niśā ।। asnehālpatarāhāraḥ so abhavat pratyahaḥ kṛśaḥ ।। vismṛteva vadhūlajjāṃ bhartṛmāndyabhayāturā ।। aṅgeṣu bhayasannāṅgīṃ kurvan kelīṃ kilāspṛśat ।।
devatāgurubhir dattaṃ kāntaṃ toṣaya mām iti ।। keyaṃ kelir anāryeti vadhūr bhartāram abravīt ।। kā hi nāgarikaṃmanyā hāsyāt naṭabaṭos traset ।। na hi mūkaṃ śukaṃ kaścic ciraṃ dharati pañjare ।।
hasataḥ spṛśataś cāṅgaṃ bhīru mā vitrasīr iti ।। caṇḍābhir ghaṭadāsībhis taṃ bhuktaṃ nirabhartsayat ।। rahasyaṃ na bhinatty etat tāvan nyāyyam ito gatam ।। pānāhāravihāreṣu kim icchati bhavān iti ।।
pitarau draṣṭum icchāmi priyaputrau priyāv iti ।। evaṃ vadati jāmātā tac ca pratividhīyatām ।। kṛtam apy akṛtaṃ tat tad etasmiñ jātam āture ।। jagatprasiddhisiddhaṃ hi suhṛddarśanam auṣadham ।।
śyāmāṃ niśām iva kṛśena tuṣārabhāsā prāsthāpayat saha vareṇa vaṇiktanūjām ।। śreṣṭhī ca dviguṇān prītān prāhiṇot paricārakān ।। nivartitavyaṃ yuṣmābhir iti cāsāv uvāca tān ।। śreṣṭhine kathitaṃ tābhyāṃ varaḥ svastho manāg iti ।।
śanakaiḥ śanakair māndyam atyajat sa tathā tathā ।। varaṃ sāgaradattāya hṛṣṭapuṣṭāṅgam ākhyatām ।। ācaturvedacaṇḍālaṃ vitatāra nidhīn api ।। gṛhītabrāhmaṇākalpaḥ prasthitaḥ padagaḥ pathi ।।
sendracāpataḍiddāmnā ghaneneva niśākaraḥ ।। āruroha varākāraḥ prītaḥ kurubhakaḥ khalaḥ ।। pravidhūya vadhūr aṅgaṃ locane samamīlayat ।। niragāt tyaktakartavyā javanā janatā purāt ।।
dṛṣṭvā dhutakaraiḥ paurair adhikṣiptaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। kiṃ punar yaḥ sadācāraḥ sargahetur bhavādṛśaḥ ।। yenaitāv apsaraḥpretau duryojyau yojitāv iti ।। vadhūm abhyanayat kāntyā jitarājagṛhaṃ gṛham ।।
iyam evāstu te putras tanayā ca vadhūr iti ।। naṭādiṣu ca nṛtyatsu sārkaṃ tad agamad dinam ।। yajñaguptavayasyena kubjakena sahāviśat ।। vadhūr varavayasyo api tadanantaram unnatam ।।
amūlāgrāṇi pattrāṇi lilikhur namitānanāḥ ।। api nāmaiṣa māṃ muktvā brāhmaṇo na vrajed iti ।। api nāmaiṣa niryāyād bahir vāsagṛhād iti ।। gamanaṃ cātmanaḥ śreyas tato nirgantum aihata ।।
dārān āpadgatān muktvā prasthitaḥ kva bhavān iti ।। āpannāsmīti mā vocas tiṣṭhantī tasya saṃnidhau ।। vayaṃ tu kharadharmāṇo bhāramātrasya bhāginaḥ ।। anicchām aicchad ākraṣṭuṃ grāmyaḥ kurubhakaś ca tām ।।
vyāharantīva taṃ vipraṃ nirjagāma javena sā ।। yajñaguptas tayā naiva dṛṣṭas tatra gṛhāṅgaṇe ।। yaṃ kaṃcid api sā yāntam anvayāsīt tadāśayā ।। hiṇḍīvāditrabhītā ca kumbhakārakuṭīgamāt ।।
suśliṣṭā hanta rakṣeyam ity adhyavasitaṃ tayā ।। abhyastavaṇigācārā babandha dṛḍham ambare ।। ghūrṇamānā madād grāmaṃ bāhyaṃ niragamat purāt ।। svagṛhālindakāsīnā dṛṣṭā karpāsakarttrikā ।।
dhik kṣudraṃ buddhavarmāṇam iti sakrodham abravīt ।। sādhoḥ kiṃ duṣkṛtaṃ tasya nindyate yad asāv iti ।। tadīyaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ yena prakāśam api na śrutam ।। mādṛśī tu na śaktaiva vaktuṃ prakṛtikātarā ।।
ḍiṇḍimadhvanisaṃbhinnā paribabhrāma ghoṣaṇā ।। nāgaraḥ kaścid ācaṣṭe sa dāridryeṇa mucyate ।। pāṭayaty adhanaṃ kṛtvā dāruṇaiḥ krakacair iti ।। paritoṣaparādhīnā jahāsa ca ruroda ca ।।
nātisaṃdhīyate dhūrtair mūladevasamair iti ।। yayā sakubjakaḥ pāpo buddhavarmātisaṃdhitaḥ ।। yajñaguptena saṃgamya tvayāpi sthīyatāṃ tathā ।। niṣkāraṇajanany eṣā gopāyiṣyati mām iti ।।
gāḍham āliṅgya sā caināṃ prītā prāveśayad gṛham ।। tadbhāraparikhinnāni gātrāṇi paryavāhayat ।। sthūlaceladalāstīrṇe śayane samaveśayat ।। bhrāmyatsaṃbhrāntapauraṃ tat sā prātaḥ prāviśat puram ।।
iti pṛṣṭavatī kaṃcid asau puranivāsinam ।। putraḥ kurubhako nāma svanāmavikṛtākṛtiḥ ।। śailūṣeṇeva lubdhena svabhāryā pratipāditā ।। pradoṣe kvāpy apakrāntā lokas tenāyam ākulaḥ ।।
bhadra ṣaṇḍhasya tasyāśu gṛhaṃ nayata mām iti ।। yajñaguptagṛhaṃ prāpad brahmanirghoṣabhūṣaṇam ।। sāntevāsinam āsīnaṃ yajñaguptaṃ dadarśa sā ।। ko ayaṃ vyākhyāyate grantha ity apṛcchat samatsarā ।।
etasyāṃ cāturāśramyaṃ cāturvarṇyaṃ ca varṇyate ।। lokāyatam idaṃ manye nirmaryādajanapriyam ।। na hi vaidyaḥ svaśāstrajñaḥ kuṣṭhī māṃsaṃ niṣevate ।। vyatikrāntasavarṇena pariṇītā varā tvayā ।।
yūnā ca kāṇakuṇṭhāya matkuṇāya kilārpitā ।। tvayā kṛtam akartavyaṃ yuktaṃ cet kathyatām iti ।। vidheyair avikāryārthād guruvākyād anuṣṭhitam ।। mātuḥ kṛttaṃ śiras tatra kim āha bhagavān iti ।।
na hi rudreṇa pīteti pibanti brāhmaṇāḥ surām ।। guruḥ kiṃ nāma na brūyād duḥkhakrodhādibādhitaḥ ।। śiro me chinddhi putreti kiṃ kāryaṃ tena tat tathā ।। tat tasyaiva prabhāvena sadyaḥ saṃghaṭitaṃ punaḥ ।।
divyaprabhāvahīnena tat kathaṃ kāryam anyathā ।। guruvākyaṃ kṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ yad gataṃ gatam eva tat ।। vādivācye hi nirdoṣe kiṃ vācyaṃ prativādinaḥ ।। bhikṣāvelāpadeśena tam āmantyoccacāla sā ।।
tenātraiva sadāhāraṃ karotu bhagavān iti ।। asaṃbhojyam abhojyatvād annaṃ kāpālikair api ।। punaḥsaṃvaraṇaṃ cāsau yāti bhojyānnatām iti ।। apanīya ca taṃ veṣam ācaran majjanādikam ।।
yajñaguptagṛhaṃ gatvā dinaśeam ayāpayat ।। śeṣaṃ ca yajñaguptasya sānayad divasān bahūn ।। akāryam idam etena kṛtaṃ karma dvijanmanā ।। kārye hi sulabhopāye na muhyanti sumedhasaḥ ।।
asau vikrāpayām āsa tayā brāhmaṇavṛddhayā ।। tāmrakumbhayuganyastaṃ sīmānte nihitaṃ tayā ।। ālāpaiś ciram āsitvā yajñaguptam abhāṣata ।। iti pravrajitācāram etaṃ veda bhavān iti ।।
tyaktapravrajitācāras tad abhavat prītivañcitaḥ ।। viraktāḥ svaśarīre api niḥsaṅgāḥ kiṃ mumukṣavaḥ ।। tīrthadarśanatantrā hi somasiddhāntavādinaḥ ।। mahākālamataṃ nāma nidhānotpāṭanāgamam ।।
ujjvalair lakṣitaś cihnaiḥ kenāpi nihito nidhiḥ ।। saphalāḥ khalu saṃparkāḥ sādhubhis tvādṛśair iti ।। sadhīrāptataracchāttraḥ pracchannaṃ gṛham ānayat ।। mahākālamatajñātvaṃ tasya kāpālikasya ca ।।
mahābhiksor mahājñānaṃ mahākālamataṃ paṭha ।। nidhigarbhāṃ naro yena chidrāṃ paśyati medinīm ।। mahākālamatasyārthe yatnād ārādhyatām iti ।। yajñagupto bravīti sma prasthitāṃ kundamālikām ।।
dṛṣṭādṛṣṭamahāśreyaḥkāraṇaṃ mādṛśām iti ।। mahākālamataprepsur asau naiva nivṛttavān ।। ratnaṃ nātimahāmūlyam iti cainam abhāṣata ।। na tu tāruṇyamūḍhena saṃbhāṣyā gaṇikā tvayā ।।
veśyāvaśyaḥ svadārāṇāṃ yāty avaśyam avaśyatām ।। yaj jīvati tad āścaryaṃ kva dharmaḥ kva yaśaḥsukhe ।। ārādhyavākyāni hi bhūtikāmāḥ sevāvidhijñā na vikalpayanti ।। naimiṣaṃ jagmatus tasmād gaṅgādvāraṃ tataḥ kurūn ।।
kārttikānte mahāpuṇyaṃ dṛṣṭavantau mahālayam ।। bahudraviṇam utpādya dadāmi bhavate nidhim ।। trivargeṇa hi yujyante gṛhasthā gṛhamedhinaḥ ।। bhavanti khalu dharmārthaṃ tīrthayātrāparāyaṇāḥ ।।
sā hi kāpālikālīnā gaṇikānām ivākaraḥ ।। yātrāyāṃ kila yudhyante yuddhamātraprayojanāḥ ।। kākatālīyamokṣā hi śastrapañjaracāriṇaḥ ।। svargavad brahmaghātena tena sā durgamā tvayā ।।
prāvṛtya ca tataḥ paśya sanidhiḥ pitarāv iti ।। hanta saṃprati saṃprāptaṃ mahākālamataṃ mayā ।। sarvam apy ujjhati sphītaṃ kim u grantham anarthakam ।। mahākālamataṃ tan me kathaṃ nāma na dāsyati ।।
tasya pracchādanopāyo yat kiṃcid iva tucchakaḥ ।। paruṣākulakeśaṃ ca na kaścil lakṣayaiṣyati ।। kiṃ cāntevāsināṃ yuktaṃ moktum ācāryam āpadi ।। na hi gacchati pūrṇendau kalaṅko asya na gacchati ।।
anujñātavatī tasya gamanaṃ kundamālikā ।। iha bhadravaṭe bhadra vinayasva pathiśramam ।। yāvat tāvat tvayotkaṇṭhā na kāryā mām apaśyatā ।। āśaṅke ciram ātmānaṃ paribhrāntam itas tataḥ ।।
na hy aujjayanakāḥ paurāḥ sthirān nidadhate nidhīn ।। muktvā kāpālikākalpam amalām akarot tanum ।। śaraddyaur iva sābhāsīj jyotsnātārākulākulā ।। jālaśikyasthitālābūḥ sā pratasthe sapiṇḍikā ।।
vyāharanti sma tām uccaiḥ kuñcitāṅgulipāṇayaḥ ।। tena sārdhaṃ yathāśraddhaṃ pānam āsevyatām iti ।। tān atidrutayā gatyā jagāma ca jagāda ca ।। alaṃ bhagavatāṃ dṛṣṭvā māṃ dṛṣṭiviṣakanyakām ।।
īrṣyāvān apramattaś ca sadā rakṣati mām asau ।। yameneva kṣayaṃ nītā koṭir yuṣmādṛśām iti ।। tan na kevalam etasyām adhikaṃ copapadyate ।। āścaryaṃ yan na yudhyante brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ।।
anugṛhṇātu sasnehair iyam ālokitair iti ।। āśīḥkalakalonnītam agacchad bhavanaṃ pituḥ ।। mātur vāsagṛhadvāri bhikṣāṃ dehīti cābravīt ।। āśiraścaraṇāṅguṣṭham apaśyat kundamālikām ।।
praviśya kathayām āsa svāminyai śanakair asau ।। śirīṣāmālikālolā duhitā kundamālikā ।। iyaṃ tiṣṭhati te dvāri svayaṃ vā dṛśyatām iti ।। vācyatām anapekṣyaiva snehād etac cacāra sā ।।
ciccheda guḍikāṃ śaśvat śaṅkhasphatikamaṇḍanam ।। maṅgalasnānaśuddhāntāṃ śuddhāntam anayat tataḥ ।। kim etad evam eveti sā tatas tām abhāṣata ।। asatībhir api kṣiptaṃ caret kāpālikavratam ।।
asti me guru kartavyaṃ sādhyate tac ca tair iti ।। kiṃ kim etat kathaṃ ceti śaśaṅke viṣasāda ca ।। āśvāsayitum āliṅgya vavande vijahāsa ca ।। jāmātā tava sa syālais tasmād ānāyyatām iti ।।
labdho asi putracaureti mṛṣā paruṣabhāṣibhiḥ ।। tvām āhūyati rājeti sasmitāś cainam abruvan ।। mānastokam ṛcaṃ japtvā śikhābandhaṃ cakāra saḥ ।। mama kāpāliko mitraṃ yāvad āyāty asāv iti ।।
sa gataḥ prathamaṃ tatra tenaiva grāhito bhavān ।। niṣprayojanasauhārdāvacaḥsadṛ।acetasaḥ suhṛdo api virajyante khalānāṃ tvādṛśām iti ।। gṛhītvā gṛham ājagmuḥ prītabandhujanāvṛtam ।।
pariṣvaktasya jāmātuḥ saprāṇam abhavad vapuḥ ।। adhyaśeta mahāśayyāṃ ramyamaṇḍapasaṃstṛtām ।। āptāś ca śreṣṭhinaḥ paurāḥ paritaḥ samupāviśan ।। vācālakalahaṃseva niṣkalaṅkāmbarā śarat ।।
yajñaguptaḥ punar dṛṣṭyā sarāgāñjanagarbhayā ।। vivāhādiyathāvṛttam ātmavṛttaṃ nyavedayat ।। dvyaṅgulaprajñayā yo ahaṃ vañcitaḥ kulakanyayā ।। kuśāgrīyadhiyo yoṣāyāsāṃ karmesam īdṛśam ।।
tiṣṭhatāṃ gatisaṃsthāne svaro api parivartitaḥ ।। iti ye vicikitseyus teṣām eṣā nidarśanam ।। tasmād asmy anayaivādya mocitaḥ pātakād iti ।। sahajāmātṛkānītā svagṛhaṃ kundamālikā ।।
sa dattvā yajñaguptāya sasmitas tām abhāṣata ।। tvayā dhīratayā putri tathā saṃpādyatām iti ।। na hi kṣitīśān avilaṅghyaśāsanān vilaṅghayanti priyajīvitaśriyaḥ ।। niṣevamānaḥ sukṛtaṃ ca saṃtataṃ nināya vipraḥ saphalaṃ samāśatam ।।
saṃtoṣakṣatasattvasattvadayitaḥ saṃsevitaḥ kātarais tasmāt pauruṣamārutena balinā daivādrir unmūlitaḥ ।। drutapravahaṇārūḍho gomukhaś ca parāgataḥ ।। sarvanāgarakaśreṇigrāmaṇīr dṛśyatām iti ।। yuvānam api vainītyāl lajjitasthaviraṃ naram ।।
saṃbhāvitaguṇāḥ sadbhir arhanty eva ca satkriyām ।। sāṃyātrika ivāmbhodhiṃ tadāvāsam avātaram ।। dinaśeṣaṃ nayāmi sma gītiśrutivinodanaḥ ।। katham eṣa tvayā prāptaḥ suhṛd ity atha so abravīt ।।
na ca kaṃcana paśyāmi yogyam āśrayadāyinam ।। saṃbhavaḥ sarvasādhūnāṃ nāsti rājakulād ṛte ।। rājadvāraṃ vigāhante samudram iva sindhavaḥ ।। rājadvāraṃ hi kāryāṇāṃ dvāram uktaṃ budhair iti ।।
tad gatvā smṛtavān asmi pretādhipadhanādhipau ।। āśrayaprārthanā tasmān nāsmin saṃpadyate mṛṣā ।। tena saṃbhāvyate nāsmāt prārthanāphalam aṇv api ।। abhyantarāt pratīhāraṃ dṛṣṭavān asmi nirgatam ।।
pratimānitavān sarvān sakṛn namitamastakaḥ ।। kāryibhir yugapat tatra kāryavijñāpanā kṛtā ।। bhavataḥ sumukho rājā mā tvariṣṭa bhavān iti ।। avatārya samīpasthe nyastavān paricārake ।।
na hi dṛṣṭasuvarṇādriḥ tāmraṃ dhamati vātikaḥ ।। māṃ muhuḥ paśyatā prītyā tenaiva sahito agamam ।। āgacchati kutaḥ kiṃ vā mad icchati bhavān iti ।। vidyāsthānam idaṃ śrutvā avantideśāt samāgatau ।।
balavattaragupto hi kṛśo api balavān iti ।। agrāmyālāparūpāṇāṃ svagṛhaṃ bhavatām iti ।। kṣubhitāmbhodhikallolakolāhalam iva kṣaṇam ।। kiṃ tvam etan na vettheti na vedeti mayoditam ।।
vṛtaḥ kitavasaṃghena dīvyati dyūtamaṇḍape ।। vitaraty arthivargāya tasyaiṣa tumulo dhvaniḥ ।। viṣādamuṣitālāpādhyāyanti śivam arthinaḥ ।। pratīhāreṇa kathite tataś cintitavān aham ।।
yeṣāṃ yantritavākkāyair agrato duḥkham āsyate ।। vyasanī ca svatantraś ca so asmākam adhunā suhṛt ।। nirdhāryeti tam āmantrya dyūtakārasabhām agām ।। sarasīvāmiṣāsvādagṛddhair bakakadambakaiḥ ।।
akṣaḥ koṇena patitaḥ saṃdigdhapadapañcakaḥ ।। iti jātā tayoḥ spardhā parasparajayaiṣiṇoḥ ।। pratyuktam itareṇāpi yathecchasi tathāstv iti ।। katarat paśyasi spaṣṭaṃ padapañcakayor iti ।।
dīrghatvād eṣa nirbuddhir ato anyaḥ pṛcchyatām iti ।। nedṛśāḥ praśnam arhanti bahudoṣā hi khaṭvakāḥ ।। sādho yadi na doṣo asti tato nau chinddhi saṃśayam ।। tena madhyapramāṇatvād gaccha madhyasthatām iti ।।
pāradraviṇagṛddheṣu kitaveṣu viśeṣataḥ ।। aprakāśaṃ hi vijñānaṃ kṛpaṇārthanirarthakam ।। na hi prayuñjate prājñāḥ veśād anyatra vaiśikam ।। dhanavanmitralābhaṃ hi nidhilābhādikaṃ viduḥ ।।
akṣāṣṭāpadaśārīṇām ākhyaṃ bhūmeś ca lakṣaṇam ।। supiṣṭamiṣṭakākṣodam akṣasyopari dattavān ।। so apatat sakalo bhūmau pañcakasyopari sthitaḥ ।। tasyottānatvam utkṛṣṭaṃ kṣodas tatra yataḥ sthitaḥ ।।
aho sādhv iti nirghoṣaḥ samantāt sahasotthitaḥ ।। dhruvaṃ vijayate dūrān nalakuntīsutāv iti ।। ayaṃ jayati jetārāv api puṣakarasaubalau ।। padavādī jito yo asāv asau mantharam uktavān ।।
dyūtasthāne hi kiṃ kṛtyaṃ pravīṇaiḥ prāśnikair iti ।। yo ahaṃ trailokyasāreṇa paṇena paṇavān iti ।। ehi dīvyāva mitreti tam ahaṃ dhūrtam uktavān ।। dṛṣṭas tṛṣṇāviśālākṣaiḥ pataṃgair iva pāvakaḥ ।।
mayā saha sasaṃrambham akṣān ārabdha devitum ।। prabuddhair gardhagṛddhena sahasratritayaṃ jitaḥ ।। lakṣam ekena pātena jitaḥ sa kitavādhamaḥ ।। na virantuṃ na vā rantum asāv aśakad ākulaḥ ।।
vailakṣyād ghaṭṭayann akṣān na kiṃcit pratipannavān ।। kitavo ayam idaṃ lakṣam acalaṃ dāpyatām iti ।। tathā pūjitavān devaṃ haraṃ dattavaraṃ yathā ।। tad udgrāhyedam ānītaṃ lakṣaṃ te gṛhyatām iti ।।
sādhitaṃ bhavatā yac ca tasya svāmī bhavān iti ।। svāmino yūyam evāsya dhanasyety atra kā kathā ।। adhigacchati yad dāso bhartur eva hi tad dhanam ।। bhūtalaṃ yūyam āyātāḥ kiṃ nimittaṃ tripiṣṭapāt ।।
ākārāntaranirmāṇaṃ nātyantam anuśīlitam ।। dṛṣṭāḥ kena manuṣyeṣu yādṛśo bhavatām iti ।। dūreṇa hy atinindāyāduḥkhahetur atistutiḥ ।। yan mayā kāryam ākhyātaṃ tad evāsmai niveditam ।।
tvādṛśasyāpi yo jyeṣṭhaḥ kīdṛśaḥ sa bhaviṣyati ।। sarvatīrthādhike deśe taṃ prāpayata mām iti ।। yac cottaram atas tatra pratyakṣaṃ bhavatām api ।। na hiṃsanti na sarvatra śriyaḥ puṇyavatām iti ।।
phalaṃ sucaritasyaiva hṛdayaṃ yasya gomukhaḥ ।। parānnaṃ hi vṛthābhuktaṃ duḥkhāyaiva satām iti ।। nītavān asmi yāminyāḥ prātaś cāgāt punarvasuḥ ।। ballavaḥ kuśalaḥ kaścit kutaścana gaveṣyatām ।।
parapākanivṛttā hi sādhuvṛttā dvijātayaḥ ।। ārādhanānurodho hi caritaṃ mahatām iti ।। yady evaṃ jagadīśānāṃ kiṃ nāsti bhavatām iti ।। ākārakṣiptanāsatyāv apaśyaṃ puruṣau puraḥ ।।
prasārya sabhujān pādāñ jayety uktvā bhuvaṃ gatau ।। vanditvā punar abrūtāṃ brūta kiṃ kriyatām iti ।। satyaṃ ced idam āryasya pākaḥ saṃsādhyatām iti ।। snātau soṣṇīṣamūrdhānau mahānasam agacchatām ।।
sarvā tābhyām apūrveva prakriyā saṃprasāritā ।। tāvatyā velayā tābhyāṃ pāka eva samāpitaḥ ।। āhārasthānam adhyāsi viprapaṅktinirantaram ।। āhāro yaiḥ praśastas tair aśitaṃ prākṛtāśanam ।।
samutsṛṣṭāmṛtāhārābhaveyur nāmarās tadā ।। sūdābhyāṃ bhuktabhaktābhyām ayutaṃ dīyatām iti ।। smitasaṃsūcitaprītir upākramata bhāṣitum ।। avasthāsādṛśaṃ kiṃ tu yat kiṃcid gṛhyatām iti ।।
na yuktaṃ dhanam ādātum āvābhyām iti bhāṣitam ।। jitatrailokyavitteśaṃ vitteśaṃ yo anukampase ।। susthitāni bhaviṣyanti dauḥsthityaṃ tasya kīdṛśam ।। duḥsthitas tādṛśo yasya susthitas tasya kīdṛśaḥ ।।
dhārayitvā kṣaṇaṃ mūrdhnā prasthāya prāptavān gṛham ।। divyam aiśvaryam āgāmi kathaṃ veda bhavān iti ।। śatayajñādhikaśrīkaḥ pañcayajñaḥ pitābhavat ।। dvitīya iva tasyātmā devavān iti ballavaḥ ।।
rājñā tasmai svarājyasya daśamo aṃśaḥ prakalpitaḥ ।। īdṛśākāravijñānāv āvām eva ca viddhi tau ।। sahajñānaprayogābhyāṃ kulavidyeti śikṣite ।। śrotāraṃ guruvākyānāṃ na spṛśanti vipattayaḥ ।।
bhavadbhyāṃ śikṣitavyāni citrādiś ca kalāgaṇaḥ ।। śāstrakāvyakathālāpair vinodaṃ prabhur icchati ।। vinodaṃ tasya kuryātaṃ śāstrālāpādibhir yuvām ।। prakāśitamanovṛttair bhṛtyāḥ krīḍanti bhartṛbhiḥ ।।
svavidyālāpaparyāyakhinnaś ciram udīkṣate ।। gatasaṃśayaduḥkhatvāt sukhināṃ parameśvaraḥ ।। dīrghāyur vittavanto hi saṃsevyāḥ sevakair iti ।। ramyāsvādaṃ ca pathyaṃ ca ko avamanyeta bheṣajam ।।
jyaiṣṭhacandrasahasrāṃśudīrghāyuś ceti nau matiḥ ।। na hi vandanasāmānyam arhanti bahuvanditāḥ ।। śiraḥspandanamātreṇa tān āvāṃ pūjayāvahe ।। jyeṣṭhasya dṛṣṭam aiśvaryam ataḥ śraddhīyatām iti ।।
bhāvaṃ hi saṃśayatamaḥ paṭalāpinaddham udbhāvayanty avitathā vacanapradīpāḥ ।। punarvasugṛhe stokān divasān avasaṃ sukhī ।। śramaṇāṃ dṛṣṭavān asmi śiṣyāsaṃghapuraḥsarīm ।। ye tasyā varṇasaṃsthāne varṇayanti hatatrapāḥ ।।
yenākāraviruddho asyām ācāro durbhagaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। ghaṭayitvā ghaṭaḥ kena loṣṭena śakalīkṛtaḥ ।। śoṣitā tuhineneti dhik tasya khalatām iti ।। gomukhaḥ sphuritotsāhaḥ pṛcchati sma punarvasum ।।
eṣā pravrajitā bhadra kva gacchati gatair iti ।। vītarāgatayā siddhān atiśete jinān api ।। kanyakāntaḥpurād eti yāti svaśayanāsanam ।। ambike sahaśiṣyāyās te namo astu namo astv iti ।।
kim artham iti tenokte tayoktam avadhīyatām ।। dvijau jyeṣṭhakaniṣṭhākhyau tvadgṛhe kila tiṣṭhataḥ ।। draviṇaṃ kṛpaṇeneva pracchannam upabhujyate ।। sukhasaṃvaraṇāyāsād viparītas tu duḥkhitaḥ ।।
teṣām atrānayopāyaḥ samarthaś cintyatām iti ।। ।। । sahanandopanandaś ca jināyatanamaṇḍapam ।।
ṛṣidattāṃ ca tad datte viṣṭare samupāviśam ।। sthitvā devakuladvāre jinastotram udāharat ।। ṛṣabhapramukhebhyaś ca sarvajñebhyo namo astv iti ।। ityādi bahu nirgranthāḥ prītyāstuvata gomukham ।।
abravīt suprasannau me bhavantau bhavatām iti ।। śrāvakasyāpi saṃvādyā pratipattir bhavatv iti ।। eṣa saṃnihitaḥ saṃghaḥ sakalaḥ suhṛdām iti ।। asaṃnihitahaṃseva nalinī nīravā sabhā ।।
udīkṣantām iti tataḥ saṃprāpto gaṅgarakṣitaḥ ।। ākhyāta nipuṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā kataro rūpavān iti ।। gaṅgarakṣitarūpeṇa rūpaṃ me sadṛśaṃ yataḥ ।। upamānam upādeyaḥ so api rūpavatām iti ।।
upāviśat punaś coktam upanandena pūrvavat ।। anāyāte sadaḥ sarvam idam apriyadarśanam ।। ayam āyāta ity ākhyan nāgarāḥ priyadarśanam ।। eṣā puruṣaveṣeṇa bhūṣitā priyadarśanā ।।
kṣiptatrailokyasaundaryam ākhyātaṃ straiṇam ātmanaḥ ।। ciraṃ sundari jīveti mayāpi prativanditā ।। citraṃ nāgarakaiḥ kaiścil lajjitaiḥ kaiścid ambaram ।। sagomukham apaśyan mām āśiraścaraṇaṃ ciram ।।
abhāṣata suhṛdvargaṃ goṣṭhī prastūyatām iti ।। yathā vigatarāgād yair nirgranthair api mūrchitam ।। punarvasor agād vīṇā kramāt taṃ gaṅgarakṣitam ।। parājayata dūreṇa pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ paraḥ paraḥ ।।
sarasvatīva vittāḍhyād īśvarād durgataṃ gatā ।। yathā nāgarikair dīnair īkṣito gaṅgarakṣitaḥ ।। kulaṭeva priyotsaṅgāt kāminaṃ priyadarśanam ।। vailakṣyād gomukhasyāsīd abhiprāyaḥ palāyitum ।।
yat satyam aham apy āsam adbhutaśrutivismitaḥ ।। adhunā prāptaparyāyaṃ vādanaṃ bhavatām iti ।। yo māṃ yatra kvacit tucche pravartayati vastuni ।। vīṇāṃ vādayamānasya mādṛśaḥ kīdṛśaṃ phalam ।।
campāyāṃ kīdṛśaṃ kāryam abhavad bhavatām iti ।। prāptir gandharvadattāyās tatra kāryam abhūd iti ।। ihāpi gomukhaprāptiḥ phalam uttamam iṣyatām ।। idaṃ me śreṣṭham āgamya śreṣṭhināpahṛtaṃ yaśaḥ ।।
tyajāmy eṣa tataḥ prāṇān duḥkhabhārāturān iti ।। maraṇābhyadhikakleśo mānabhaṅgo hi māninām ।। kāntayā ca vimuktasya duḥkhaṃ kenopamīyate ।। vyavasthāpayituṃ tantrīr ārabhe durvyavasthitāḥ ।।
anyonyasya niraikṣanta vadanāni sadaḥsadaḥ ।। hā hā kim idam ity uktvā pustanyastā ivābhavan ।। taiś ca muktāyatocchvāsair jīvaloko avalokitaḥ ।। abhrājata tataḥ sadyo gomukhānanapaṅkajam ।।
jitadurjayavādīva prītimān mām abhāṣata ।। iti me prasthitā kīrtir āpayodhi vasuṃdharām ।। rāghavotkṛttamūrdhnas tu śambūkasyāmalaṃ yaśaḥ ।। vīṇāvādārthinaṃ śiṣyaṃ parigṛhṇīta mām iti ।।
ayam eva mamāpy arthaḥ saphalīkriyatām iti ।। anāyāsopadeśau ca yat tad evaṃ bhavatv iti ।। prārthanā pratipanneti gomukhenoditaṃ tataḥ ।। yac cānyad api tat sarvaṃ gaṅgarakṣitarakṣitam ।।
tasyāpadbhir asaṃkīrṇāhastasthāḥ sarvasaṃpadaḥ ।। sa yasya kiṃkaras tasya kiṃkarā sakalā purī ।। na hy anālocyakartāraḥ kiṃkarā bhavatām iti ।। namaskṛtārhadvratacārisaṃghaḥ punarvasor veśma gatas tato aham ।।
akṛtrimasuhṛdbhāvaiḥ sagataḥ sukham āsiṣi ।। atha nītam anāhārair asmābhir api tad dinam ।। tad anāthamatodvignaṃ māṃ vinītavad uktavān ।। bhṛtyo hariśikhasyaiva lokenāntaritaḥ sa ca ।।
kārye hi guruṇi vyagraṃ jighatsāpi na bādhate ।। tasmān mā mām apaśyantaḥ kṛdhvaṃ duḥkhāsikām iti ।। madamantharasaṃcāro bahujalpann upāgamat ।। sthitvā kṣaṇam anālāpaḥ paruṣālāpam abravam ।।
iti paṅgos turaṃgasya kṛtā garuḍavegatā ।। adhunā madhunā mattaḥ kathaṃ paśyasi mām iti ।। sadoṣaṃ tu vaco vaktuṃ mayāyaṃ kṛtrimaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। dūṣayanti na vaktāram ato ayaṃ kṛtrimo madaḥ ।।
madapracchādanopāyaḥ kiṃ nv adoṣo api vidyate ।। ayam ārabhatākhyātuṃ lajjāmantharitākṣaram ।। ārabhya divasāt tasmāc cetoviṣayatām iti ।। kasmād aviṣaye cakṣuś cetasā me prasāritam ।।
rāgādhīnaṃ na me cakṣuḥ pravṛttaṃ gaṇikāsv api ।। saṃkalpena mamaitasyāṃ durdāntaturago ayataḥ ।। jijñāsye tāvad ity enām agacchaṃ draṣṭum anv aham ।। dvitrair eva dinais tasyāviśvāsam udapādayam ।।
ke ke deśās tvayā dṛṣṭāḥ krāmatā pṛthivīm iti ।। vatsadeśaḥ sa dṛṣṭaḥ prāṅ mameti kathite mayā ।। kriyatāṃ vatsakauśāmbīsaṃbandhaiva punaḥ kathā ।। gomukhaṃ nāma niṣṇātaṃ savidyāsu kalāsv iti ।।
atha vā dhig adhīraṃ mām evaṃ tāvad bhavatv iti ।। ātmānaṃ ko na jānāti sa hi me paramaḥ suhṛt ।। tena māṃ paśyatā vyaktaṃ dṛṣṭo bhavati gomukhaḥ ।। sānurāgeva dṛṣṭvā māṃ ciraṃ mantharam abravīt ।।
vatsarājasutaṃ muktvā nānyena sadṛśaḥ kṣitau ।। vidyādharakumāreṇa gomukhaḥ sadṛśas tataḥ ।। gandhaśailo api hi ślāghyas tulyamānaḥ sumeruṇā ।। asau roditum ārabdhā sotkamastanamaṇḍalā ।।
rudyate mṛtapatyeva gomukhaśravaṇād iti ।। padmo nāma dhanaṃ yasya padmasyeva mahānidheḥ ।। sumanā mahadinnā ca tasya bhārye babhūvatuḥ ।। putrābhyāṃ dayite pitros tathā duhitarāv api ।।
nagaryāṃ pariṇītātra śreṣṭhinā kāliyena sā ।। cedivatseśamitreṇa pariṇītarṣabheṇa sā ।। na kutaścin na kasyāṃcit kaścij jagati yādṛśaḥ ।। himādrer api niyānti saritaḥ kṣāravārayaḥ ।।
kaṃ hi nāma na gacchanti kanyāpitror manorathāḥ ।। himakāla ivāsādhuḥ kālaḥ padmam anāśayat ।। unmūlitadṛḍhastambhamandirāvasthāṃ gatam ।। sthāpitāhaṃ pitṛṣvasrā duhiteva ca lālitā ।।
pīḍyamānā babhūvāndhā pratyākhyātā cikitsakaiḥ ।। asīc chrutadharā nāma śramaṇā karuṇāvatī ।। mām asāv acireṇaiva tasmād vyādher amocayat ।। atha krodhād ivāgṛhṇāt saiva jvaraparaṃparā ।।
sa ca yātaḥ punar vyādhir mantrāgadabhayād iva ।। pravrajyāgrāhaṇeneyaṃ bālikā jīvyatām iti ।। sakalaḥ śramanāsaṃghaḥ siṣyatām agaman mama ।। nirvāṇasya ca sāratvaṃ niṣṭhāṃ śrutadharāgamat ।।
gaṇanīm akarod asmin vihāre mām anicchatīm ।। balād ālambanaṃ tatra gomukhaḥ saṃnidhīyate ।। mukhottarapadas tatra jāyate sa tadā tadā ।। gośabdapūrvapadatāṃ balāt tatropagacchati ।।
iti cintāparādhīnā mahāntaṃ kālam akṣipam ।। āgatā yāvad anyaiva vārttā dattanirāśatā ।। gomukhaḥ sasuhṛdvargaḥ pulindair antare hataḥ ।। vicāraṇasamarthāyāḥ prajñāyāḥ sā samarthatā ।।
ramyām ākarṇayiṣyāmi gomukhasya kathām iti ।। hataḥ pravādamātreṇa gomukhaḥ śabarair iti ।। amṛtābhyadhikatve api duḥkhahetuṃ kathām iti ।। yuṣmaddāsāḥ kathaṃ kuryuḥ pāpasaṃkalpam anyathā ।।
kumārī sānurāgā ca tasmān na tyāgam arhati ।। aduṣṭaṃ grahaṇopāyam aham etaṃ prayuktavān ।। mardanābhyañjanādyaiś ca laghu saṃgham atoṣayam ।। mitravārtāvidāvyagraṃ pratīkṣadhvaṃ na mām iti ।।
śrāvakaiḥ saṃnidhāryantām annasaṃskārakārakāḥ ।। ṛṣibhyaḥ śramaṇābhyaś ca dātum icchāmi bhojanam ।। tad ekam arhataṃ bhaktyā sadyaḥ pāpaṃ pramārjyate ।। saśrāvakagaṇān āryāṃs tāṃs tad āmantryatām iti ।।
jitajihvair api prītaṃ jinaśāsanapāragaiḥ ।। patitas tuṅgaromāñcaḥ savepathuvijṛmbhakaḥ ।। duṣkaraḥ paritāpo api yathā saṃbhāvitas tayā ।। dantakūjitasaṃbhinnaṃ mayāpy etan niveditam ।।
jvareṇānubhavāmy etām avasthām īdṛśīm iti ।। mām asau karuṇāviṣṭā saṃvāhitavatī ciram ।। mahājanavivikto ayam āvāsaḥ kriyatām iti ।। tadabhiprāyajijñāsur atha tām idam abravam ।।
vratasthānāṃ viśeṣeṇa sthātuṃ saha rahaś ciram ।। pṛthagjanā janāś caite tena nirgamyatām iti ।। muktvā tvāṃ sthātum anyatra kiṃ punaḥ saṃtatajvaram ।। ślāghyā kiṃśukaśākhāpi vasantasahacāriṇī ।।
kālakūṭam api ślāghyaṃ līḍhaśaṃkarakaṃdharam ।। sā mahāgrahacaṇḍena gṛhītā bhāvajanmanā ।। sarve saṃkrāmiṇo rogāḥ spṛśatāṃ prāṇinām iti ।। kathaṃ nāma na saṃkramet tatra yaḥ paramārthikaḥ ।।
jvarasya parivāro ayam aṅgam asyāḥ prabādhate ।। lāvaṇyam iva gātreṣu tad asyāḥ prāsphurat sphuṭam ।। śītajvarārtam aṅgair yā na pīḍayasi mām iti ।। viralevāruṇālokaṃ niśāntaśaśicandrikā ।।
apāyātāṃ muhūrtena kṛtrimākṛtrimau jvarau ।। saṃghaḥ saṃhatya tāṃ svasmān nivāsān niravāsayat ।। anayan muditaḥ śreṣṭhī gṛhaṃ maṅgalasaṃkulam ।। prītanāgarakānīkaṃ karagraham akārayat ।।
atha vā kiṃ vikalpena svayam ālokyatām iti ।। duḥśraddhānaṃ hi sahasā kākatālīyam īdṛśam ।। prasthāpya prāk tadārhāṇi tāṃ didṛkṣus tato agamam ।। nānāpuṣpāṃ hasantīva vasantopavanaśriyam ।।
lajjitāsurakanyāsu tādṛśīṣu tu kā kathā ।। durlabhāṇi kvacit tasyāvācakāny akṣarāṇy api ।। alaṃkārakalāpasya gurusārasya dhāraṇam ।। na śakyā sarvathā draṣṭuṃ janair lolekṣaṇair api ।।
prakāśayati tal loke paṭumaṇḍanaḍiṇḍimaḥ ।। avandata prahṛṣṭāpi pravrajyātyāgalajjitā ।। sarāgaiva satī yā tvaṃ vītarāgagatiṃ gatā ।। kṣīṇaduḥsahaduḥkhatvān mokṣaṃ prāptāsi sarvathā ।।
yo,sito hi jitadṛṣṭabhartṛkās toṣayanti jananīsakhījanam ।। tām āmantrya svam āvāsam agacchaṃ sahagomukhaḥ ।। vipaṇer gṛham āyātam apaśyaṃ priyadarśanam ।। payodharāntarālakṣyaḥ śaśīva parimaṇḍalaḥ ।।
stanakeśivatītvaṃ hi prathamaṃ strītvalakṣaṇam ।। bhrāntijñānam idaṃ tasya kiṃcit sādṛśyakāritam ।। na hi dṛṣṭena dṛṣṭārthe draṣṭur bhavati saṃśayaḥ ।। apaśyad ṛṣidattā māṃ paśyantaṃ priyadarśanam ।।
ātmānaṃ cetayasveti priyadarśanam abravīt ।। taḍidguṇa ivāmbhodaṃ prāviśan mandirodaram ।। yayāpakramitaḥ śreṣṭhī mama locanagocarāt ।। punarvasugṛhaṃ prāpya paryaṅkaśaraṇo abhavam ।।
tumulāyudhiseneva yugapad mām abādhata ।। tathājñāpitavān asmi gomukhaṃ rūkṣayā girā ।। akṛtapratikarmaiva kṣipram ānīyatām iti ।। tyājitāḥ stha yayā sadyaś cetasaḥ sthiratām iti ।।
ayam eva jagatsāraḥ pramadā priyadarśanā ।। bhavataḥ katham ekasya pramadeti tad ucyate ।। adhunā bhavataḥ kāntā jātety atra kim ucyate ।। paramārthaṃ punar veda sahasraikaḥ pumān iti ।।
kriyate chagalaḥ śvāpi saṃhatya bahubhir balāt ।। aśraddheyaṃ na vaktavyaṃ pratyakṣam api yad bhavet ।। pramāṇaṃ hi pramāṇajñaiḥ purākalpe api vartitam ।। satyavratatayā loke prasiddhaḥ satyakauśikaḥ ।।
saśiṣyaparivāreṇa tarantī prekṣitā śilā ।। nāyam artho mahānarthaḥ prakāśyaḥ putrakair iti ।। vipaṇau mantrayāṃ cakre kasyacid vaṇijaḥ puraḥ ।। tarantīṃ dṛṣṭavān asmi sopādhyāyaḥ śilām iti ।।
etad ālāpam ākarṇya rājapatnyai nyavedayat ।। baṭunākhyātam āhvāyya pṛṣṭavān satyakauśikam ।। mithyā brūhīti no vācyaḥ kāmī mithyāvrato hi saḥ ।। pramadāt satyam apy ete vadanti baṭavo yataḥ ।।
kim etat satyam āho svin mṛṣety ākhyāyatām iti ।। duḥśraddhānam aniṣṭaṃ ca yan mayā vācyam īdṛśam ।। iti satyapravādo ayaṃ na tyājyaḥ satyavādibhiḥ ।। asatyam abhidhāsyāmi satyavādaśatādhikam ।।
agniṃ paśyati yaḥ śītaṃ plavamānāṃ śilām asau ।। capalasyopamānaṃ hi prathamaṃ baṭumarkaṭāḥ ।। viruddhavādinaṃ kruddhaḥ piṅgalaṃ niravāsayat ।। satyam satyapratijño api nāvadat satyakauśikaḥ ।।
viruddham idam īdṛk kaḥ śraddadhyād vadatām iti ।। yasyāsmin pramadāratne pumān iti viparyayaḥ ।। acirāt svīkariṣyāmi krośatāṃ tvādṛśām iti ।। vaidyarājaṃ samāhūya vaidyarājam upāgamat ।।
pradhārya cāparair vaidyaiḥ śanakair idam abravīt ।। tenāsmai rucitaṃ yat tad āśu saṃpādyatām iti ।। māṃ punarvasuhastena gomukhaḥ prāg abhojayat ।। triphalākvāthavaddveṣān mamāṅgāni vyadhūnayat ।।
saviṣādau karomi sma viṣādāv iva vairiṇau ।। lajjāmandapadanyāsaṃ namitānanam ānayat ।। grāsān agrāsayat ṣaḍ vā sapta vā gomukhājñayā ।। śailendrāḥ śuciśukrabhānudahanapluṣṭopalādhityakāmandair apy udabindubhir navatarair ujjhanti saṃtaptatām ।।
priyadarśanam āliṅgam anaṅgonmūlitatrapaḥ ।। pāṇāv ākṛṣya tvaritaḥ svagṛhān pratiyātavān ।। pāṇḍityāndhaka mitrāre mā sma tiṣṭhaḥ puro mama ।। yasya yas tasya kas tasmād arātir aparaḥ paraḥ ।।
rāhuṇeva tuṣārāṃśur agamad dhūmadhūmratām ।। pravṛddhair gamayāmi sma niṣādāsanacaṅkramaiḥ ।। priyadarśanasaṃprāpter upāyam agaveṣayam ।। vismitau ciram ālokya sthavirau mām avocatām ।।
bhavantam icchati draṣṭum iṣṭaṃ ced gamyatām iti ।। gomukhasya smarāmi sma vicāracaturaṃ manaḥ ।। vitarkya kṣaṇam āsīn me saṃdehacchedanī matiḥ ।। sa hi śṛṅkhalanistriṃśapāṇibhiḥ parivāryate ।।
rājñām ājñām avajñāya teṣāṃ jīvanti te katham ।। ākhyatīva priyāprāptiṃ mahyaṃ tad gamanaṃ hitam ।। kañcukyānītam adrākṣam ārukṣaṃ cāviśaṅkitaḥ ।। rājadvāraṃ vrajāmi sma citramaṅgalamaṇḍalam ।।
prāvikṣaṃ prathamāṃ kakṣāṃ dvāḥsthavṛndābhinanditaḥ ।। ko hi varṇayituṃ śakto naro meror adhityakām ।। saptamyāṃ dṛṣṭavān asmi mahāsthānaṃ mahīpateḥ ।। dhanurvedāditattvajñaiḥ kalādakṣaiś ca sevitam ।।
sukhasevyaṃ durīkṣaṃ ca taptāṃśum iva haimanam ।। adhyatiṣṭhaṃ nṛpādiṣṭaṃ nirvikārāmbarāvṛtam ।। tatas tārakarājākhyaṃ senābhṛtāram aikṣata ।। avocad vacanaṃ cāru vispaṣṭamadhurākṣaram ।।
rājā manmukhasaṃkrāntair vākyais tvām eṣa bhāṣate ।। sā kim ākhyāyate tubhyaṃ prathitā pṛthivīva yā ।। ye guṇās te api te buddhāḥ śiśirāṃśor ivāṃśavaḥ ।। saphalair draviṇair yasmād draviṇeśo api lajjitaḥ ।।
atha sā gṛhiṇī tasya kāle putraṃ vyajāyata ।। pure sāntaḥpure ramyaṃ mahāmaham akārayat ।। aṅgair vidyākalābhiś ca sakalābhir alaṃkṛtaḥ ।। dvāre vaḥ kāliyaḥ śreṣṭhī tiṣṭhatīti sasaṃbhramaiḥ ।।
kas tvaṃ kasya kuto veti pṛṣṭaś cedam abhāṣata ।। lālitaḥ pālitaś cāsaṃ śikṣitaś cākhilāḥ kalāḥ ।। cyāvayitvā divaṃ nīto na hi nāśo asti karmaṇām ।। jātāṃ putra iti khyātim anayal lobhadūṣitā ।।
bhāryayā hi kṛtaṃ karma patyāv api vipacyate ।। etam īdṛśam ākāraṃ vahāmi jananinditam ।। kasmaicid abhirūpāya varāya pratipādyatām ।। prayāge saṃnyasiṣyāmi prasthāpayata mām iti ।।
pūrvaṃ yad āvayor vṛttaṃ tat kiṃcit smaryatām iti ।। asaṃdigdhaṃ suviśrabdhas tat tat pṛṣṭatu mām iti ।। aśeṣaṃ tat tad etena saviśeṣaṃ niveditam ।। āhainaṃ dārikā kasmai jāmātre dīyatām iti ।।
rocate yo varas tasyai tasmai sā dīyatām iti ।। pṛṣṭā devīsamūhena hriyā kūrmāṅganākṛtiḥ ।। bhavatyai rocate neti mātar ākhyāyatām iti ।। puṇḍarīkam ivāvāte mantharaṃ calitaṃ śiraḥ ।।
svedārdrāṃśukayā prāgvan na tad vicalitaṃ śiraḥ ।। adyaiva śreṣṭhikanyāyāḥ pāṇim ālambatām iti ।। bhītāntaḥpuradṛṣṭena cirād idam udīritam ।। vedaśāstrāgamāyaiva na yoṣitprāptivāñchayā ।।
yogakṣemārthibhir bhavyais tasmād evaṃ bhavatv iti ।। pratidhvānadhvanadvyoma prādhvanat tūryamaṇḍalam ।। vivāhārthaḥ sa saṃbhāro rājñā saṃbhāritaḥ kṣaṇāt ।। rājājire mamodāraṃ karagraham akārayat ।।
samṛddhim anveṣya ca kāliyasya prāsthāpayan māṃ mudito narendraḥ ।। vardhamāno yathā rājā śreṣṭhī jāta iti sthitā ।। priyadarśanayā cāsmi saha kṣiptaśacīpatiḥ ।। mahāvyasanasaṃkīrṇa ivāsīn me mahotsavaḥ ।।
vidagdhasuhṛdāṃ kaścid api nāmānayed iti ।। adrākṣaṃ bhṛtyavargaṃ ca saṃcarantam itas tataḥ ।। balād ānāyayāmy enaṃ kiṃ duḥkhāsikayā mama ।। āsīnaḥ smayamānena sopālambham ivoditaḥ ।।
tasya sādhyāni kāryāṇi na sidhyantīti so abravīt ।। na tu tatkāraṇair yogyair vinā sidhyati kasyacit ।। tatrāpi gomukhasyaiva prājñaṃmanyasya kauśalam ।। bhṛtyān udvejayanty eva teṣāṃ kiṃ kriyatām iti ।।
ākhyātum ayam ārabdhaḥ śrūyatāṃ yan mayā kṛtam ।। tatra prāvṛtya mūrdhānaṃ patitvā śayano sthitaḥ ।। kim etad iti tasyaiva na mayā dattam uttaram ।। yuṣmadvṛttāntam akhilaṃ tadā kathitavān aham ।।
vatseśvarasutaḥ kaścid āryajyeṣṭho bhaved iti ।। āma subhrū sa evāyam iti tasyai nyavedayam ।। sāsūyā sapramodeva mām uktvākathayat kathām ।। divyajñānā marudvegā nāmnā ca priyadarśanā ।।
tvaṃ mām āpadi kaṣṭāyāṃ vartamānā smarer iti ।। śreṣṭhinyāḥ kanyakā jātā śokānalaghṛtāhutiḥ ।। sārasyāsyāsmadīyasya pālakaḥ ko bhaviṣyati ।। tataś cintitamātraiva dadṛśe priyadarśanā ।।
avocat sakhi mā bhaiṣīr janayitvedṛśīṃ sutām ।। priyā priyatamā tasmāj jṛmbhantāṃ tūryapaṅktayaḥ ।। kanyāyā hāṭakaṃ dṛṣṭvā kaṇṭhe gaṇḍakam abravīt ।। drakṣyanti puruṣaṃ muktvā bhaviṣyaccakravartinam ।।
paśyanti hi yathābhūtam arthaṃ divyena cakṣuṣā ।। cakravartī patiś cāsyāḥ sarvavidyādharādhipaḥ ।। idam eva ca nāmāsyāḥ praśastaṃ kriyatām iti ।। vidyādharendrayogyeyaṃ pramadā priyadarśanā ।।
ciraṃ sundari jīveti tenaiva viditaṃ mayā ।। yas tu paśyati sma vyaktaṃ cakravartīty abhūn mama ।। sarūpaḥ savayāś cānyo nāsti yac cakravartinaḥ ।। kauśāmbītaḥ paṭe nyastaṃ tac ca niścayakāraṇam ।।
cakravartīti vijñātaḥ paścimaṃ stanadarśanam ।। ghaṭane durghaṭasyāpi caturo hi bhavān iti ।। yasmān niścitavān asmi trayaṃ maraṇakāraṇam ।। atra jīvati yas tasya mṛta evāmṛtopamaḥ ।।
iti yaḥ svāminādiṣṭas tasya mṛtyum arhotsavaḥ ।। tasmān maraṇam evāstu dhik prāṇān duḥsthitān iti ।। kasyāpy adṛṣṭarūpasya vācam aśrauṣam ambare ।। na hi duḥkhakṣayopāyo mṛtyur iṣṭaḥ satām iti ।।
puraḥ puruṣam adrākṣaṃ skandhāropitadārakam ।। iti saṃtakṣitaḥ pitrā karkaśair vacanakṣuraiḥ ।। na vahāmi na puṣṇāmi bhavantaṃ niṣprayojanam ।। mārayiṣyāmi tad gaccha vaivasvatapurīm iti ।।
etāvatā hi te kāryaṃ na madīyena mṛtyunā ।। tad bhavān māṃ sahasreṇa vikrīnītāṃ mahātmasu ।। mā sma tasmād vinā kāryān mārayan māṃ bhavān iti ।। kutaś cānyan mahat kāryaṃ yuṣmajjīvitarakṣaṇāt ।।
tucchamūlyas tathāpy eṣa tṛṇamuṣṭisamā hi sā ।। krīṇāmi sma sahasreṇa cintāmaṇim ivāśmanā ।। pracchannaṃ śreṣṭhino vṛttaṃ tāvan me kathyatām iti ।। tat tat sumanase bhartrā kathitaṃ dhīracetase ।।
tayā tad ṛṣidattāyai duṣprakāśaṃ prakāśitam ।। kubjena brahmadattāya śeṣaṃ pratyakṣam eva ca ।। tad ācakṣveti kāryaṃ tad etad atra mayā kṛtam ।। prāśaṃsaṃ caritaṃ tasya praśasyā hi guṇādhikāḥ ।।
prajñādhikkṛtadevadānavagurur yeṣāṃ suhṛd gomukhaḥ te yat piṣṭapasaptakāptivimukhās tatkarmaṇāṃ jṛmbhitam ।। upātiṣṭhanta kāśikyāḥ śreṇayaḥ paṇyapāṇayaḥ ।। ayam āryakaniṣṭho vaḥ śreṇiśresṭhī bhavatv iti ।। sopāne tāram aśrauṣaṃ haṃsānām iva nisvanam ।।
padamantharasaṃcāro yac cāvicchinnasaṃtatiḥ ।। utsavābhyudayeṣv eva tā hi bibhrati bhūṣaṇam ।। kim artham api sopāne caraty ābharaṇadhvani ।। citrāṃśukadharā nārīr apaśyaṃ rūḍhayauvanāḥ ।।
pragalbhāpi vinīteva vanditvā mām abhāṣata ।। vijñāpayati vanditvā sādaraṃ rājadārikā ।। vaṇṭakas tasya yuṣmābhiḥ sadārair gṛhyatām iti ।। vāsaḥkusumagandhāṃś ca hārigandhān upāsarat ।।
dviprakārān alaṃkārān naranārījanocitān ।। preṣitaṃ yoṣitā yat tad yoṣid eva yato arhati ।। tasyai dattvā ca tad dravyam agacchan kṛtavandanāḥ ।। anabhyastaṃ hi yad yena tena tad vastu duḥsaham ।।
sarvo asāv āryaputreti muktvaitāṃ puruṣām iti ।। yeyam asmadvidhaiḥ sārdhaṃ lokayātrā niraṅkuśaiḥ ।। na dhanāyaty api svāṅgaṃ kim aṅga dhanam adhruvam ।। andhakāramukhenāhaṃ gomukhena iti bhāṣitaḥ ।।
lokayātrety athāvocam enaṃ parihasann iva ।। atha vā saṃkaṭāt trātā mamāsty eva bhavān iti ।। āgatyedam abhāṣanta savrīḍāvinayā iva ।। asmaddoṣe kṛtavrīḍā vijñāpayati sāñjaliḥ ।।
muḍhabhṛtyakṛtā doṣāna grāhyāḥ svāminām iti ।। asti cet kṣānta evāsau tathāpy ākhyāyatām iti ।। āryajyeṣṭhas tvayālāpān bhāṣitaḥ kīdṛśān iti ।। sāsūyā saviṣādeva vepamānedam abravīt ।।
yathokto mandayā jyeṣṭho yaśobhāginn iti tvayā ।। parasaṃdeśahārī hi pratīto gaṇikājanaḥ ।। priyadarśanayā sārdham abhinnaiva hi me tanuḥ ।। tathā vijñāpyatāṃ cedaṃ yathāvajñāṃ na manyate ।।
vratakotsavam āsevya sāyāhne pratiyāsyati ।। etasmād yad asāv āha bhāryā prasthāpyatām iti ।। kuṭumbijanayoṣeva gacchet paragṛhān iti ।। nedaṃ paragṛhaṃ devyās tathā viditam eva vaḥ ।।
tac caitac ca gṛhaṃ tasmād abhinnaṃ dṛśyatām iti ।। prāsādāgrād avārohat samaṃ tu priyadarśanā ।। gobhiḥ pravahaṇaṃ yuktam apaśyaṃ rājavartmani ।। nārīvarṣavaraprāyajanavṛndaiś ca saṃvṛtam ।।
tad dinaṃ gamayāmi sma dīrghabandhanadurgamam ।। daityocchinnaturaṃgo vā yenāstaṃ katham apy agāt ।। tad eva yānam adrākṣaṃ dīpikāvalayāvṛtam ।। sopāne dṛṣṭavān asmi śrāmyantīṃ priyadarśanām ।।
cirād āropayāmi sma harmyāgraśayanāntikam ।। tataś caḍ iti vicchinnaṃ tatkāñcīguṇabandhanam ।। śiñjānā raśanā śayyāṃ tan nitambād athāpatat ।। dṛṣṭvā pṛṣṭā mayā tasyāḥ saṃprāptiṃ priyadarśanā ।।
uktvā ruṣṭaiva tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sācaṣṭa sma kathām imām ।। na ca tatra mayā dṛṣṭā mārgayantyā nṛpātmajā ।। gṛhopavanam adhyāste tatra saṃbhāvyatām iti ।। vasantasumanaḥkḹptamālābharaṇadhāriṇī ।।
aśokaṣaṇḍas tatrāste vivikte rājadārikā ।। yo ayaṃ priyaṅguṣaṇḍasya yāti madhyena nirbhayaḥ ।। mādhavīsahakārānām aṅkolānāṃ ca varjaya ।। bhṛṅgadaṃśabhayāt kas taṃ nāpramattas tyajed iti ।।
mālatīsaptaparṇāś ca mañjarīcchannapallavān ।। anṛtāv api yenaite jṛmbhitāḥ pādapā iti ।। śilāpṛṣṭhe mayā dṛṣṭā sāndracandanakardame ।। madhyaṃdine jvareṇaiva khedyamānā balīyasā ।।
vījyamānā vacobhiś ca sāntvyamānātikomalaiḥ ।। tayāpi kṣiptacetastvān na kiṃcid api bhāṣitam ।। pratibuddhām avocat tāṃ bhaginī dṛśyatām iti ।। āliṅgitavatī svāṅgair dhvāntāṅgārāgniduḥsahaiḥ ।।
satataṃ kuśalītyādi tatheti ca mayoditam ।। āhārādyair durārādhas tvayā tad iti me matiḥ ।। tena naivopacaryo asau mayeti kathitaṃ mayā ।। rājyāṃśo daśamas tābhyām abhimānāt kilojjhitaḥ ।।
dāsam abhyupagacchetāṃ kathaṃ nāmeti durghaṭam ।। yad evādiśataḥ kiṃcit tat tathaiva hi sidhyati ।। tenāṅgīkṛtavantau tau madbhartur bhṛtyatām iti ।। tanūruhavikāreṇa sāśruṇāliṅgitā balāt ।।
aṅgaṃ pravahaṇakṣobhāt khinnam abhyañjyatām iti ।। tāvad balād balātailaṃ nyadhāt kumudikā mayi ।। sā me abhyaṅgāpadeśena vivṛtyāṅgāni paśyati ।। madīyam aṅgam ālokya rājadārikayoditam ।।
yayeha duḥsahā soḍhā komalāṅgyā kadarthanā ।। yena prabaladarpeṇa kṛtaṃ vaiṣamyam īdṛśam ।। dantineva mahāndhena mathitā puṇḍarīkiṇī ।। na hi cūḍāmaṇiḥ pāde prabhavāmīti badhyate ।।
chāyākomalagātryas tu na hi vānijadārikāḥ ।। satkārair annapānāntaiḥ saṃmānitavatī ciram ।। yuṣmatkathāprasaṅgena sārkaṃ gatam idaṃ dinam ।। āmucan mekhalām enāṃ mannitambe laghīyasi ।।
svahastavilatair yatnān mṛṇālītantusūtrakaiḥ ।। mekhalā skhalitā ceyaṃ chittvā tat tantubandhanam ।। saṃkalpajanmanāmṛṣṭaḥ saṃkalpayitum ārabhe ।। etad eva suparyāptam anurāgasya lakṣaṇam ।।
satsv apy anyeṣu sūtreṣu tatredaṃ cintitaṃ tayā ।। atheyaṃ mekhalā srastā śayyāyāṃ nipatiṣyati ।। anayā prītim ādhāsyaty api kām iti ।। mayā tu jñātakāryatvād utprekṣeyam upekṣitā ।।
kathaṃ vettheti sāpṛcchad athettham aham uktavān ।। śyāmānāṃ maṇḍanaṃ tajjñais citravarṇaṃ tu varṇitam ।। bālā dūrvādalaśyāmā niyataṃ rājadārikā ।। darśanīyatamā śyāmā nārīṇām iti darśanam ।।
janaḥ pracchādanīyo api khyāpito yaiḥ śaṭhair api ।। prāptyupāyavicāreṇa tṛtīyaḥ prerito mayā ।। devatās tat kariṣyanti yena śāntir bhaviṣyati ।। yathā tāḥ prāptavān asmi tathā rājasutām iti ।।
bhagīrathayaśā yuṣmān vanditvā yācate yathā ।। te jātā mañjarībhārabharabhaṅgurapallavāḥ ।। kartrī vivāhasaṃskāram apareṣāṃ ca pūjanam ।। prātar eva prāyātāsmi tad eṣā mucyatām iti ।।
draṣṭavyā rājaputrīti khidyamāno anayaṃ niśām ।। bhagīrathayaśāḥ prāptā gacchatv aryasuteti mām ।। prāsādāgrasthito dvāḥsthasvacchapravahaṇāsthitām ।। suṣuptāv asthitasyeva naṣṭasaṃkalpadarśane ।।
asāv akālamṛtyur yair nārīrūpo na vīkṣitaḥ ।। sahasrākṣaṃ svam ātmānaṃ taccakṣuṣkādikojjvalam ।। mayi dṛṣṭam adāt tasyāṃ gāḍha ṭhagrahārhaṇām ।। kañcukyādicamūguptā nagaropavanaṃ gatā ।।
harmyamūrdhānam ārohaṃ rājaputrīdidṛkṣayā ।। madgṛhadvāram āgacchad dūrād unnamitānanā ।। gāḍhaṃ niṣpīḍayantī ca ciram aṅgaṃ nyapīḍayat ।। cetovinimayaṃ kṛtvā pravṛttā śibikām iti ।।
ityādyupāyaśatacintanatāntacetāḥ kṛcchrān niśām anayam apratilabdhanidraḥ ।।
